# Introduction

> 引言

### 0.1 **What Is Organic Chemistry and Why Is It Important?**

> 0.1 有机化学是什么以及它为什么重要？

On a lovely Saturday afternoon in April, you are relaxing in a garden whilst enjoying a hot cup of coffee. Colourful spring blossoms lace the air with a pleasant aroma, and the green grass, warm sunshine and rich espresso make the afternoon a charming occasion.

> 四月的一个晴朗周六下午，你正坐在花园里，享受着一杯热咖啡。五彩缤纷的春日花朵散发着宜人的香气，绿草如茵、阳光温暖、浓郁的意式浓缩咖啡，使这个下午显得格外迷人。

Your mind begins to drift as you contemplate the combination of scents, colours and tastes that surround you in this moment, and how they make up the human experience's unique and fascinating complexities.

> 你的心思开始飘离，你沉思着此刻包围你的气味、色彩和味道的组合，以及它们如何构成了人类体验中独特而迷人的复杂性。

If you have ever wondered about the origins of nature's vibrant hues or the reasonings behind the alluring flavour of coffee, you would be able to find every answer within the elaborate spectrum of knowledge in the study of Organic Chemistry.

> 如果你曾经好奇自然界绚丽色彩的来源，或是咖啡诱人风味背后的原因，那么你将会在有机化学这门学科所涵盖的丰富知识体系中找到所有答案。

Organic chemistry is the chemistry of compounds containing the carbon element: the common element of all living organisms. **Anthocyanins** are the pigments that give flowers their various colours, **chlorophyll** is responsible for the green shades of grass is involved in the photosynthesis process of plants, and **caffeine** is what makes coffee function the way that it does. All these substances contain **carbon**, and they are all organic compounds.

> 有机化学是研究含有碳元素化合物的化学，碳元素是所有生物体的共同元素。花青素是使花朵呈现各种颜色的色素，叶绿素负责植物光合作用过程中草的绿色调，而咖啡因则是使咖啡发挥其功能的物质。所有这些物质都含有碳元素，它们都是有机化合物。

*Image of a Cyanidin, Pelargondin, Chlorophyll a, and Caffeine*

> 花青素、胭脂红、叶绿素a和咖啡因的图像

The root of the term *organic*dates back from over two hundred years ago, when its original meaning did not even involve the element of carbon. The word *organic* was first introduced in 1807 by Jöns Jakob Berzelius, a Swedish chemist, and was used to refer to compounds derived from living organisms. It was once believed that organic compounds could only be obtained directly from nature as they contained a mystical essence of life known as "vita force", therefore making it impossible to create organic compounds artificially. This theory was shattered by a famous experiment conducted by German chemist Friedrich Wohler in 1828. In his experiment, Wohler successfully synthesized the crystal urea by heating ammonia and cyanic acid together. The synthesis of urea marked a new era in the history of organic chemistry, not only redefining the term *organic*, but also rerouting organic chemistry into a completely new scientific discipline. The contemporary definition of *organic,* being carbon-containing compounds, is now the scientific way of describing the term. However, it has remained true over the years that organic compounds are essential to every known lifeform, as an abundance of organic molecules constitute all living organisms.

> “有机”一词的起源可以追溯到两百多年前，当时它的原始含义甚至并不包含碳元素。1807年，瑞典化学家约翰·雅各布·贝尔泽柳斯（Jöns Jakob Berzelius）首次引入了“有机”这个词，用来指代来源于生命体的化合物。过去人们曾认为有机化合物只能直接从自然界中获得，因为它们被认为含有某种神秘的生命本质，称为“生命力”（vita force），因此无法人工合成有机化合物。这一理论在1828年由德国化学家弗里德里希·沃勒（Friedrich Wöhler）进行的一项著名实验中被彻底打破。在实验中，沃勒通过加热氨和氰酸，成功合成了尿素晶体。尿素的合成标志着有机化学史上的一个新时代，不仅重新定义了“有机”一词，还将有机化学引向了一个全新的科学领域。如今，“有机”一词的定义为含有碳元素的化合物，这是对这一术语的科学描述方式。然而，多年来一直为真的是：有机化合物对于所有已知的生命形式都是必不可少的，因为大量有机分子构成了所有生命体。

There are two additional notes regarding the modern definition of *organic*. Firstly, while it is true that organic compounds are those containing the element carbon, it is important to know that not all compounds that contain carbon are organic compounds. For example, calcium carbonate (CaCO3), the primary component in certain rocks and chalk, can never be labelled as organic. Secondly, the "organic" food that is often found in supermarkets refers to the fact that the agricultural products were grown without the use of artificial pesticides, herbicides, or synthetic fertilizers, and has nothing to do with the presence of carbon in their chemical structures. This use of the word *organic* is possibly derived from the old definition, implying that the products came from nature, without human intervention.

> 关于有机化合物的现代定义，还有两个需要注意的要点。首先，虽然有机化合物确实是指含有碳元素的化合物，但需要明确的是，并非所有含碳的化合物都是有机化合物。例如，碳酸钙（CaCO₃）是某些岩石和粉笔的主要成分，但它永远不能被归类为有机化合物。其次，超市中常见的“有机”食品，指的是这些农产品在种植过程中未使用人工农药、除草剂或合成肥料，这与它们化学结构中是否含有碳无关。这种“有机”一词的使用可能源于旧的定义，意味着这些产品来源于自然，未经过人工干预。

As you may have been able to deduce, organic chemistry can be found in every corner of the world around us. From the food we eat, (the carbohydrates in bread, the protein in meat, the fructose in fruit, and more) to the fabric we wear, (cotton, nylon, polyester) and the fuels that power the technology around us (gasoline, natural gas, coal), the list of organic compounds involved in our lives is endless. An important significance in the application of organic chemistry is its critical role in the development of medicine and pharmaceuticals. The active ingredients found in medicine are most often organic compounds, either isolated from naturally occurring materials or synthesized in a lab. Just a few well-known examples include Aspirin, Tylenol, penicillin, insulin, Warfarin, and Tamiflu. The rapid developments of the pharmaceutical industry, in which organic chemistry has acted as a major driver, have saved millions of lives and has dramatically improved today's quality of life.

> 正如你可能已经能够推断出的那样，有机化学无处不在，存在于我们周围世界的每一个角落。从我们所吃的食物（如面包中的碳水化合物、肉类中的蛋白质、水果中的果糖等），到我们所穿的织物（如棉花、尼龙、聚酯纤维），以及驱动我们周围技术的燃料（如汽油、天然气、煤炭），与我们的生活息息相关的有机化合物种类繁多，不胜枚举。有机化学在应用中的一个重要意义在于其在医药和制药领域发展中的关键作用。药物中所含的活性成分大多是有机化合物，这些化合物要么是从天然材料中提取出来的，要么是在实验室中合成的。一些众所周知的例子包括阿司匹林、泰诺、青霉素、胰岛素、华法林和奥司他韦。制药工业的快速发展，其中有机化学起到了重要的推动作用，已经挽救了数百万人的生命，并极大地改善了当今的生活质量。

The magic element that is the key to organic chemistry and all living organisms is **carbon**. What is it about the carbon element that makes it so special? This can mainly be attributed to the special bonding ability that carbon possesses. Carbon atoms can form strong covalent bonds with other carbon atoms in the form of chains and rings, and it also forms strong bonds with other elements such as hydrogen, oxygen, nitrogen, sulfur and more. As a result, the structures of organic compounds are hugely diverse and can be rather complex.

> 有机化学以及所有生命体的关键元素是碳。碳元素为何如此特殊？这主要归功于碳所具有的特殊成键能力。碳原子能够通过链状和环状结构与其他碳原子形成牢固的共价键，同时也能与氢、氧、氮、硫等其他元素形成牢固的键。因此，有机化合物的结构种类繁多，结构也往往较为复杂。

#### 0.1.1 **Tips for Studying Organic Chemistry**

> 0.1.1 学习有机化学的建议

Learning organic chemistry can be both exciting and challenging. The most commonly misleading learning strategy is the notion that "I can be successful by simply memorizing everything". While memorization may be necessary at times, it is but a small fraction of what is needed to learning organic chemistry; the more important factor is your understanding. There are many structures, reactions and mechanisms involved in the course, and surface-level memorization will not carry you all the way through. However, if you know the connections between the structures, understand the underlying principles of the reactivity of certain compounds, and can tell the similarities and differences between different mechanisms, you will find that it becomes much easier. A few suggestions for learning include:

> 学习有机化学既令人兴奋，又充满挑战。最常见的误导性学习策略是认为“只要记住所有内容，我就能成功”。虽然在某些情况下记忆是必要的，但它只是学习有机化学所需知识的一小部分；更为重要的是你对知识的理解。课程中涉及大量的结构、反应和反应机理，仅靠表面的记忆无法让你顺利通过整个学习过程。然而，如果你了解结构之间的联系，理解某些化合物反应性的基本原理，并能够区分不同反应机理的异同，你会发现学习会变得容易得多。以下是一些学习建议：

- Rewrite your own notes when studying. For example, restate the concepts in your own words, or write a map of the concepts that are related.
- Practice makes perfect. Do as many practice questions as you can, and try to make your own questions to double check your understanding.
- Use molecule model sets for certain topics.

> 学习时要重新整理自己的笔记。例如，用你自己的话重述概念，或绘制相关概念之间的关系图。  
熟能生巧。尽可能多做练习题，并尝试自己出题来检验自己的理解。  
对于某些主题，使用分子模型套装进行学习。

### 0.2 **About the Book** 关于本书

Due to the high price barrier, about half of Organic Chemistry students at KPU do not have access to the textbook. This has become a serious issue that significantly affects the learning outcomes for the course. The creation of this open textbook is intended to provide a solution to this problem and help students get success in this course.

> 由于教材价格较高，约有一半的KPU有机化学课程学生无法获得教材。这已成为一个严重影响课程学习效果的严重问题。编写此开放教材旨在解决这一问题，帮助学生在本课程中取得成功。

The book contains ten chapters, with the contents cover from the basic concepts on chemical bonding, functional group, to stereochemistry, spectroscopy for structure determination (IR and NMR) and organic reactions (nucleophilic substitution, elimination, radical substitution of alkanes, addition and oxidation reactions of alkenes, preparation and reactions of alkynes).

> 本书共包含十章，内容涵盖从化学键基本概念、官能团，到立体化学，以及用于结构解析的光谱学（红外光谱和核磁共振谱），还有有机反应（亲核取代反应、消除反应、烷烃的自由基取代反应、烯烃的加成与氧化反应，以及炔烃的制备与反应）。

Organic Chemistry is a challenging subject for lots students. To help readers understand the concepts more easily, simple and concise languages are intentionally applied in the book. The featured shaded textbox areas are included frequently in the book, where readers can find useful learning tips, reminder of common errors, comparison between similar concepts. To help readers develop the problem-solving skills, a small section labelled as "strategy" is usually given for the examples in the book. Readers are encouraged to try solving the problems by themselves with helpful hints provided in the "strategy", and then compare their work with the detailed solutions provided afterwards.

> 有机化学对于许多学生来说是一个具有挑战性的学科。为了帮助读者更轻松地理解相关概念，本书有意采用了简单、简洁的语言。书中频繁地设置了带有阴影的文本框区域，读者可以在其中找到有用的学**习提示**、常见错误的提醒以及相似概念之间的对比。为了帮助读者培养解决问题的能力，书中通常会在例题旁设置一个标记为“策略”的小节。鼓励读者在“策略”中提供的提示帮助下，尝试自己解决这些问题，然后将他们的解答与随后提供的详细解答进行比较。

## 1 CHAPTER 1 BASIC CONCEPTS IN CHEMICAL BONDING AND ORGANIC MOLECULES

> 第1章 化学键与有机分子的基本概念

Before beginning our Organic Chemistry journey, a review of some basic knowledge from the General Chemistry course will be very helpful and important. We will start with chemical bonding and review how to draw Lewis Structure to show and predict the bonding in a chemical species, followed by Valence Bond Theory and Hybridization to explain how the bonds are formed.

> 在我们开始有机化学的学习之前，复习一些普通化学课程中的基础知识将非常有帮助且重要。我们将首先从化学键开始，复习如何绘制路易斯结构式，以展示和预测化学物种中的成键情况，接着学习价键理论和杂化理论，以解释化学键的形成过程。

# 1.1 Chemical Bonding

> 1.1 化学键

To summarize simply, a chemical bond is the attractive force holding atoms or ions together. Such attractive interaction leads to a more stable state for the whole system comparing to individual atoms.

> 简而言之，化学键是使原子或离子相互结合的吸引力。这种吸引力使得整个体系比单独的原子处于更加稳定的状态。

**Valence electrons** play a fundamental role in chemical bonding. In the electron configuration of an atom, the outermost shell is called the valence shell, and the *electrons in the valence shell (outermost shell)* are known as **valence electrons**. Take the carbon atom for example: the electron configuration of carbon is 1s<sup>2</sup> 2s<sup>2</sup> 2p<sup>2</sup> . The outermost shell is the 2nd principal shell, so there are 4 valence electrons in carbon. Valence electrons are the electrons that are the furthest away from the nucleus, and thus experience the least attraction from the nucleus and therefore are most reactive. They play the most important role in chemical bonding.

> 价电子在化学键形成中起着基础性作用。在原子的电子排布中，最外层的电子壳层称为价壳层，而位于价壳层中的电子则称为价电子。以碳原子为例：碳原子的电子排布为 1s² 2s² 2p²。最外层是第二主壳层，因此碳原子有 4 个价电子。价电子是距离原子核最远的电子，因此受到原子核的吸引力最小，因而最活泼。它们在化学键形成中起着最重要的作用。

#### 0.1.1 *Exercises 1.1*

> 0.1.1 习题 1.1

Determine the number of valence electrons for following elements: B, N, O, Cl, Mg.

> 确定下列元素的价电子数目：B、N、O、Cl、Mg。

Answers to Practice Questions Chapter 1

> 练习题答案 第1章

#### 0.1.2 **Ionic Bond and Covalent Bond**

> 0.1.2 离子键与共价键

There are two major types of chemical bonding: **ionic bonds** and **covalent bonds**. An ionic bond is a bond that results from the electrostatic attraction (force) between ions of opposite charges. Ionic bonds apply to ionic compound, such as sodium chloride (NaCl).

> 化学键主要有两种类型：离子键和共价键。离子键是由带相反电荷的离子之间的静电吸引力（力）形成的。离子键存在于离子化合物中，例如氯化钠（NaCl）。

In simple ionic compounds, the metal element loses valence electron(s) to form the cation and the non-metal element gains electron(s) to form the anion. With the proper number of electron(s) lost or gained, both the cation and the anion achieve a full outer shell that contains eight electrons, as in the following examples of Na + , Ca<sup>2</sup> , Cl– and O2– . According to Lewis's Theory, *an atom is most stable if its outer shell is filled or contains eight electrons*. This is also called the **octet rule**.

> 在简单的离子化合物中，金属元素失去最外层电子形成阳离子，而非金属元素获得电子形成阴离子。当金属元素失去或非金属元素获得适当数量的电子后，阳离子和阴离子的最外层都达到八个电子的稳定结构，如 Na⁺、Ca²⁺、Cl⁻ 和 O²⁻ 所示。根据路易斯理论，一个原子如果其最外层电子数达到八个（即填满外层电子壳层），则最为稳定。这一规则也被称为八电子规则。

Na (atom) 
$$\rightarrow$$
 Na<sup>+</sup> + e<sup>-</sup> Ca (atom)  $\rightarrow$  Ca<sup>2+</sup> + 2e<sup>-</sup> Cl (atom) + e<sup>-</sup>  $\rightarrow$  Cl<sup>-</sup> O (atom) + 2e<sup>-</sup>  $\rightarrow$  O<sup>2-</sup>

> Na（原子）  
Na<sup>+</sup> + e<sup>-</sup> Ca（原子）    Ca<sup>2+</sup> + 2e<sup>-</sup> Cl（原子） + e<sup>-</sup>    Cl<sup>-</sup> O（原子） + 2e<sup>-</sup>    O<sup>2-</sup>

A covalent bond is a bond formed through the sharing of electron pairs between the two bonding atoms. The shared electron pairs are mutually attracted by the nuclei of both atoms. By sharing the electron pairs, both atoms also gain a filled outer shell, or an **octet**. Almost all of the bonds involved in organic compounds are covalent bonds.

> 共价键是两个成键原子之间通过共用电子对而形成的化学键。共用的电子对同时受到两个原子核的吸引。通过共用电子对，两个原子都能获得一个充满的最外层电子壳层，即八个电子的稳定结构。有机化合物中几乎所有的化学键都是共价键。

Covalent bond can be non-polar or polar.

> 共价键可以是非极性的或极性的。

For covalent bonds formed between two identical atoms, the electron pairs are shared equally between the two nuclei. Electron density is distributed evenly through the bond, making the bond a non-polar bond. Examples include all homonuclear molecules, such as H-H, Cl-Cl, O=O, N≡N.

> 当两个相同原子之间形成共价键时，电子对在两个原子核之间均等地共享。电子密度在键中均匀分布，使该键成为非极性键。例如，所有同核分子，如 H-H、Cl-Cl、O=O、N≡N 等。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_15_Picture_0.jpeg)

![](_page_15_Figure_1.jpeg)

*Figure 1.1a nonpolar covalent bond and polar covalent bond*

> 图1.1（a）非极性共价键与极性共价键

For heteronuclear bonds (the bond formed between two different atoms), the electron pairs are not shared evenly, and the bond is polar. The electron pairs are *more* attracted to the atom that has the *stronger ability* to pull the electron pairs towards itself. This ability is measured with **electronegativity**. The relative values of electronegativity (EN) are listed using the scale devised by Linus Pauling, as summarized in the following table:

> 对于异核键（由两种不同原子形成的化学键），电子对的共享并不均匀，因此该键具有极性。电子对更倾向于被那些对电子对具有更强吸引力的原子所吸引。这种能力通过电负性来衡量。电负性的相对值是使用林纳斯·鲍林（Linus Pauling）设计的标度来表示的，如下表所示：

![](_page_15_Figure_6.jpeg)

*Figure 1.1b Electronegativity Values in Pauling Scale*

> 图1.1b 津林电负性标度值

#### 0.1.3 **Notes about electronegativity values for Organic Chemistry purposes:**

> 0.1.3 关于有机化学中电负性值的说明：

- It is much more important to know the trend of electronegativity than to memorize the values. The trend is that EN values decrease along the group from top to bottom and increase along the period from left to right (the trend mainly works for Main Group elements, not transition metal elements).
- It is very useful (although not mandatory) to know the EN values of a few select elements: F (4.0, highest), O (3.5), N (3.0), C (2.5) and H (2.1).
- The EN of C (2.5) and H (2.1) is rather close, which makes the C-H bond (the bond involved in all organic compounds) technically non-polar.

> 了解电负性的变化趋势比单纯记忆数值更为重要。电负性变化的趋势是：在同一主族中，从上到下电负性逐渐减小；在同一周期中，从左到右电负性逐渐增大（这一趋势主要适用于主族元素，不适用于过渡金属元素）。

了解一些元素的电负性数值（虽然不是必须的，但非常有用）会很有帮助：F（4.0，最高）、O（3.5）、N（3.0）、C（2.5）和H（2.1）。

碳（2.5）和氢（2.1）的电负性非常接近，因此碳-氢键（所有有机化合物中都存在的键）在技术上被认为是而非极性的。

With the introduction to the concept of electronegativity, bond polarity can be represented with the

> 在引入电负性概念之后，键的极性可以用以下方式表示：

electronegativity difference between the two bonding atoms, which is known as ΔEN. For non-polar bonds, ΔEN equals to zero, and for polar bonds, ΔEN is not zero. The greater the ΔEN, the more polar the bond is.

> 两个成键原子之间的电负性差异称为ΔEN。对于非极性键，ΔEN等于零；而对于极性键，ΔEN不为零。ΔEN越大，键的极性越强。

#### 0.1.4 *Exercises 1.2*

> 0.1.4 习题 1.2

- 1. Identify the following bonds as "polar" or "non-polar": C-C, C-H, B-F, O-O, C=N
- 2. Rank the following bonds in order of increasing bonding polarity: C—S, C—O, C—F (referring to the trend of EN, you do not need to use the exact EN values).

> 判断下列化学键是“极性”还是“非极性”：C—C，C—H，B—F，O—O，C=N  
按键的极性由小到大排列下列化学键：C—S，C—O，C—F（只需根据电负性（EN）的变化趋势进行排序，不需要使用具体的EN值）。

#### 0.1.5 Answers to Practice Questions Chapter 1

> 0.1.5 习题答案 第1章

Because of the electronegativity difference, the atom with the higher EN attracts the shared electron pairs more strongly, therefore bearing a slightly negative charge (δ-). The other atom with a lower EN bears a slightly positive charge (δ+). The direction of the bond polarity can be indicated with an arrow, with the head of the arrow pointing to the negative end and a short perpendicular line near the tail of the arrow marking the positive end. The following example of an H-Cl molecule indicates how to show the bond polarity and partial charges of the polar bond.

> 由于电负性差异，电负性较高的原子对共用电子对的吸引力更强，因此带有一个微弱的负电荷（δ-）。而电负性较低的原子则带有一个微弱的正电荷（δ+）。共价键的极性方向可以用箭头表示，箭头的头部指向带负电的一端，箭头尾部附近画一条短的垂直线以表示带正电的一端。以下以H-Cl分子为例，说明如何表示极性键的极性和部分电荷。

![](_page_16_Picture_6.jpeg)

# 1.2 Lewis Structure

> 1.2 路易斯结构

The Lewis structure is a structure that shows the bonding between atoms as short lines (some books use pairs of dots), and non-bonding valence electrons as dots.

> 路易斯结构是一种展示原子之间共价键的结构，用短线表示（有些书籍用点对表示），非键合的价电子则用点表示。

#### 0.1.1 **1.2.1 Lewis Structure of Diatomic Molecules**

> 0.1.1 1.2.1 双原子分子的路易斯结构

To learn about Lewis structures, we will start with the Lewis symbol. The Lewis symbol is the chemical symbol of an element with valence electrons represented as dots. The Lewis symbols of some elements are shown here:

> 为了学习路易斯结构（Lewis structures），我们将首先了解路易斯符号（Lewis symbol）。路易斯符号是元素的化学符号，其价电子用点表示。一些元素的路易斯符号如下所示：

*Figure 1.2a The Lewis structures of aluminum, tin, nitrogen, chlorine and bromine*

> 图1.2a 铝、锡、氮、氯和溴的路易斯结构

For simple **diatomic molecules**, combining the Lewis symbols of each element gives its Lewis structure.

> 对于简单的双原子分子，将各元素的路易斯符号组合起来即可得到该分子的路易斯结构。

**H2 example**: (H only needs two electrons; usually referred to as a **duet.**)

> H₂ 示例：（H 只需要两个电子；通常被称为双电子对。）

*Figure 1.2b The Lewis structure of Hydrogen*

> 图1.2b 氢的路易斯结构

#### 0.1.2 **F2 example:**

> 0.1.2 F2 示例：

![](_page_17_Figure_11.jpeg)

*Figure 1.2c The Lewis structure of the Florine molecule*

> 图1.2c 氟分子的路易斯结构

Terms used in Lewis structures (see example of F2):

> 路易斯结构中使用的术语（见 F₂ 示例）：

- **Bonding pair:** The pair of valence electrons involved in a covalent bond. The covalent bonds are drawn as short lines in this book, and one covalent bond means one pair of bonding electrons, that is 2 electrons. Single bonds and multiple bonds (double or triple bonds) may be involved.
- **Lone pair**: The pairs of valence electrons **not** involved in the covalent bond. Lone pair electrons can also be called non-bonding electron pairs.

> 成键电子对：参与共价键的价电子对。本书中，共价键用短横线表示，一条共价键表示一对成键电子，即2个电子。单键和多重键（双键或三键）都可能涉及。

孤电子对：不参与共价键的价电子对。孤电子对也被称为非成键电子对。

Special note: Non-bonding electrons can also be unpaired (single) electrons. A species with one or more unpaired (single) electrons is called a radical (free radical). More examples of radicals with single electrons will be in **section 1.2.5** and **Chapter 9**.

> 特别说明：非键合电子也可以是不成对（单个）电子。具有一个或多个不成对（单个）电子的物种称为自由基（自由基）。更多关于具有单个电子的自由基的例子将在第1.2.5节和第9章中介绍。

#### 0.1.3 **HCl example:**

> 0.1.3 盐酸示例：

$$H^{\bullet} + {\bullet} \overset{\bullet}{C} : \longrightarrow H - \overset{\bullet}{C} :$$
 (single bond)

> （单键）

*Figure 1.2d The Lewis structure of covalent bond between hydrogen and chlorine*

> 图1.2d 氢与氯之间共价键的路易斯结构

### 0.2 **O2 example:**

> 0.2 O₂ 示例：

$$\cdot \ddot{O} \cdot + \cdot \ddot{O} \cdot \longrightarrow \ddot{O} = \ddot{O}$$
 (double bond)

> （双键）

*Figure 1.2e The Lewis structure of a covalent bond between two oxygen atoms*

> 图1.2e 两个氧原子之间的共价键的路易斯结构

Draw the Lewis structure of the N2 molecule.

Answers to Practice Questions Chapter 1

> 练习题答案 第1章

### 0.3 **1.2.2 Lewis Structures of Polyatomic Molecules or Ions**

> 0.3 1.2.2 多原子分子或离子的路易斯结构

For more complicated **polyatomic molecules and ions**, the Lewis structures cannot be obtained by simply combing Lewis symbols. A specific procedure with certain steps have to be followed. It is very important that you follow the following **procedure** in order to get the correct Lewis structures for polyatomic molecules and ions.

> 对于更复杂的多原子分子和离子，仅通过组合莱纳斯·鲍林（Linus Pauling）提出的莱韦斯符号（Lewis符号）无法得到正确的莱韦斯结构（Lewis结构）。必须遵循一个特定的步骤程序。为了获得多原子分子和离子的正确莱韦斯结构，遵循以下程序非常重要。

*Lewis Structure Drawing Procedure for Polyatomic Molecules and Ions*

> 多原子分子和离子的路易斯结构绘制步骤

1. Calculate the total number of valence electrons. For ions, make sure charges are properly included in the calculation. For example of NH4 + cation:

> 计算总共有多少个价电子。对于离子，要确保在计算中正确包含电荷。例如，NH₄⁺ 离子：

the total number of electrons = 5 (N atom) + 4×1 (four H atoms) -1 (minus the charge for cation) = 8 valence electrons

> 电子总数 = 5（N原子） + 4×1（四个H原子） -1（减去阳离子的电荷） = 8个价电子

- 2. Write a plausible skeletal structure using the following steps:
- a) Write atomic symbols for the central and terminal atoms.
- Hydrogen atoms are always terminal
- Central atoms are generally those with the lowest electronegativity
- Carbon atoms are always central
- b) Connect the central atom with each of the terminal atom by drawing a single bond.
  - 3. For each single bond, subtract two electrons from the total number of valence electrons.
- 4. Using the remaining valence electrons, complete the octets of the terminal atoms first, and then complete as many as possible for the central atoms.
  - 5. If you have used up all of the valence electrons to complete octets for all of the atoms, you are done.
- 6. If not, then complete the octets of all central atoms by moving lone-pairs from terminal atoms to form multiple bonds.
  - 7. Calculate the Formal Charges on all atoms and label the non-zero formal charges in the structure:

> 按照以下步骤写出一个合理的骨架结构：

a) 写出中心原子和终端原子的原子符号。  
氢原子总是作为终端原子  
中心原子通常是电负性最低的原子  
碳原子总是作为中心原子  

b) 用单键将中心原子与每个终端原子连接起来。  
对于每个单键，从总价电子数中减去两个电子。  
使用剩余的价电子，首先完成终端原子的八隅体，然后再尽可能完成中心原子的八隅体。  
如果你已经用完了所有价电子来完成所有原子的八隅体，那么你就完成了。  
如果还有剩余的价电子，则通过将终端原子的孤对电子转移到中心原子上形成多重键，以完成所有中心原子的八隅体。  
计算所有原子的形式电荷，并在结构中标出非零的形式电荷。

**Formal Charge on an atom =** No. of valence electrons in free atom–No. of lone pair electrons –½ (No. of bonding electrons)

> 原子的正式电荷 = 自由原子的价电子数 – 键合电子数的一半 – 单电子对数

*Formula 1.1*

> 公式 1.1

*Examples: Here we will take CO*2 *molecule as an example to explain the procedure step by step:*

> 示例：下面我们以 CO₂ 分子为例，逐步说明该过程：

1. Total number of valence electrons: 4 (C atom) + 2×6 (2 O atoms) = 16

> 价电子总数：4（碳原子） + 2×6（2个氧原子） = 16

Always DOUBLE CHECK: In the correct Lewis structure, the total number of electrons involved (bonding plus non-bonding electrons) must be **equal** to this number, less or more are both incorrect!!

> 务必双重检查：在正确的路易斯结构中，所涉及的总电子数（包括成键电子和孤对电子）必须等于该数值，多于或少于都是错误的！！

2. Write a plausible skeletal structure:

> 写出一个合理的骨架结构：

Carbon atoms are always central, so the skeletal structure is: O — C — O

> 碳原子总是处于中心位置，因此骨架结构为：O — C — O

- 3. Four electrons are used so far, and there are 16 4 = 12 electrons remained.
- 4. The remaining 12 electrons must be used to complete the octet for both terminal O atoms first, and no electrons left after that.

> 到目前为止，已经使用了4个电子，还剩下16 - 4 = 12个电子。  
剩下的12个电子必须首先用于完成两个终端氧原子的八隅体，之后不能再有电子剩余。

![](_page_19_Picture_22.jpeg)

It is very important to keep in mind that the remaining electrons should be used to give the octet of **terminal atoms first**!

> 必须牢记的是，剩余的电子应首先用于给终端原子提供八电子结构！

- 5. The central C atom does not get octet yet, we should do next step.
- 6. Moving one lone pair from each terminal O atom, the following structure is obtained.

> 中心碳原子尚未满足八隅体，我们应进行下一步操作。  
将每个终端氧原子上的一个孤对电子移动，得到如下结构。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_20_Picture_0.jpeg)

this is the complete Lewis structure of CO2.

> 这是CO₂的完整路易斯结构。

For Lewis structure purposes, the lone-pairs can only be moved f**rom terminal atoms to the central** atom to form multiple bonds, **not** the other way around.

> 在绘制路易斯结构时，孤对电子只能从终端原子转移到中心原子以形成多重键，而不能反过来。

7. Formal charges check: all atoms have formal charges equals to 0 in this structure.

> 形式电荷检查：在此结构中，所有原子的形式电荷均为 0。

$$FC(C) = 4 - \frac{1}{2} \times (4 \times 2) = 0$$

> 

FC (O) = 
$$6 - 4 - \frac{1}{2} \times (2 \times 2) = 0$$

> FC (O) =

Since the two oxygen atoms have the same bonding, one calculation is enough for both oxygen atoms.

> 由于两个氧原子具有相同的成键方式，因此只需进行一次计算即可适用于两个氧原子。

### 0.4 **1.2.3 Guidelines about Formal Charges in Lewis Structures**

> 0.4 1.2.3 路易斯结构中形式电荷的指导原则

The purpose of formal charges is to compare the *difference* between the number of valence electrons in the free atom and the number of electrons the atom "owns" when it is bonded. The smaller the difference the "happier" (more stable) the atom is. The atom owns *all* of the lone pair (non-bonding) electrons and *half* of the bonding (shared) electrons, which is why the formula is in the way given in *Formula 1.1.*

> 形式电荷的作用是将自由原子的价电子数目与该原子在成键时所拥有的电子数目进行比较。原子所拥有的电子数目与自由原子的价电子数目之间的差异越小，该原子就越“幸福”（即越稳定）。原子拥有所有的孤对电子（非键合电子）以及一半的成键电子（共享电子），这就是公式1.1中给出公式的原因。

Formal charges can be used as guidelines to determine the plausibility of Lewis structures by comparing the stability of non-equivalent resonance structures, which is particularly important for organic species. The rules about formal charges are:

> 形式电荷可用于通过比较非等价共振结构的稳定性来判断路易斯结构的合理性，这对于有机物种尤为重要。关于形式电荷的规则如下：

- The sum of the formal charges must equal to the total charge on the molecule or ion.
- Formal charges should be as small as possible (comparing the absolute value of formal charges for such purposes).
- "-" FC usually appears on the most electronegative atoms (with the stronger ability to pull the shared electrons; this atom is "winning" electrons in the sharing).
- "+" FC usually appears on least electronegative atoms (with the weaker ability to pull the shared electrons; this atom is "losing" electrons in the sharing).
- Structures having formal charges of the same sign on adjacent atoms are unlikely.

> 形式电荷的总和必须等于分子或离子的总电荷。  
形式电荷应尽可能小（在比较形式电荷的绝对值时）。  
“-”形式电荷通常出现在最电负性的原子上（该原子具有更强的拉扯共用电子的能力；该原子在共用中“赢得”电子）。  
“+”形式电荷通常出现在电负性最弱的原子上（该原子拉扯共用电子的能力较弱；该原子在共用中“失去”电子）。  
相邻原子上具有相同符号的形式电荷的结构是不太可能的。

There is a *derived way* for calculating formal charge: since each bond contains 2 electrons, half of the bonding electrons simply equals to the number of bonds. So, the formal charge can also be calculated based on the derived version of the formula:

> 计算形式电荷的一种衍生方法是：由于每个共价键包含2个电子，因此每个键中的电子数的一半就等于键的数量。因此，形式电荷也可以根据该公式的衍生版本进行计算：

**Formal Charge on an atom =** No. of valence electrons in free atom–No. of lone pair electrons – No. of covalent bonds around the atom *Formula 1.2*

> 原子的正式电荷 = 自由原子的价电子数 – 孤对电子数 – 原子周围的共价键数目 公式 1.2

Double bonds count as 2 and triple bond count as 3 in *Formula 1.2*. Both *Formula 1.1* and *1.2* work for counting the formal charge; you can choose either one for your convenience. While almost all of the other textbooks show *Formula 1.1* as the official way, *Formula 1.2* is easier to use and can be regarded as the practical one based on experience.

> 在公式1.2中，双键计为2，三键计为3。公式1.1和公式1.2都可以用于计算形式电荷，你可以根据自己的方便选择使用其中任何一个。虽然大多数其他教材都将公式1.1作为标准方法，但根据经验，公式1.2更为简便，可以视为一种实用的方法。

Why is the following structure not the best way to show the Lewis structure of CO2 ?

> 为什么以下结构不是展示CO₂分子最合适的路易斯结构呢？

Answers to Practice Questions Chapter 1

> 练习题参考答案 第1章

### 0.5 **1.2.4 Kekulé Structures** *vs* **Lewis Structures**

> 0.5 1.2.4 凯库勒结构与路易斯结构

The complete Lewis structure always has to include all the *bonding* electrons and *lone pair* electrons. However, organic species are usually shown as KeKulé structures (more discussion will be in **Chapter 2**) with *all the lone pair electrons completely omitted* (with exceptions to the lone pairs that are shown to highlight special properties). Therefore, when viewing Kekulé structures, it is very helpful to keep in mind that atoms other than C and H should have a certain number of lone pairs. Examples of Kekulé structures of some compounds are given here:

> 完整的路易斯结构必须包括所有的成键电子和孤对电子。然而，有机物种通常以凯库勒结构（关于凯库勒结构的更多讨论将在第2章中进行）的形式表示，其中所有的孤对电子都被完全省略（例外情况是那些为了突出某些特殊性质而特意显示的孤对电子）。因此，在查看凯库勒结构时，应牢记除碳和氢以外的原子应具有一定数量的孤对电子。以下是一些化合物的凯库勒结构示例：

![](_page_21_Figure_6.jpeg)

*Figure 1.2f The Kekulé structures of ethanol, acetic acid, ethyl amine, and ethyl bromide*

> 图1.2f 乙醇、乙酸、乙胺和溴乙烷的凯库勒结构

To count how many lone pairs should be involved on a certain atom, apply the octet rule. All of the atoms (except H) should have 8 electrons around it, therefore, N usually has 1 lone pair, O has 2 lone pairs and halogens have 3 lone pairs.

> 要计算某个原子上应涉及多少个孤对电子，可以应用八隅体规则。除氢原子外，所有原子周围应有8个电子。因此，氮原子通常具有1个孤对电子，氧原子具有2个孤对电子，卤素原子具有3个孤对电子。

#### 0.5.1 **1.2.5 Exceptions to Octet Rule in Lewis Structure**

> 0.5.1 1.2.5 洛斯结构中八隅规则的例外情况

So far we have always been applying the **octet rule** in Lewis structures, however there are some cases in which the rule does not apply. For example, H only needs 2 electrons. Here we will see some other cases where the octet rule is compromised.

> 到目前为止，我们在绘制路易斯结构时一直应用的是八隅体规则，然而也有一些情况该规则并不适用。例如，氢原子只需要2个电子。在这里，我们将看到一些八隅体规则被打破的其他情况。

#### 0.5.2 • **Odd number of electrons**

> 0.5.2 • 奇数电子

If the total number of valence electron is an odd number, the octet rule can not be applied to all atom in the species. The examples could include NO (nitrogen monoxide *or* nitric oxide), NO2 (nitrogen dioxide) and alkyl radicals.??

> 如果该物质中价电子总数为奇数，则无法对其中所有原子都应用八电子规则。例如包括NO（一氧化氮）、NO₂（二氧化氮）以及烷基自由基等。

**NO molecule**: Although NO is a diatomic molecule, it is possible to draw the Lewis structure by following the *procedure*. Depending on which atom is given the octet first in Step 4, you may get two possible structures. By applying the formal charge guideline, we can decide that the first structure is the better choice with zero formal charges.

> 一氧化氮分子（NO）：尽管NO是一个双原子分子，但按照上述步骤仍可以绘制其路易斯结构。在第4步中，根据先给哪个原子满足八电子结构，可能会得到两种可能的结构。通过应用形式电荷规则，我们可以判断第一种结构是更优的选择，因为它具有零形式电荷。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_22_Picture_2.jpeg)

*Figure 1.2g NO molecule Lewis structure*

> 图1.2g 一氧化氮分子的路易斯结构

**NO2 molecule**: The Lewis structure of NO2 molecule is shown below.

> NO₂分子：NO₂分子的路易斯结构如下所示。

*Figure 1.2h NO2 molecule Lewis structure*

> 图1.2h NO₂分子的路易斯结构

For above molecules, they all contain unpaired (single) electrons. The neutral species that contain an unpaired electron is called **radical** (or free radical). When the carbon atom of a alkyl group has an unpaired electron, the species is the alkyl radical.

> 上述分子中，它们都含有不成对（单个）电子。含有不成对电子的中性物种称为自由基（或自由基）。当烷基中的碳原子具有不成对电子时，该物种称为烷基自由基。

**Alkyl radicals:** The simplest example of alkyl radical is •CH3, with the total number of valence electron as 7. The structure is:

> 烷基自由基：烷基自由基的最简单例子是•CH₃，其价电子总数为7。其结构为：

*Figure 1.2i CH3 Lewis structure*

> 图1.2i 甲基的路易斯结构

More discussions about the properties and reactions of radicals will be included in Chapter 9.

> 关于自由基的性质和反应的更多讨论将在第9章中进行。

#### 0.5.3 • **Incomplete Octet**

> 0.5.3 • 不完整的八隅体

An incomplete octet means that the atom has less than 8 electrons involved. This could be because the total number of valence electrons is less than 8, or due to formal charge concerns.

> 不完整的八电子结构意味着该原子参与成键的电子数少于8个。这可能是由于价电子总数不足8个，或者是由于形式电荷的考虑。

**BH3 molecule**: The total number of valence electrons is 6, so the central boron atom does not get an octet.

> BH3分子：价电子总数为6，因此中心硼原子无法形成八电子结构。

![](_page_23_Figure_0.jpeg)

*structure*

> 结构

**BF3 molecule**: Even though all of the atoms do have a chance to get octets in the structure of BF3, the actual structure of BF3 keeps the incomplete octet. Applying the FC guideline explains why the first structure is the better choice. Similar examples include BeF2, AlCl3.

> BF3分子：尽管在BF3的结构中，所有原子都有机会形成八电子结构，但BF3的实际结构仍保持不完整的八电子结构。应用形式电荷（FC）规则可以解释为什么第一种结构是更优的选择。类似的例子还有BeF2、AlCl3。

![](_page_23_Figure_2.jpeg)

*Figure 1.2k BF3 molecule Lewis structure*

> 图1.2k BF3分子的路易斯结构

F is the atom with the highest electronegativity, therefore F **never** has "+" formal charge in any plausible Lewis structure!

> F 是电负性最高的原子，因此在任何合理的路易斯结构中，F 原子永远不会带有“+”形式电荷！

**CH3 +** : This is another reactive intermediate in organic reactions (more discussions in Chapter 8). FC calculations indicate that the "+" charge lies on the C atom, so such a species is also called a *carbocation*. Carbon has an incomplete octet.

> CH₃⁺ ：这是有机反应中另一种活性中间体（更多讨论请参见第8章）。从分子轨道计算可知，正电荷位于碳原子上，因此这种物种也被称为碳正离子。碳原子的外层电子未达到八电子稳定结构。

*Figure 1.2l CH3+ molecule Lewis structure*

> 图1.2l CH₃⁺分子的路易斯结构

#### 0.5.4 • **Expanded Valence Shell**

> 0.5.4 • 扩展价层

For elements in Period 3 or higher, they can have more than 8 electrons if that helps to lower the formal charges. Common examples involve the species with P, S or Cl, etc as central atoms. Sometimes multiple double bonds are necessary to minimize the formal charge of the central atom. The structure of the phosphate anion, PO4 3-, is given here as an example.

> 周期表中第三周期及更高周期的元素，如果这样有助于降低形式电荷，它们的最外层可以拥有超过8个电子。常见的例子包括以P、S或Cl等元素作为中心原子的物种。有时为了最小化中心原子的形式电荷，需要形成多个双键。此处以磷酸根离子PO₄³⁻的结构作为示例。

*Figure 1.2m phosphate anion Lewis structure*

> 图1.2m 磷酸根离子的路易斯结构

Elements in Period 3 (or higher) have 3 (or more than 3) principle shells, so the *d* orbital is available in the valence shell. That is why they can accommodate more than 8 electrons.

> 周期表第3周期（或更高级别的周期）中的元素具有3个（或更多）主电子壳层，因此d轨道在价电子壳层中是可利用的。这就是为什么它们能够容纳超过8个电子的原因。

*Key Takeaways*

> 重点总结

**For elements in 2nd period, C, N, O, F and Ne, the** *maximum* **number of electrons involved in Lewis structure is eight!!!**

> 第二周期的元素C、N、O、F和Ne，其路易斯结构中参与成键的电子最大数目为八个！！！

# 1.3 Resonance Structures

> 1.3 共轭结构

In the case that more than one reasonable (plausible) Lewis structure can be drawn for a species, these structures are called **resonance structures** or **resonance contributors**. Resonance structures can be either equivalent or nonequivalent.

> 当一个物种可以画出多个合理的（可接受的）路易斯结构时，这些结构被称为共振结构或共振贡献体。共振结构可以是等价的，也可以是非等价的。

### 0.1 **Equivalent Resonance Structures**

> 0.1 等价共振结构

Let's consider the example of carbonate anion, CO3 2-

> 让我们以碳酸根离子 CO₃²⁻ 为例进行分析。

![](_page_25_Figure_4.jpeg)

*Figure 1.3a Versions of the carbonate anion Lewis structure*

> 图1.3a 碳酸根离子的路易斯结构的不同版本

By following Step 6 in the **Lewis structure drawing procedure**, the double bond can be built between the central C and any of the terminal O's to generate three structures, and they all look "the same". However, they are not really identical (or same), they are just equivalent. Each structure is called a **resonance structure,** and they can be connected by the double-headed resonance arrow. There are total three *equivalent resonance structures* for CO3 2- , and the actual structure of CO3 2 is the *hybrid* of the three resonance contributors.

> 按照绘制路易斯结构的第6步，可以在中心碳原子与任意一个末端氧原子之间形成双键，从而生成三种结构，它们看起来“相同”。然而，它们实际上并不是完全相同（或相同），只是相互等价。每一种结构被称为共振结构，它们之间可以通过双箭头（共振箭头）相互连接。碳酸根离子（CO₃²⁻）总共有三种等价的共振结构，而碳酸根的实际结构是这三种共振结构的杂化体。

*Figure 1.3b Three equivalent resonance contributors of carbonate anion*

> 图1.3b 碳酸根离子的三种等价共振结构

The arrows used here to connect between resonance structures is the "**resonance arrow**", which has double arrow heads. Resonance structures have to be connected using resonance arrows.

> 此处用于连接共振结构的箭头称为“共振箭头”，其箭头为双头箭头。共振结构必须使用共振箭头进行连接。

Since the resonance structures are equivalent, they are all in the same level of energy and have the same stability, so they make the same contributions to the actual structure of CO3 2- . This is supported by the experimental evidence that all the carbon-oxygen bonds in CO3 2 are the same bond length, which is longer than a regular double bond but shorter than a single bond. As a result of the resonance structures, the two negative charges in CO3 2 are not localized on any oxygen atoms, but are spread evenly among all three oxygen atoms, and is called charge **delocalization.** Because of charge delocalization, each oxygen atom has two-thirds of a full negative charge. Charge delocalization helps to *stabilize* the whole species. The stability a species gains from having charge delocalization through resonance contributors is called *resonance stabilization effect.* The greater the number of resonance contributors, the greater the resonance stabilization effect, and the more stable the species is.

> 由于共振结构是等价的，它们处于相同的能量水平，具有相同的稳定性，因此它们对碳酸根离子（CO₃²⁻）的实际结构做出相同的贡献。这一结论得到了实验证据的支持：CO₃²⁻ 中所有的碳-氧键的键长都相同，其键长比普通的双键长，但比单键短。由于共振结构的存在，CO₃²⁻ 中的两个负电荷并不局限在任何一个氧原子上，而是均匀地分布在三个氧原子之间，这种现象称为电荷离域。由于电荷离域，每个氧原子都带有三分之二的负电荷。电荷离域有助于稳定整个离子。一个物种由于通过共振结构实现电荷离域而获得的稳定性，称为共振稳定效应。共振结构的数目越多，共振稳定效应就越显著，物种也就越稳定。

The actual structure of the carbonate anion is a combination of all the three equivalent resonance structures, that can be called a hybrid. What does the actual structure look like, and can we draw one structure on paper to show the actual structure? The actual structure can not be shown with a conventional Lewis structure, because the regular Lewis structures do not include partial charges, and there is two-thirds of a full negative charge on each oxygen atom in CO3 2- . An attempt to show the hybrid structure can be by using dashed lines to show that the bond between carbon and oxygen is somewhere between a single and double bond, and each oxygen atom has partial charges.

> 碳酸根离子的实际结构是三种等效的共振结构的组合，这种结构可以称为杂化结构。实际的结构是怎样的？我们能否在纸上画出一个结构来表示实际的结构呢？实际上，无法用常规的路易斯结构来表示碳酸根离子的结构，因为常规的路易斯结构不包含部分电荷，而在CO₃²⁻中，每个氧原子上都带有三分之二的负电荷。为了表示这种杂化结构，可以尝试用虚线表示碳与氧之间的键介于单键和双键之间，同时标明每个氧原子具有部分电荷。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_26_Picture_3.jpeg)

*Figure 1.3c Dashed lines drawn on the CO3 molecule Lewis structure to show the actual structure and partial charges*

> 图1.3c 在CO₃分子的路易斯结构上画出虚线，以显示实际结构和部分电荷

The delocalized charges can also be represented by the calculated **electrostatic potential map** of the electron density in the CO3 2 anion. In an electrostatic potential map, regions with different charges are shown in different colours. More specifically, colours trending towards red means higher negative charges, while colours trending toward blue means more positive charge (the colour system generated by different softwares might not be same, but will follow the same trend). In the electrostatic potential map of carbonate anion below, the same shade of red of all three oxygen atoms indicate the equal charge distribution at the three oxygen atoms.

> 分散化的电荷也可以通过CO₃²⁻阴离子中电子密度的计算静电势图来表示。在静电势图中，不同电荷区域会以不同的颜色表示。更具体地说，颜色向红色过渡表示负电荷更高，而颜色向蓝色过渡则表示正电荷更多（不同软件生成的颜色系统可能有所不同，但趋势是相同的）。在下面的碳酸根阴离子静电势图中，三个氧原子均呈现相同的红色，表明这三个氧原子上的电荷分布是相等的。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_27_Picture_0.jpeg)

*Figure 1.2d The electrostatic potential map of carbonate anion*

> 图1.2d 碳酸根阴离子的静电势图

#### 0.1.1 *Exercises 1.5*

> 0.1.1 习题 1.5

Draw all the equivalent resonance structures for following species. Include any non-zero formal charges in the structures.

> 画出下列物种的所有等价共振结构，并在结构中包含任何非零的形式电荷。

- O3 molecule
- nitrate anion NO3 –
- chlorate anion ClO3 – .

> O₃分子  
硝酸根离子 NO₃⁻  
氯酸根离子 ClO₃⁻

### 0.2 Answers to Practice Questions Chapter 1

> 0.2 习题解答 第1章

### 0.3 **Non-equivalent Resonance Structures**

> 0.3 非等价共振结构

Resonance structures can also be non-equivalent. For the example of OCN– , there are three *non-equivalent resonance structures*, depending on how the multiple bonds are formed in Step 6 of the **Lewis structure drawing procedure**.

> 共振结构也可以是非等价的。例如OCN⁻，存在三种非等价的共振结构，这取决于在路易斯结构绘制步骤第6步中，多重键是如何形成的。

$$\begin{bmatrix} \ddot{O} & & & \ddot{O} \\ \ddot{O} & & & \ddot{O} \end{bmatrix}^{-1} \longrightarrow \begin{bmatrix} \ddot{O} & & & & & & \\ \ddot{O} & & & & & & \\ \vdots & \ddot{O} & & & & & \\ & & & & & & & \\ & & & & &$$

> 

*Figure 1.3e Three non-equivalent resonance structure contributors of OCN-*

> 图1.3e OCN⁻ 的三种非等价共振结构贡献体

For non-equivalent resonance structures, the bonding and charge distributions are different, so they are in different energy levels. Some are more stable (better) resonance structures than others. The guidelines for comparing the relative stability between non-equivalent resonance structures are (the lower the energy, the more stable the structure is and vice versa):

> 对于非等价的共振结构，其成键和电荷分布不同，因此它们处于不同的能量水平。某些结构比其他结构更为稳定（更优）。比较非等价共振结构之间相对稳定性的指导原则如下（能量越低，结构越稳定，反之亦然）：

- The structure with complete octets is usually more stable, except in the cases in **section 1.2.4** "Exceptions to Octet Rule".
- The structure involving the smaller formal charges is more stable.
- Negative charges should be preferentially located on atoms with greater electronegativity, and positive charges should be preferentially located on atoms with less electronegativity
- Charge separation decreases the stability (increases the energy).

> 具有完整八隅体结构的分子通常更加稳定，除非在第1.2.4节“八隅体规则的例外情况”中所提到的特殊情况。  
涉及较小形式电荷的结构更加稳定。  
负电荷应优先位于电负性较大的原子上，正电荷应优先位于电负性较小的原子上。  
电荷分离会降低稳定性（增加能量）。

By applying the rules above, we can predict that for OCN– , structure **3** is the least stable one since it has the highest formal charges. For both structures **1** and **2**, the formal charge is "-1". It is more preferable for negative formal charges to be on oxygen, the more electronegative atom; therefore structure **2** is the most stable one.

> 根据上述规则，我们可以预测，对于OCN⁻而言，结构3是最不稳定的，因为它具有最高的形式电荷。对于结构1和结构2，形式电荷均为-1。由于氧原子比氮原子更具电负性，因此负的形式电荷更倾向于出现在氧原子上，因此结构2是最稳定的。

*Exercises 1.6*

> 练习 1.6

Draw all of the resonance structures for azide anion, N3 – , and indicate the most stable one.

> 画出叠氮化物离子 N₃⁻ 的所有共振结构，并指出其中最稳定的结构。

Answers to Practice Questions Chapter 1

> 练习题参考答案 第1章

# 1.4 Resonance structures in Organic Chemistry

> 1.4 有机化学中的共振结构

**Resonance stabilization effect** (also known as **resonance effect**), as briefly mentioned in **Section 1.3**, is one of the fundamental concepts of Organic Chemistry and has broad applications. The discussion of resonance effect heavily relies on the understanding of resonance structures. Here we will focus on how to draw resonance structures (or resonance contributors) for organic chemistry species, and how to compare the relative stabilities between the structures.

> 共振稳定效应（也称为共轭效应）如第1.3节中简要提到的，是有机化学中的一个基本概念，并具有广泛的应用。共轭效应的讨论高度依赖于对共振结构的理解。在这里，我们将重点介绍如何为有机化学物种绘制共振结构（或共振贡献体），以及如何比较不同结构之间的相对稳定性。

According to **resonance effect***,* the greater the number of resonance contributors, the greater the resonance stabilization effect, and the more stable the species is. Therefore, to predict whether the resonance effect applies or not, we usually need to construct "new" resonance structures (contributors) based on the "original" one that is available. There are some very important rules we need to follow for such purposes.

> 根据共轭效应，共振贡献体的数量越多，共振稳定化效应就越强，物种也就越稳定。因此，为了判断是否具有共轭效应，我们通常需要根据已知的“原始”共振结构，构建出“新的”共振结构（贡献体）。为了实现这一目的，我们需要遵循一些非常重要的规则。

#### 0.1.1 **Guidelines for Drawing Resonance Structures:**

> 0.1.1 绘制共振结构的指导原则：

- All resonance structures must be valid Lewis structures. **(Keep in mind that all the rules applied to Lewis structures still apply here!)**
- All resonance structures must have the same atom connectivity, and only differ in the electron arrangement. **(Atoms NEVER move, only electrons move.)**
- All resonance structures have the same number of electrons and net charge. **(Formal charges on individual atom could be different, but net charge, that is the sum of all the charges, must be the same.)**
- To move electrons, only π electrons and lone-pair electrons **(NEVER move σ bonds!)** can be moved from the higher electron density area to lower electron density area by following one of the three transformations:
  - **π bond forms another π bond;**
  - **π bond forms the lone pair electrons;**
  - **lone pair electrons forms a π bond.**
- Use **curved arrows** to indicate the electron movement in the "original" resonance structure. The "new" resonance structure should be a "product" automatically obtained by following the arrows.
- Calculate the formal charge in the "new" structure and label any non-zero formal charges.

> 所有共振结构都必须是有效的路易斯结构。（请记住，所有适用于路易斯结构的规则在这里仍然适用！）  
所有共振结构必须具有相同的原子连接方式，仅在电子排布上有所不同。（原子**绝不会**移动，只有**电子**会移动。）  
所有共振结构具有相同数量的电子和相同的总电荷。（单个原子的**形式电荷**可能不同，但**总电荷**，即所有电荷的总和，必须相同。）  
要移动电子，只能移动**π电子**和**孤对电子**（**绝不要移动σ键**！），从高电子密度区域移动到低电子密度区域，遵循以下三种转变之一：  
- π键形成另一个π键；  
- π键形成孤对电子；  
- 孤对电子形成π键。  
使用**带箭头的曲线**来表示“原始”共振结构中电子的移动方向。  
“新”的共振结构应通过遵循箭头方向**自动产生**。  
计算“新”结构中的**形式电荷**，并标记任何非零的形式电荷。

The way to use curved arrows show electron transfer is also called **arrow pushing**, it is a very important fundamental skill you need to master in organic chemistry. For the purpose of constructing "new" resonance structures, arrows have to be shown in the "original" structure.

> 使用弯曲箭头来展示电子转移的方法也被称为“箭头推动法”（arrow pushing），这是有机化学中一个非常重要的基础技能，你需要掌握。为了构建“新的”共振结构，必须在“原始”结构中画出箭头。

*Examples: Draw another resonance structure based on the given one.*

> 示例：根据给定的结构，画出另一种共振结构。

1.

> 1.

$$\begin{array}{c} H \\ C = C \\ H \\ C \\ H \end{array}$$

> 

**Approach:** There is only one π bond in this example, and no any lone pairs, so only the π electrons can be moved around. There is a carbocation beside the π bond, which is the low electron density spot. Therefore it is reasonable to move the π electrons to the position beside carbocation to form another π bond, and that gives the "new" structure. The two resonance structures here are *equivalent*.

> 方法：在这个例子中，只有一个π键，且没有孤对电子，因此只能移动π电子。在π键旁边存在一个碳正离子，这是电子密度较低的区域。因此，将π电子移动到碳正离子旁边形成另一个π键是合理的，这样就形成了“新的”结构。此处的两个共振结构是等同的。

#### 0.1.2 **Solution**

> 0.1.2 解决方案

![](_page_30_Figure_4.jpeg)

# 2.

> 2.

**Approach:** More electrons available for movement in this example: several lone pairs and one π bond. The guideline of "move electrons from the **higher** electron density area **to the lower** electron density area" provides a useful hint about where to start. The nitrogen atom has a "-" formal charge, meaning it has relatively high electron density, higher than other neutral spots. So it is reasonable to move the lone pair on nitrogen away to form a π bond **(**keep in mind that **lone pair can only form π bond,** *not* **another lone pair)**. However, when the new π bond is formed around the carbon atom, there are 5 bonds (10 electrons) on that carbon, which is not allowed. So, another electron pair has to be moved away, and the only available electron pair to be moved is the π electrons in C=O bond. It can be moved onto the oxygen atom and become another lone pair on the oxygen atom.

> 方法：在此例中，有更多的电子可供移动：多个孤对电子和一个π键。遵循“从高电子密度区域向低电子密度区域移动电子”的指导原则，可以为我们提供一个良好的起点。氮原子带有“-”形式电荷，意味着它具有相对较高的电子密度，比其他中性区域的电子密度更高。因此，将氮原子上的孤对电子移走，形成一个π键是合理的（请注意，孤对电子只能形成π键，而不能形成另一个孤对）。然而，当在碳原子周围形成新的π键时，该碳原子上会有5个键（共10个电子），这是不允许的。因此，必须再移走一个电子对，而唯一可移动的电子对是C=O键中的π电子。这些π电子可以移至氧原子上，形成氧原子上的另一个孤对电子。

### 0.1 **Solution:**

> 0.1 解法：

The two resonance structures in this example are *non-equivalent*, so one is more stable than the other. By applying the formal charge guideline, the "-" formal charge is more preferable on oxygen, which is more electronegative than nitrogen, so the 2nd structure is the more stable one with lower energy, and makes more contribution to the actual structure in this species. The more stable structure can also be called as the major resonance contributor.

> 此例中的两个共振结构是非等价的，因此其中一个比另一个更稳定。根据形式电荷规则，负形式电荷更倾向于出现在电负性更高的氧原子上，而非氮原子上。因此，第二个结构更稳定，能量更低，对实际结构的贡献更大。这种更稳定的结构也被称为主要共振贡献体。

### 0.2 **Comparing the relative stability of different resonance contributors:**

> 0.2 比较不同共振结构的相对稳定性：

- Structures with a maximum of octets are most important.
- Charge separation usually decrease the stability (increase the energy of the contributor).
- Negative charges should be preferentially located on atoms with greater electronegativity, and positive charges should be preferentially located on atoms with less electronegativity.

> 具有最多八电子的结构最为重要。  
电荷分离通常会降低稳定性（增加贡献体的能量）。  
负电荷应优先位于电负性更大的原子上，正电荷应优先位于电负性较小的原子上。

### 0.3 **Common errors for drawing resonance structures:**

> 0.3 绘制共振结构时的常见错误：

- 1. **σ bond is moved**
- 2. **Atom is moved**
- 3. **More than eight electrons located around C, N or O**
- 4. **Arrows are not shown in the proper way**
- 5. **Electron pairs are moved too far away, they should only be moved to the next position/atom.**

> σ 键被移动  
原子被移动  
碳、氮或氧原子周围有超过八个电子  
箭头未以正确方式表示  
电子对被移动得太远，它们应仅移动到下一个位置或原子

*Exercises 1.7 Draw new resonance structure and compare the relative stability, show arrows in the original structure.*

> 练习 1.7 画出新的共振结构并比较其相对稳定性，在原结构中用箭头标明电子转移方向。

1. 2.

> 2.

Answers to Practice Questions Chapter 1

> 练习题参考答案 第1章

# 1.5 Valence-Shell Electron-Pair Repulsion Theory (VSEPR)

> 1.5 价层电子对互斥理论（VSEPR）

The **Valence-Shell Electron-Pair Repulsion (VSEPR)** theory helps us to understand and predict the geometry (shape) of molecules or ions. The theory is:

> 价层电子对互斥理论（VSEPR理论）帮助我们理解并预测分子或离子的几何形状（结构）。该理论是：

- Electron pairs repel each other whether they are in chemical bonds or lone pairs.
- Valence electron pairs are oriented to be as far apart as possible to minimize repulsions.

> 电子对无论是处于化学键中还是作为孤对电子，都会相互排斥。  
价层电子对会尽可能远离彼此，以最大限度地减少排斥作用。

Based on this theory, depending on the number of electron pairs (both bonding pairs and lone pairs) around the central atom, a certain shape is adopted to minimize the repulsion between election pairs, as summarized in the table below:

> 根据这一理论，根据中心原子周围电子对（包括成键电子对和孤对电子）的数量，分子会采取一定的几何构型，以最大程度地减少电子对之间的排斥作用，具体总结如下表：

| Total number of electron groups<br>(electron pairs) around central atom | Geometry (Shape) of electron groups<br>(electron pairs) |  |
|-------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------|--|
| 2                                                                       | linear                                                  |  |
| 3                                                                       | trigonal planar                                         |  |
| 4                                                                       | tetrahedral                                             |  |
| 5                                                                       | trigonal bipyramidal                                    |  |
| 6                                                                       | octahedral                                              |  |

> | 中心原子周围的电子对总数（电子组数） | 电子对的几何构型（形状） |  |
|-----------------------------|--------------------------|---|
| 2                           | 直线型                  |   |
| 3                           | 三角平面型              |   |
| 4                           | 四面体型                |   |
| 5                           | 三角双锥型              |   |
| 6                           | 八面体型                |   |

**Table 1.1 Basic VSEPR Shapes**

> 表 1.1 基本的VSEPR模型

#### 0.1.1 **Notes**:

> 0.1.1 注释：

- For VSEPR purpose, the terms "**shape**" and "**geometry**" are interchangeable; "**electron pair**" and "**electron group**" are also interchangeable.
- Multiple bonds (double or triple bond) are regarded as **one electron group** for VSEPR purpose.

> 在VSEPR理论中，“形状”和“几何构型”可以互换使用；“电子对”和“电子组”也可以互换使用。  
多个键（双键或三键）在VSEPR理论中被视为一个电子组。

For species that do not have any lone pair electrons (LP), the geometry (shape) of the species is just the same as the geometry of the electron groups.

> 对于没有孤对电子（LP）的物种，其空间构型（形状）与电子对的几何构型完全相同。

For the example of the PCl5 molecule, there are five electron groups on the central phosphorous, and they are all bonding pairs (BP). The shape of the electron groups is trigonal bipyramidal, and the shape of the PCl5 molecule is trigonal bipyramidal as well. The trigonal bipyramidal shape can be drawn on paper using solid and dashed wedges: the three bonds lie within the paper plane are shown as ordinary lines, the solid wedge represent a bond that points out of the paper plane, and the dashed wedge represent a bond that points behind the paper plane.

> 以五氯化磷（PCl₅）分子为例，中心磷原子周围共有五个电子对，且均为成键对（BP）。这些电子对的排布形状为三角双锥形，因此PCl₅分子的几何构型也是三角双锥形。三角双锥形结构可以用实线、楔形线和虚线在纸上表示：位于纸面平面上的三个键用普通直线表示，实线楔形表示指向纸面前方的键，虚线楔形表示指向纸面后方的键。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_34_Picture_0.jpeg)

*Figure1.5a Tigonal bipyramidal shape of PCl5 molecule*

> 图1.5a PCl₅分子的三角双锥构型

However, for the species that has lone pair electrons on the central atom, the shape of the species will be *different* to the shape of the electron groups. The reason is that even though the lone pairs occupy the space, there are no terminal atoms connected with lone pair, so the lone pair become "invisible" for the shape of the species.

> 然而，对于中心原子上存在孤对电子的物种，其分子的几何形状与电子对的排布形状会有所不同。原因在于，尽管孤对电子占据了一定的空间，但由于没有与孤对电子相连的终端原子，因此孤对电子在确定分子形状时变得“不可见”。

For the example of the water (H2O) molecule, the central oxygen atom has two BPs and two LPs, and the shape of all the electron groups is tetrahedral. The shape of a water molecule is bent because only the atoms are counted towards the molecular shape, not the lone pair electrons.

> 以水分子（H₂O）为例，中心氧原子具有两个成键电子对（BPs）和两个孤对电子（LPs），所有电子对的几何构型为四面体。水分子的形状为V形（弯曲形），这是因为分子形状的判断仅考虑原子的位置，而不包括孤对电子。

![](_page_34_Picture_4.jpeg)

*Figure 1.5b Bent shape of H20 molecule*

> 图1.5b 水分子的弯曲形状

The VSEPR shapes can be rather diverse, considering the different numbers of total electron pairs together with the different numbers of lone pairs involved. The most common shapes are summarized in the following table (Table 1.2). To describe a certain shape, the specific name has to be used properly, and the bond angle information is important as well.

> 根据总电子对数和孤对电子数的不同，VSEPR模型所预测的分子几何形状可以有多种多样。最常见的分子几何形状总结在下表中（表1.2）。要准确描述某种分子几何形状，必须正确使用特定的名称，同时，键角信息也具有重要意义。

| Total number of e-groups | Geometry (shape) ofall the<br>electron groups | # of Bonding Pairs (BP) and Lone<br>Pairs (LP) | Geometry (shape) of the species | Angles (°)    |
|--------------------------|-----------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------|---------------|
| 2                        | linear                                        | 2BP                                            | linear                          | 180           |
|                          |                                               | 3BP                                            | trigonal planar                 | 120           |
| 3                        | trigonal planar                               | 2BP, 1LP                                       | bent                            | <120          |
|                          |                                               | 4BP                                            | tetrahedral                     | 109.5         |
| 4                        | tetrahedral                                   | 3BP, 1LP                                       | trigonal pyramidal              | <109.5        |
|                          |                                               | 2BP, 2LP                                       | bent                            | <109.5        |
|                          |                                               | 5BP                                            | trigonal bipyramidal            | 120, 90, 180  |
| 5                        |                                               | 4BP, 1LP                                       | see-saw                         | <120, 90, 180 |
|                          | trigonal bipyramidal                          | 3BP, 2LP                                       | T-shape                         | 90, 180       |
|                          |                                               | 2BP, 3LP                                       | linear                          | 180           |
|                          |                                               | 6BP                                            | octahedral                      | 90, 180       |
| 6                        | octahedral                                    | 5BP, 1LP                                       | square pyramidal                | 90, 180       |
|                          |                                               | 4BP, 2LP                                       | square planar                   | 90, 180       |

> | 电子对总数 | 所有电子对的几何构型（形状） | 键对（BP）和孤对（LP）数量 | 分子的几何构型（形状） | 键角（°） |
|------|-----------------------------|------------------|------------------|--------|
| 2 | 直线型 | 2BP | 直线型 | 180 |
|  |  | 3BP | 平面三角形 | 120 |
| 3 | 平面三角形 | 2BP, 1LP | V型（弯曲型） | <120 |
|  |  | 4BP | 四面体 | 109.5 |
| 4 | 四面体 | 3BP, 1LP | 三角锥型 | <109.5 |
|  |  | 2BP, 2LP | V型（弯曲型） | <109.5 |
|  |  | 5BP | 三角双锥型 | 120, 90, 180 |
| 5 |  | 4BP, 1LP | 交错型（见习型） | <120, 90, 180 |
|  | 三角双锥型 | 3BP, 2LP | T型 | 90, 180 |
|  |  | 2BP, 3LP | 直线型 | 180 |
|  |  | 6BP | 八面体型 | 90, 180 |
| 6 | 八面体型 | 5BP, 1LP | 平面正方形 | 90, 180 |
|  |  | 4BP, 2LP | 平面正方形 | 90, 180 |

#### 0.1.2 **Table 1.2 Summary of specific VSEPR shapes**

> 0.1.2 表1.2 特定VSEPR模型的总结

The website **https://phet.colorado.edu/sims/html/molecule-shapes/latest/molecule-shapes\_en.html** provides good resources for visualizing and practicing VSEPR topics.

> 网站 https://phet.colorado.edu/sims/html/molecule-shapes/latest/molecule-shapes_en.html 提供了用于可视化和练习VSEPR理论的优质资源。

We will see more applications of VSEPR in organic compounds in next section.

> 在下一节中，我们将看到VSEPR理论在有机化合物中更多的应用。

# 1.6 Valence Bond Theory and Hybridization

> 1.6 键合理论与杂化

#### 0.1.1 **1.6.1 Valence Bond Theory**

> 0.1.1 1.6.1 价键理论

We have talked about how covalent bonds are formed through the sharing of a pair of electrons; here we will apply the **valence bond theory** to explain in more detail how the sharing happens. The valence bond theory describes the covalent bond formed from the overlap of two half-filled atomic orbitals on different atoms.

> 我们已经讨论过共价键是如何通过一对电子的共享形成的；在这里，我们将应用价键理论，更详细地解释这一共享过程。价键理论描述了共价键的形成，即两个不同原子上各有一个半充满的原子轨道发生重叠而形成的。

Let's start with the simple molecule H2. The atomic electron configuration of a hydrogen atom is 1s<sup>1</sup> , meaning that there is one electron (which is also the valence electron) in the sphere-shaped 1s orbital.

> 让我们从简单的分子 H₂ 开始。氢原子的原子电子排布是 1s¹，这意味着在球形的 1s 轨道中有一个电子（同时也是它的价电子）。

When two hydrogen atoms are approaching each other, the two 1s orbitals overlap, allowing the two electrons (each H donates 1 electron) to pair up for the bonding with the overlapping orbitals. The shared pair of electrons are under the attraction of both hydrogen nuclei simultaneously, resulting in them serving as a "glue" that holds the two nuclei together.

> 当两个氢原子相互接近时，两个1s轨道发生重叠，使得两个电子（每个氢原子贡献一个电子）能够配对，形成共价键。这两个共享的电子同时受到两个氢原子核的吸引，从而起到一种“胶合剂”的作用，将两个原子核结合在一起。

![](_page_37_Figure_5.jpeg)

*Figure 1.6a Formation of H-H bond*

> 图1.6a H-H键的形成

The overall energy changes of the system *versus* the distance between the two hydrogen nuclei can be summarized in the energy diagram below.

> 系统总体能量变化与两个氢核之间的距离之间的关系可总结在下面的能量图中。

![](_page_38_Figure_0.jpeg)

*Figure 1.6b Potential energy of the hydrogen molecule as a function of internuclear distance*

> 图1.6b 氢分子的势能与核间距的关系

When the two atoms are separate, there is no overlap and no interaction. As they are getting closer, orbitals start to overlap, and there is attraction between the nucleus of one atom and the electron of the other atom, so the total energy of the system lowers. The energy lowers to its minimum level when the two atoms approach the optimal distance. The optimal distance is also defined as the **bond length**. H2 molecules have a bond length of 74 pm (often referred to as 0.74 Å, 1Å= 10-10m). The energy difference between the most stable state (lowest energy state with optimum distance) and the state in which the two atoms are completely separated is called the **bond (dissociation) energy**. The bond energy is 7.22×10-19 J for one H-H bond, or 435kJ/mol.

> 当两个原子彼此分离时，它们之间没有重叠也没有相互作用。随着它们逐渐靠近，轨道开始发生重叠，此时一个原子的原子核与另一个原子的电子之间产生吸引力，从而使系统的总能量降低。当两个原子接近到最适距离时，系统的能量降低至最低水平。这个最适距离也被称为键长。H₂分子的键长为74 pm（通常表示为0.74 Å，1 Å = 10⁻¹⁰ m）。最稳定状态（即能量最低且距离最适的状态）与两个原子完全分离的状态之间的能量差称为键（解离）能。一个H-H键的键能为7.22×10⁻¹⁹ J，或435 kJ/mol。

When the two atoms get closer than the optimal distance, the repulsion between the two nuclei become predominant, and the energy of the system becomes even higher.

> 当两个原子之间的距离小于最优距离时，两个原子核之间的排斥力变得主导，系统的能量会变得更高。

Another important character of the covalent bond in H2 is that the two 1s orbitals overlap in a way that is referred to as head-to-head. The bond formed by head-to-head overlap is called **σ (sigma) bond**. σ bonds are cylindrically symmetrical, meaning if a cross-sectional plane is taken of the bond at any point, it would form a circle.

> H₂分子中共价键的另一个重要特征是，两个1s轨道以所谓的“头对头”方式重叠。由头对头重叠形成的键称为σ（西格玛）键。σ键具有圆柱形对称性，即如果在键的任意一点取一个横截面，该截面将形成一个圆。

![](_page_38_Figure_5.jpeg)

*Figure 1.6c Cylindrical symmetry property of σ bond*

> 图1.6c σ键的圆柱对称性

The valence bond theory works well to explain the bonding in HF as well, with the 2p orbital of fluorine atom involved in the overlapping.

> 价键理论同样很好地解释了HF中的成键情况，氟原子的2p轨道参与了轨道重叠。

The fluorine atom has the valence electron configuration of 2s<sup>2</sup> 2p<sup>5</sup> as shown in the orbital diagram.

> 氟原子的价电子排布为 2s² 2p⁵，如轨道图所示。

![](_page_38_Figure_9.jpeg)

*Figure 1.6d Orbital diagram of valence electrons in fluorine atom*

> 图1.6d 氟原子价电子的轨道图

For the three 2p orbitals, two of them are filled and the other one is half-filled with one single electron. The filled orbital cannot form bonds, so only the half-filled 2p is available for overlap. Therefore, the 1s orbital of the hydrogen atom overlaps head-to-head with the half-filled 2p orbital of the fluorine atom to form the H-F σ bond, as shown below.

> 对于三个2p轨道来说，其中两个被填满，另一个则有一个单电子处于半填充状态。被填满的轨道无法形成化学键，因此只有这个半填充的2p轨道可用于重叠。因此，氢原子的1s轨道与氟原子的半填充2p轨道以“头对头”的方式重叠，形成H-F σ键，如下所示。

![](_page_39_Figure_1.jpeg)

*Figure 1.6e H-F σ bond*

> 图1.6e H-F σ键

A σ bond can also be formed through the overlap of two *p* orbitals. The covalent bond in molecular fluorine, F2, is a σ bond formed by the overlap of two half-filled 2*p* orbitals, one from each fluorine atom as shown here.

> σ 键也可以通过两个 p 轨道的重叠形成。分子氟（F₂）中的共价键是一种σ键，由两个半充满的 2p 轨道重叠形成，每个氟原子各提供一个 2p 轨道，如图所示。

![](_page_39_Figure_4.jpeg)

*Figure 1.6f F2 σ bond*

> 图1.6f F2 σ键

However, when the valence bond theory is applied to organic molecules, for instance CH4, it does **not** work. The valence electron configuration of carbon atom is 2s<sup>2</sup> 2p<sup>2</sup> as shown in the orbital diagram.

> 然而，当用价键理论来解释有机分子时，例如CH₄，该理论并不适用。碳原子的价电子排布为2s² 2p²，如轨道图所示。

![](_page_39_Picture_7.jpeg)

*Figure 1.6g Orbital diagram of valence electrons in carbon atom*

> 图1.6g 碳原子价电子的轨道图

Based on the valence bond theory, with two half-filled orbitals available, the carbon atom should be able to form two bonds. However, carbon always has four bonds in any stable organic compound. To explain the bonding of carbon and other atoms that cannot fit into the simple valence bond theory, a new theory called orbital **hybridization** will be introduced as a supplement to the valence bond theory.

> 根据价键理论，碳原子有两个半充满的轨道，应该只能形成两个共价键。然而，在任何稳定的有机化合物中，碳原子总是形成四个共价键。为了解释碳原子及其他无法用简单价键理论解释的原子的成键情况，我们将引入一种称为轨道杂化的新理论，作为对价键理论的补充。

### 0.2 **1.6.2 Hybridization and the Structure of CH4**

> 0.2 1.6.2 杂化轨道与甲烷的结构

Simply speaking, hybridization means the mathematical combination of several orbitals to generate a set of new hybrid orbitals.

> 简而言之，杂化是指将几个轨道进行数学组合，生成一组新的杂化轨道。

In the hybridization for CH4, the 2s and three 2p orbitals are combined to give a new set of four identical orbitals,

> 在CH₄的杂化过程中，1个2s轨道和三个2p轨道组合形成一组新的四个等同轨道。

that are called **sp<sup>3</sup>** hybrid orbitals. The symbol **sp<sup>3</sup>** here identify the numbers and types of orbitals involved in the hybridization: **one** *s* and **three** *p* orbitals. For the hybridization process,

> 称为sp³杂化轨道。此处的符号sp³表示参与杂化的轨道数目和类型：一个s轨道和三个p轨道。对于杂化过程，

number of hybrid orbitals = the total number of atomic orbitals that are combined

> 杂化轨道数目 = 被组合的原子轨道总数

It means that with total four orbitals combined, four new hybrid orbitals are generated, and they all named as **sp<sup>3</sup> hybrid orbitals**. These new hybrid orbitals are all in the same energy level that is between those of 2s and 2p orbitals, and are directed in a tetrahedral shape overall with the angle between any two orbitals as 109.5°. Each sp<sup>3</sup> hybrid orbital has two lobes that are very different in size. The lobe with the larger size is in the positive phase and is responsible for bonding.

> 这意味着四个轨道组合后生成了四个新的杂化轨道，它们都被称为sp³杂化轨道。这些新的杂化轨道都处于一个能量相同的能级，介于2s轨道和2p轨道的能量之间，并且整体呈正四面体形状，任意两个轨道之间的夹角为109.5°。每个sp³杂化轨道都有两个 lobes（叶），它们的大小差异很大。其中较大的那个叶处于正相位，负责成键。

![](_page_40_Figure_3.jpeg)

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_40_Figure_4.jpeg)

*Figure 1.6h Four sp3 hybrid orbitals oriented in tetrahedral shape*

> 图1.6h 四个sp³杂化轨道呈四面体形状排列

Since there are four sp<sup>3</sup> hybrid orbitals available, each of the four valence electrons occupies one of them, so there are four half-filled sp<sup>3</sup> orbitals in the carbon atom that are able to form four bonds. Therefore, the C-H bond of CH4 is formed by the overlapping between the 1s orbital in the hydrogen atom and the sp<sup>3</sup> orbital in the carbon atom.

> 由于存在四个sp³杂化轨道，每个价电子各占据一个轨道，因此碳原子中存在四个半充满的sp³轨道，能够形成四个共价键。因此，甲烷（CH₄）中的C-H键是由氢原子的1s轨道与碳原子的sp³轨道之间的重叠形成的。

![](_page_40_Figure_7.jpeg)

*Figure 1.6i Orbital overlap of C-H bonds in methane*

> 图1.6i 甲烷中C-H键的轨道重叠

Because the arrangement of the four sp<sup>3</sup> hybrid orbitals is in a tetrahedral, the shape of the CH4 molecule is also a tetrahedral, which is consistent with the shape predicted by VSEPR. The tetrahedral shape of the sp<sup>3</sup> carbon can usually be drawn using the solid and dashed wedges. Out of the fours bonds, the two bonds that lie within the paper plane are shown as ordinary lines, the solid wedge represent a bond that point out of the paper plane, and the dashed wedge represent a bond that point behind the paper plane. These perspective drawings that show the 3D tetrahedral shape is particularly important in the discussion of stereochemistry in **Chapter 5**.

> 由于四个sp³杂化轨道的排布呈正四面体结构，因此CH₄分子的形状也呈正四面体，这与VSEPR理论预测的分子形状一致。通常，sp³杂化碳原子的正四面体结构可以通过实线和虚线楔形来表示。在四个键中，位于纸平面上的两个键用普通直线表示，实线楔形表示一个键从纸面前方伸出，虚线楔形表示一个键位于纸面后方。这些展示三维正四面体结构的透视图在第5章讨论立体化学时尤为重要。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_41_Picture_1.jpeg)

*Figure 1.6j Tetrahedral shape of methane with solid and dashed wedges drawing*

> 图1.6j 甲烷的四面体结构，使用实线和虚线楔形图示

### 0.3 **1.6.3 Hybridization and VSEPR**

> 0.3 1.6.3 杂化与VSEPR理论

Other than sp<sup>3</sup> hybridization, there are also other types of hybridization that include sp, sp<sup>2</sup> , sp<sup>3</sup> d and sp<sup>3</sup> d 2 . Usually the hybridization on a certain atom can simply be determined by counting the total number of electron groups (bonding pairs and lone pairs). **The total number of electron groups just equals the total number of orbitals involved in the certain hybridization.** For example, in a CH4 molecule, the central carbon atom has four 4 bonding pairs, so the hybridization of carbon is sp<sup>3</sup> (one *s* and three *p* orbitals, 1+3=4). If a central atom has total five 5 electron groups (bonding pairs and lone pairs all together) around, then the hybridization is sp<sup>3</sup> d (one *s*, three *p* and one *d* orbitals, 1+3+1=5).

> 除了sp³杂化外，还存在其他类型的杂化方式，包括sp、sp²、sp³d和sp³d²。通常，某一原子的杂化类型可以通过计算其周围电子对（成键对和孤对）的总数来确定。总的电子对数正好等于该杂化所涉及的轨道总数。例如，在CH₄分子中，中心碳原子周围有四个成键对，因此碳原子的杂化类型为sp³（一个s轨道和三个p轨道，1+3=4）。如果中心原子周围共有五个电子对（包括成键对和孤对），则其杂化类型为sp³d（一个s轨道、三个p轨道和一个d轨道，1+3+1=5）。

This correlation may remind you of VSEPR. Hybridization and VSEPR are two separate concepts, however they can be correlated together via the number of electron groups in common. The following table is very useful in correlating the hybridization and VSEPR shape/bond angles around the central atom and the total number of electron groups together.

> 这一关联可能会让你联想到VSEPR理论。杂化轨道与VSEPR理论是两个独立的概念，但它们可以通过共有的电子对数进行关联。下表在关联中心原子周围的杂化类型、VSEPR形状和键角以及总的电子对数方面非常有用。

| Hybridization on central atom | Total number of electron pairs (BP<br>and LP) around central atom | Geometry (Shape) of electron groups<br>(electron pairs) |
|-------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------|
| sp                            | 2                                                                 | linear                                                  |
| sp2                           | 3                                                                 | trigonal planar                                         |
| sp3                           | 4                                                                 | tetrahedral                                             |
| sp3<br>d                      | 5                                                                 | trigonal bipyramidal                                    |
| sp3<br>2<br>d                 | 6                                                                 | octahedral                                              |

> | 中心原子的杂化类型 | 中心原子周围电子对总数（成键对BP和孤对LP） | 电子对的几何构型（电子组态） |
|------------------|------------------|------------------|
| sp               | 2                | 直线型          |
| sp²              | 3                | 平面三角型      |
| sp³              | 4                | 四面体型        |
| sp³<br>d         | 5                | 三角双锥型      |
| sp³<br>2<br>d    | 6                | 八面体型        |

**Table 1.3 Correlation between Hybridization and VSEPR**

> 表1.3 杂化方式与VSEPR理论的关系

> 0.3.1 习题 1.8

- 1. What is the hybridization of the oxygen atom in H2O molecule?
- 2. What is the hybridization of the xenon atom in XeF4 molecule, and what is the shape of the whole molecule?

> 水分子（H₂O）中的氧原子的杂化类型是什么？  
四氟化氙（XeF₄）分子中的氙原子的杂化类型是什么？整个分子的几何构型是什么？

### 0.4 **1.6.4 The Hybridization and VSEPR in Organic Molecules**

> 0.4 1.6.4 有机分子中的杂化与VSEPR理论

Organic molecules usually contain more than one central atom, so it is not practical to name the shape of the whole molecule; instead we can talk about the shape/bond angle about each central atom individually. For such purposes, make sure to include the lone pairs that are usually left out in the organic structures (refer to section **1.2.4**). The different structural formulas of ethanol, acetic acid and ethanenitrile molecules are shown in the table below. The 3D molecular model for each compound is shown as well to help you visualize the spatial arrangement. We can see that the hybridization and VSEPR shapes need to be indicated for each internal atom separately. Taking the oxygen atom in the OH group of ethanol as an example, since there two pairs of lone pair electrons on the oxygen atom as well (omitted in the structures in the table though), the oxygen has sp<sup>3</sup> hybridization and is in the tetrahedral shape.

> 有机分子通常含有多个中心原子，因此对整个分子的形状进行命名并不实际；相反，我们可以分别讨论每个中心原子的形状或键角。为达到此目的，请务必包括通常在有机结构中被省略的孤对电子（参见第1.2.4节）。下表展示了乙醇、乙酸和乙腈分子的不同结构式。每个化合物的三维分子模型也一并展示，以帮助你更直观地理解其空间排列。我们可以看出，每个内部原子的杂化类型和VSEPR理论所预测的几何形状都需要分别说明。以乙醇中羟基（OH）中的氧原子为例，该氧原子上还存在两对孤对电子（尽管在表中的结构式中被省略了），因此该氧原子具有sp³杂化，呈四面体结构。

![](_page_43_Figure_0.jpeg)

*Table 1.4 Hybridization and VSEPR of Organic molecule examples [Image Description]*

> 表1.4 有机分子实例的杂化与VSEPR理论 [图片描述]

#### 0.4.1 **1.6.5 Multiple Bonds in Organic Structure**

> 0.4.1 1.6.5 有机结构中的多重键

### 0.5 **Ethene (C2H4)**

> 0.5 乙烯（C₂H₄）

We will take Ethene (C2H4) as an example for understanding the structure of a double bond.

> 我们将以乙烯（C₂H₄）为例，来理解双键的结构。

$$\begin{array}{cccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccc$$

> 

*Figure 1.6k Ethene hybridization*

> 图1.6k 乙烯的杂化

According to the structure formula of C2H4, there are three electron groups around each carbon. Through referring to **Table 1.3** it is determined that both carbons are in sp<sup>2</sup> hybridization, with the trigonal planar shape and a 120° bond angle. What does sp<sup>2</sup> hybridization mean to the carbon atom in this compound? It means that only three orbitals are involved in the hybridization (one 2*s* and two of 2*p* orbitals) out of the total four, and there is one 2p orbital left out, or not included in the hybridization, which is called the unhybridized 2p.

> 根据C₂H₄的结构式，每个碳原子周围都有三个电子对。通过参考表1.3可以确定，这两个碳原子均处于sp²杂化状态，具有三角平面型结构，键角为120°。这种sp²杂化对碳原子在该化合物中的意义是什么？它意味着在四个轨道中，只有三个轨道参与了杂化（一个2s轨道和两个2p轨道），而剩下的一个2p轨道未参与杂化，即未被杂化，这种未参与杂化的2p轨道被称为未杂化2p轨道。

![](_page_44_Figure_1.jpeg)

*Figure 1.6l Orbital hybridization diagram of valence electrons in Ethene*

> 图1.6l 乙烯价电子的轨道杂化示意图

The three new sp<sup>2</sup> hybrid orbitals and the unhybridized 2p are directed in the following arrangement: the three sp<sup>2</sup> hybrid orbitals are in the trigonal planar shape, and the unhybridized 2p is in the position that is perpendicular to the plane. Each orbital has one single electron, so all the orbitals are half-filled and are available for bonding. Both carbon atoms have the same set of orbitals (three sp<sup>2</sup> hybrid orbital and one unhybridized 2p) as shown below.

> 三个新的sp²杂化轨道和未杂化的2p轨道按照以下方式排列：三个sp²杂化轨道呈三角平面构型，而未杂化的2p轨道则垂直于该平面。每个轨道中各有一个单电子，因此所有轨道都是半充满的，可以参与成键。两个碳原子具有相同的轨道组（三个sp²杂化轨道和一个未杂化的2p轨道），如下所示。

![](_page_44_Figure_4.jpeg)

*Figure 1.6m The set of orbitals: sp2 + 2p*

> 图1.6m 轨道集合：sp² + 2p

![](_page_44_Picture_7.jpeg)

*Figure 1.6n The set of orbitals sp2 + 2p*

> 图1.6n sp²杂化轨道与2p轨道的组合

When the two carbons approach each other, the sp<sup>2</sup> on the x axis overlaps head-to-head to form the C-C σ sigma bond, and the "unhybridized" 2p overlaps side-by-side to form another new bond. **The side-by-side orbital overlapping forms the π (pi) bond.**

> 当两个碳原子相互靠近时，x轴方向上的sp²杂化轨道头对头重叠，形成C—C σ键；而“未杂化”的2p轨道则以侧边重叠的方式形成另一个新的键。侧边轨道重叠形成π（π）键。

![](_page_45_Figure_0.jpeg)

*Figure 1.6o Side-by-side overlap of p orbitals leading to pi (π) bond*

> 图1.6o p轨道并排重叠形成π（π）键

So now we understand that the C=C double bond contains two different bonds: σ (sigma) bond from sp<sup>2</sup> –sp<sup>2</sup> orbital overlapping and π (pi) bond from 2p–2p overlapping. Because of the π bond, the overall shape of the whole C2H4 molecule is co-planar.

> 因此，我们现在了解到，碳-碳双键（C=C）包含两种不同的化学键：一种是来自sp²轨道重叠形成的σ（sigma）键，另一种是来自2p轨道重叠形成的π（pi）键。由于π键的存在，整个C₂H₄分子的整体结构呈共平面状。

The other sp<sup>2</sup> hybrid orbitals on each carbon atom overlap with 1s orbital of H atoms and give total four C-H σ (sigma) bonds.

> 每个碳原子上的其他sp<sup>2</sup>杂化轨道与氢原子的1s轨道重叠，形成总共四个C-H σ（西格玛）键。

![](_page_45_Picture_4.jpeg)

*Figure 1.6p Sigma (σ) bond framework of C2H4*

> 图1.6p 乙烯（C₂H₄）的σ键骨架

### 0.6 **Ethyne (C2H2)**

> 0.6 乙炔（C₂H₂）

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_45_Picture_7.jpeg)

*Figure 1.6q Ethyne hybridization*

> 图1.6q 乙炔的杂化

Ethyne C2H2 (common name is acetylene) has a C≡C triple bond. Generally, triple bonds involve one σ sigma bond and two π (pi) bonds. Both carbon atom is in sp hybridization and in linear shape. With sp hybridization, each carbon has two sp hybrid orbitals and two unhybridized 2p orbitals. Each carbon uses one sp hybrid orbital to overlap head-to-head and gives the C-C the σ sigma bond, meanwhile the 2p orbitals overlap side-by-side to give two π bonds as shown in the diagram below. The other sp orbitals are used for overlapping with 1s of hydrogen atoms to form C-H σ bonds.

> 乙炔（C₂H₂，俗称电石）含有一个碳碳三键（C≡C）。一般来说，三键由一个σ键和两个π键组成。两个碳原子均采用sp杂化轨道，形成线性结构。在sp杂化状态下，每个碳原子拥有两个sp杂化轨道和两个未杂化的2p轨道。每个碳原子用一个sp杂化轨道头对头重叠，形成C–C σ键；同时，两个2p轨道以侧边重叠的方式形成两个π键，如图所示。剩余的sp轨道则与氢原子的1s轨道重叠，形成C–H σ键。

![](_page_45_Figure_10.jpeg)

*Figure 1.6r Orbital hybridization diagram of valence electrons in Ethyne*

> 图1.6r 乙炔价电子的轨道杂化示意图

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_46_Picture_0.jpeg)

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_46_Picture_1.jpeg)

*Figure 1.6s Sigma (σ) bond framework of Ethyne and two pi (π) binds of Ethyne*

> 图1.6 乙炔的σ键骨架及两个π键

# **Image Descriptions**

> 图片描述

**Table 1.4 image description:** Ethanol's CH3, CH2, and OH are all in a sp<sup>3</sup> tetrahedral shape. Acetic acid's CH3, and OH are in a sp<sup>3</sup> tetrahedral shape and CO is in a sp<sup>2</sup> trigonal planar. Lastly, ethanenitrile's (acetonitrile) CH<sup>3</sup> in a sp<sup>3</sup> tetrahedral shape, and CN is in a sp linear shape. [Return to Table 1.4]

> 表1.4 图像描述：乙醇中的CH₃、CH₂和OH基团均处于sp³杂化形成的四面体结构中。乙酸中的CH₃和OH基团也处于sp³杂化形成的四面体结构中，而羧基中的C=O则处于sp²杂化形成的三角平面结构中。最后，乙腈（丙腈）中的CH₃处于sp³杂化形成的四面体结构中，而氰基（CN）则处于sp杂化形成的直线型结构中。[返回表1.4]

**1.2**

> 1.2

• Identify the following bond is "polar" or "non-polar"?

> • 以下哪种键是“极性”还是“非极性”？

C-C: non-polar C-H : non-polar (very close electronegativity for C and H)

B-F : polar. O-O : non-polar C=N : polar

> B-F：极性；O-O：非极性；C=N：极性

• Rank the following bonds in the order of increasing bonding polarity: C—S, C—O, C—F (referring to the trend of EN, no need to use the exact EN values).

> • 请按键合极性由小到大的顺序排列以下键：C—S、C—O、C—F（只需说明电负性（EN）的变化趋势，无需使用具体的EN值）。

bonding polarity: C—S < C—O < C—F

- **1.4** Why following structure is not the best way to show the Lewis structure of CO2?

# CHAPTER 2 FUNDAMENTAL OF ORGANIC STRUCTURES

> 第二章 有机结构基础

In this chapter we will talk about the fundamental structural features of organic compounds, the categorization and drawing of organic structures, functional groups and nomenclatures.

> 在本章中，我们将讨论有机化合物的基本结构特征、有机结构的分类与表示方法、官能团及命名规则。

### 0.1 **Organic Compounds Overview**

> 0.1 有机化合物概述

Organic compounds are compounds that contain the **carbon** element. The simplest organic compound is a **hydrocarbon**, which is a compound containing only the elements carbon and hydrogen. Hydrocarbons are composed of several sub-categories: alkane, alkene, alkyne and aromatic, depending on the type of carbon-carbon bonds involved.

> 有机化合物是指含有碳元素的化合物。最简单的有机化合物是烃类，它仅由碳和氢两种元素组成。烃类根据碳碳键的类型，可分为若干子类：烷烃、烯烃、炔烃和芳香烃。

Hydrocarbons can be in chains (straight-chain or branched-chain) or rings. The hydrocarbon chain and ring form the "carbon **backbone**" of organic compounds**,** and functional groups connected to the backbone provide the great diversity organic structures. **Functional groups** are common and specific arrangements of atoms, usually heteroatoms (atoms other than carbon and hydrogen) like N, O, Cl, that show specific and relatively high reactivities. Knowledge about the common functional groups in this Chapter will prepare us for the discussions of organic reactions later.

> 烃类可以是链状的（直链或支链）或环状的。烃类链和环构成了有机化合物的“碳骨架”，而连接在骨架上的官能团则赋予了有机化合物巨大的结构多样性。官能团是常见且特定的原子排列方式，通常包含异原子（除碳和氢以外的原子），如氮（N）、氧（O）、氯（Cl）等，这些原子表现出特定且相对较高的反应活性。了解本章中常见的官能团知识，将为我们后续讨论有机反应奠定基础。

#### 0.1.1 **Hydrocarbons:**

> 0.1.1 烃类化合物：

- **Alkane and cycloalkane**: contains only C-C (single) bonds
- **Alkene and cycloalkene**: contains one or more C=C (double) bonds
- **Alkyne**: contains one or more C≡C (triple) bonds
- **Aromatic**: contains benzene ring and its derivative

> 烷烃和环烷烃：仅含有C-C（单键）  
烯烃和环烯烃：含有一个或多个C=C（双键）  
炔烃：含有一个或多个C≡C（三键）  
芳香烃：含有苯环及其衍生物

Alkene, alkyne and aromatic rings are hydrocarbon functional groups because of the presence of multiple bonds, even without heteroatoms.

> 烯烃、炔烃和芳香环都是由于存在多重键而属于碳氢化合物的官能团，即使没有杂原子。

#### 0.1.2 **Functional Groups involving heteroatoms** (see details in **Table 2.2, section 2.3**):

> 0.1.2 含杂原子的官能团（详见第2.3节表2.2）：

• Alkyl halides (haloalkanes), alcohol, ether, nitrile, nitro, amine, aldehyde, ketone, carboxylic acid, ester, amide, anhydride

> • 卤代烷（卤代烃）、醇、醚、腈、硝基化合物、胺、醛、酮、羧酸、酯、酰胺、酸酐

# 2.1 Structures of Alkenes

> 2.1 烯烃的结构

#### 0.1.1 **2.1.1 Structures and Different Structure Formulas**
