- For the acid-base reaction between C=O group and the proton, the arrow starts from the electron pair on O, and points to the H<sup>+</sup> that is receiving the electron pair. A new O-H bond is formed as a result of this electron pair movement.
- In this acid-base reaction, ketone is protonated by H<sup>+</sup> , so this reaction can also be called the "**protonation of ketone**".
- The product of the protonation is called an "oxonium ion", which is stabilized with another resonance structure, carbocation.

> 在羰基（C=O）与质子之间的酸碱反应中，箭头起始于氧原子上的电子对，并指向接受该电子对的H⁺。由于电子对的转移，形成了一个新的O-H键。  
在此酸碱反应中，酮被H⁺质子化，因此该反应也可以称为“酮的质子化”。  
质子化产物称为“氧鎓离子”，它通过另一种共振结构——碳正离子而得到稳定。

◦ Alkene (C=C): Although there are no lone pair electrons in the C=C bond of alkene, the π electrons of the C=C double bond are able to accept proton and act as base. For example:

> ◦ 烯烃（C=C）：虽然烯烃中C=C键没有孤对电子，但C=C双键的π电子能够接受质子并表现出碱性。例如：

$$H_2C$$
  $CH_2$   $H_2$   $H_2C$   $CH_2$  Alkene is base, carbocation the  $\pi$  electrons accept the  $H^+$

> 烯烃是碱，碳正离子接受电子。

#### 0.3.1 *Example: Organic acid and base reaction*

> 0.3.1 示例：有机酸与碱的反应

Predict and draw the products of following reaction and use curved arrow to show the mechanism.

> 预测并画出以下反应的产物，并用带箭头的曲线表示反应机理。

*Approach*: If H<sup>+</sup> is the acid as in previous examples, it is rather easy to predict how the reaction will proceed. However, if there is no obvious acid (or base) as in this example, how do you determine which is the acid, and which is the base?

> 方法：如果 H⁺ 是酸，如前所述的例子，那么很容易预测反应的进行方式。然而，如果像本例这样没有明显的酸（或碱），你该如何判断哪一个是酸，哪一个是碱？

Methanol CH3OH is neutral, and the other reactant, NH2 – , is a negatively charged amide. The amide with a negative charge has higher electron density than the neutral methanol, therefore amide NH2 – should act as base, and CH3OH is the acid that donates H<sup>+</sup> .

> 甲醇（CH₃OH）呈中性，而另一个反应物NH₂⁻则是一个带负电的酰胺离子。带负电的酰胺具有比中性甲醇更高的电子密度，因此酰胺NH₂⁻应作为碱，而甲醇则是提供H⁺的酸。

#### 0.3.2 **Solution:**

> 0.3.2 解法：

$$CH_3 - \ddot{\ddot{O}} - \dot{\ddot{H}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} = CH_3 - \ddot{\ddot{O}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \dot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \ddot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \ddot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \ddot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \ddot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \ddot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - \ddot{\ddot{N}} + \ddot{\ddot{N}} - Answers to Practice Questions Chapter 3

> 第三章练习题答案

# 3.3 pKa of Organic Acids and Application of pKa to Predict Acid-Base Reaction Outcome

> 3.3 有机酸的pKa值及pKa在预测酸碱反应结果中的应用

As we mentioned before, all organic compounds could be acids, because they all have hydrogen atoms that could potentially be donated. Most organic acids are weak acids with a small *K*a. For example, acetic acid CH3COOH has a *K*a of 1.8×10-5. Lots of other organic acids are even weaker than acetic acid, and it is this weak acidity that makes it difficult to realize that some organic compounds are actually acids.

> 正如我们之前所提到的，所有有机化合物都可能具有酸性，因为它们都含有可以被捐赠的氢原子。大多数有机酸都是弱酸，其解离常数（Ka）较小。例如，乙酸（CH₃COOH）的Ka值为1.8×10⁻⁵。许多其他有机酸甚至比乙酸还要弱，正是这种弱酸性使得人们难以认识到某些有机化合物实际上具有酸性。

However, this weak acidity is very important in Organic Chemistry. Since it is not that very convenient to say or to remember *<sup>K</sup>*<sup>a</sup> values like 1.8×10-5 , **p***K***a** is used more often in Organic Chemistry to refer to the relative acidity of different acids. The definition of p*K*a is:

> 然而，这种弱酸性在有机化学中却非常重要。由于像 1.8×10⁻⁵ 这样的 Ka 值不太方便记忆或表述，因此在有机化学中更常用 pKa 来表示不同酸的相对酸性。pKa 的定义是：

$$pK_a = -logK_a$$

> 

**The smaller the p***K***a value, the larger the** *K***a, and the stronger the acidity is.**

> pKa 值越小，Ka 值越大，酸性越强。

The p*K*a of most organic acids range between 5~60. While it is impossible to know the p*K*a of every organic compound, it is very useful to understand the p*K*a (and acidity) based on the functional groups involved, because the same functional groups usually have similar p*K*as. The approximate ranges of p*K*a values for seven major functional groups are listed in **Table 3.1**, which serves as a very valuable starting point for us to predict and understand the acidity of any organic molecule. The strongest organic acid listed here is carboxylic acid, with a p*K*a of about 5; the weakest organic acids are the alkanes with p*K*a values of over 50. Since approximate ranges of p*K*a values are listed in the table, the exact p*K*a value of a group varies for different compounds because of the structural differences. Fortunately however, it is usually not necessary to know the exact p*K*a values for most cases in organic chemistry, and the approximate range is good enough.

> 大多数有机酸的pKa值范围在5~60之间。虽然不可能知道每种有机化合物的pKa值，但了解与特定官能团相关的pKa值（以及酸性）是非常有用的，因为相同类型的官能团通常具有相似的pKa值。表3.1列出了七种主要官能团的pKa值的大致范围，这为我们预测和理解任何有机分子的酸性提供了一个非常有价值的起点。表中列出的最强有机酸是羧酸，其pKa值约为5；而最弱的有机酸是烷烃，其pKa值超过50。由于表中列出的是pKa值的大致范围，因此不同化合物中同一官能团的精确pKa值可能会因结构差异而有所不同。不过幸运的是，在大多数有机化学情况下，通常并不需要精确知道pKa值，pKa值的大致范围已经足够使用。

| Acidic Hydrogen in Functional Groups                       | Approximate Range of pKa                    | Conjugate Base                                                                                         |
|------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| Carboxylic acid  O    R  OH                                | ~5                                          | O<br>  <br> C<br> O                                                                                    |
| Alcohol R—OH                                               | ~16<br>(H <sub>2</sub> O: ~16; Phenol: ~10) | R—0 <sup>⊖</sup>                                                                                       |
| Aldehyde/Ketone  O  II  II  R  C  H  R  C  CH <sub>3</sub> | ~16 to ~20                                  | $ \begin{array}{cccc} O & O \\ \parallel & & \parallel \\ C & \Theta & C \\ R & C & CH_2 \end{array} $ |
| Alkyne<br>R—C≡C—H                                          | ~25                                         | R—c≡c <sup>⊖</sup>                                                                                     |
| Amine<br>R——NH <sub>2</sub>                                | ~35 to 40 (NH₃: ~38)                        | R—NH <sup>⊖</sup>                                                                                      |
| Alkene<br>R—CH=CH <sub>2</sub>                             | ~45                                         | R—CH≡CH                                                                                                |
| Alkane<br>RCH <sub>3</sub>                                 | >50                                         | ⊖<br>R—CH <sub>2</sub>                                                                                 |

> | 功能团中的酸性氢 | pKa 的近似范围 | 共轭碱 |
|------------------|----------------|--------|
| 羧酸 R—COOH     | ~5             | R—COO⁻ |
| 醇 R—OH         | ~16<br>(H₂O: ~16; 苯酚: ~10) | R—O⁻ |
| 醛/酮 R—C(=O)—H 或 R—C(=O)—CH₃ | ~16 至 ~20 | — |
| 炔烃 R—C≡C—H    | ~25           | R—C≡C⁻ |
| 胺 R—NH₂        | ~35 至 40<br>(NH₃: ~38) | R—NH⁻ |
| 烯烃 R—CH=CH₂   | ~45           | R—CH≡CH |
| 烷烃 R—CH₃      | >50           | R—CH₂⁻ |

*Table 3.1: Approximate ranges of pKa values for common organic functional groups*

> 表3.1：常见有机官能团的pKa值近似范围

### 0.1 *Notes for the pK***a** *values in Table 3.1:*

> 0.1 表3.1中pKa值的说明：

• Acidity is the ability of a compound to donate H<sup>+</sup> , so when we talk about the acidity (*K*a and p*K*a) of an organic compound, it must be about a specific **H atom** (highlighted blue in the table). For different H atoms in the same compound, the acidity and p*K*a are different. As for the example of methanol:

> • 酸性是指化合物释放 H⁺ 的能力，因此当我们讨论有机化合物的酸性（Ka 和 pKa）时，必须是指特定的氢原子（表中用蓝色突出显示）。同一种化合物中不同的氢原子，其酸性和 pKa 值是不同的。例如甲醇的情况：

![](_page_101_Figure_0.jpeg)

*Figure 3.3a Methanol*

> 图3.3a 甲醇

- It is very useful to memorize the approximate ranges of p*K*a listed in Table 3.1.
- The acidity of the functional groups in the table *decreases* from top to the bottom, and the basicity of the conjugate bases in the last column *increases* from top to bottom, because *the stronger the acid, the weaker the conjugate base is.*

> 记住表3.1中列出的pKa近似范围是非常有帮助的。  
表中功能团的酸性从上到下逐渐减弱，而最后一列共轭碱的碱性则从上到下逐渐增强，因为酸性越强，其共轭碱的碱性就越弱。

### 0.2 **Predict the Outcome of Organic Acid-Base Reaction — Use p***K***a as Criterion**

> 0.2 预测有机酸碱反应的产物——以pKa值为判断依据

With the knowledge of acidity and p*K*a, we are now ready to see how to apply this information to the understanding of organic reactions from an acid-base perspective.

> 掌握了酸性和pKa的相关知识后，我们现在可以运用这些信息，从酸碱的角度来理解有机反应。

The following reaction is an **example** in **Section 3.2.** If you take a closer look at the reactants and products, you will find that the "product" side also contains an acid (ammonia NH3), and a base (methoxide CH3O – ). Now the question is, how can we be so sure that the reaction proceeds to the "product" side as written? The question can also be asked in a different way: if equilibrium is established for the reaction mixture, which side will the position of the equilibrium predominantly favour? Left or right?

> 以下反应是第3.2节中的一个例子。如果你仔细观察反应物和生成物，会发现“产物”一侧也含有酸（氨 NH₃）和碱（甲氧基 CH₃O⁻）。现在的问题是，我们如何能如此确定该反应按照所写的方向进行？这个问题还可以换一种方式来问：如果反应混合物达到平衡，平衡位置会更倾向于哪一侧？左边还是右边？

+    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +    +

*Figure 3.3b Acid-Base Reaction*

> 图3.3b 酸碱反应

To answer that question, we will learn about a general rule for acid-base reaction: **Acid-base reactions always favour the formation of the** *weaker* **acid and the** *weaker* **base.** This is because the equilibrium always favours the formation of more stable products, and weaker acids and bases are more stable than stronger ones.

> 要回答这个问题，我们将学习一条酸碱反应的一般规律：酸碱反应总是有利于较弱酸和较弱碱的生成。这是因为平衡总是倾向于生成更稳定的产物，而较弱的酸和碱比强酸和强碱更加稳定。

![](_page_102_Figure_0.jpeg)

*Figure 3.3c Smaller pKa and larger pKa*

> 图3.3c 较小的pKa值和较大的pKa值

With p*K*a values available at hand, the relative acidity of reactants *vs* products can be compared by comparing their p*K*a values, and **the reaction will proceed to the side of the acid with a** *larger pK***a** (larger p*K*a means smaller *K*a, therefore weaker acid).

> 只要手头有各物质的pKa值，就可以通过比较反应物与产物的pKa值，判断它们的相对酸性强弱。反应将向具有较大pKa值的酸一侧进行（较大的pKa值意味着较小的Ka值，因此酸性较弱）。

So for this reaction, the p*K*a check indicates that ammonia NH3 is a weaker acid than methanol CH3OH, so the reaction does proceed to the right side with CH3O – and NH3 as the major products.

> 因此，对于这个反应，pKa 值的比较表明，氨（NH3）比甲醇（CH3OH）酸性更弱，因此反应向右进行，主要生成 CH3O⁻ 和 NH3。

![](_page_102_Figure_4.jpeg)

*Figure 3.3d Which direction does the reaction go?*

> 图3.3d 反应向哪个方向进行？

**Notes: Only comparing between acids is good enough for this purpose,** because if CH3OH is stronger than NH3, then the conjugate base CH3O – must be weaker than the other base NH<sup>2</sup> – .

> 注：仅比较酸的强度就足以达到此目的，因为如果 CH₃OH 比 NH₃ 酸性强，那么其共轭碱 CH₃O⁻ 必定比另一种碱 NH₂⁻ 更弱。

*Examples*

> 示例

Show the products of the following reactions and predict the predominant side of the equilibrium.

> 写出下列反应的产物，并预测平衡的主要方向。

#### 0.2.1 **Reaction 1**

> 0.2.1 反应 1

### 0.3 **Reaction 2**

> 0.3 反应 2

### 0.4 **Solutions:**

> 0.4 解法：

### 0.5 **Reaction 1**

> 0.5 反应 1

H—C
$$\equiv$$
C—H +  $\stackrel{\Theta}{:}$ NH<sub>2</sub>  $\Longrightarrow$  H—C $\equiv$ C: $\stackrel{\Theta}{:}$  + NH<sub>3</sub>
 $pKa: \sim 25$ 
 $pKa: \sim 38$ 
 $pKa: \sim 38$ 
 $pKa: \sim 38$ 
 $pKa: \sim 38$

C—H + NH₂   H—C  C:   + NH₃

> 0.5.1 反应

H—C
$$\equiv$$
C—H +  $\stackrel{\Theta}{:}$ OH  $\Longrightarrow$  H—C $\equiv$ C: $\stackrel{\Theta}{=}$  + H<sub>2</sub>O

weaker acid stronger acid

> H—C  
C—H +   OH    H—C  C:   + H<sub>2</sub>O   
      
较弱的酸  强酸

Are there any practical applications for such a prediction? Yes! Let's compare the two reactions in the exercises above. Reaction 1 indicates that if ethyne (HC≡CH) and amide (NH2 – ) are mixed together, the reaction **does** proceed to the products side, meaning **HC≡CH could be deprotonated by amide NH2 –** . However, if HC≡CH and hydroxide OH – are mixed together as shown in **reaction 2**, no reaction occurs, or we can say that **HC≡CH can not be deprotonated by OH –** because OH – is not strong enough! So if you are working in the lab and have the option of choosing between NH2 – or OH – to deprotonate HC≡CH, you now know which one to choose.

> 这样的预测有没有实际应用呢？是的！让我们比较上面练习中的两个反应。反应1表明，如果乙炔（HC≡CH）与酰胺（NH₂⁻）混合，反应确实会向产物方向进行，也就是说，HC≡CH 可以被酰胺 NH₂⁻ 去质子化。然而，如反应2所示，如果将 HC≡CH 与氢氧根 OH⁻ 混合，则不会发生反应，或者说 HC≡3CH 不能被 OH⁻ 去质子化，因为 OH⁻ 的碱性不够强！因此，如果你在实验室中可以选择使用 NH₂⁻ 或 OH⁻ 来对 HC≡CH 进行去质子化，现在你已经知道应该选择哪一个了。

The idea that OH – is not a strong enough base may bother you a lot, since it conflicts with the "common knowledge" that we learned in General Chemistry, where OH – is a strong base. Generally speaking, OH – is a pretty strong base; however, it is just barely not strong enough to deprotonate HC≡CH, which is a very weak acid, with a p*K*a of about ~25. Since HC≡CH is much weaker than the "weak acids" we learned in General Chemistry, a much stronger base, like NH2 – , is required to deprotonate it.

> OH⁻ 不足以作为强碱这一观点可能会让你感到困惑，因为它与我们在普通化学中学到的“常识”相冲突，即 OH⁻ 是一种强碱。一般来说，OH⁻ 确实是一种很强的碱；然而，它仅略逊一筹，无法将 HC≡CH（乙炔）这种非常弱的酸（pKa 约为 ~25）质子去除。由于 HC≡CH 的酸性远弱于我们在普通化学中学习的“弱酸”，因此需要一种更强的碱，如 NH₂⁻，才能将其质子去除。

# 3.4 Structural Effects on Acidity and Basicity

> 3.4 结构对酸碱性的影响

We have learned that different functional groups have different strengths in terms of acidity. In this section, we will gain an understanding of the fundamental reasons behind this, which is *why* one group is more acidic than the other one. Many of the concepts that we will learn here will continue to apply throughout this course as we tackle many other organic topics.

> 我们已经了解到，不同的官能团在酸性强弱方面存在差异。在本节中，我们将深入了解导致这种差异的根本原因，即为什么某一官能团比另一官能团更具酸性。我们在这里所学的许多概念将在整个课程中继续应用，帮助我们解决许多其他有机化学相关的问题。

#### 0.1.1 **3.4.1 Element Effect**

> 0.1.1 3.4.1 元素效应

### 0.2 **A. Periodic Trend: Electronegativity**

> 0.2 A. 周期性变化：电负性

The element effect is about the *individual atom that connects with the* **hydrogen** (keep in mind that the acidity is about the ability to donate a certain hydrogen). Let's compare the acidity of hydrogens in ethane, methylamine and ethanol as shown below.

> 元素效应涉及与氢原子相连的单个原子（请注意，酸性是指释放特定氢原子的能力）。让我们比较乙烷、甲胺和乙醇中氢原子的酸性，如下所示。

![](_page_105_Figure_5.jpeg)

A clear trend in the acidity of these compounds is: the acidity increases for the elements from left to right along the second row of the periodic table, C to N, and then to O. This is consistent with the increasing trend of electronegativity along the period from left to right. The connection between electronegativity and acidity can be explained as the atom with a higher electronegativity being able to better accommodate the negative charge of the conjugate base, therefore stabilizing the conjugate base in a better way. Therefore, *the more stable conjugate base, the weaker the conjugate base is, and the stronger the acid is*. For the discussions in this section, the trend in the stability (or basicity) of the conjugate bases often helps to explain the trend of the acidity.

> 这些化合物的酸性呈现出一个清晰的趋势：在元素周期表的第二周期中，从碳（C）到氮（N），再到氧（O），元素的酸性逐渐增强。这与周期表中从左向右电负性逐渐增强的趋势是一致的。电负性与酸性的关系可以这样解释：电负性越高的原子，越能更好地容纳共轭碱的负电荷，从而更有效地稳定共轭碱。因此，共轭碱越稳定，共轭碱就越弱，对应的酸就越强。在本节的讨论中，共轭碱的稳定性（或碱性）趋势常常有助于解释酸性的变化趋势。

The relative acidity of elements in the same period is:

> 同一周期中元素的相对酸性强弱为：

**For elements in the same period, the more electronegative an atom, the stronger the acid is; the acidity increases from left to right across the period.**

> 同一周期中，原子的电负性越强，其对应的酸性越强；同周期中，酸性从左向右逐渐增强。

### 0.3 **B. Group (vertical) Trend: Size of the atom**

> 0.3 B. 族（垂直）趋势：原子的大小

When moving vertically within a given group on the periodic table, the trend is that acidity increases from top to bottom. This can be illustrated with the haloacids HX and halides as shown below: the acidity of HX increases from top to bottom, and the basicity of the conjugate bases X– decreases from top to bottom.

> 在元素周期表中，同一主族内垂直移动时，酸性呈现从上到下逐渐增强的趋势。这一趋势可以通过卤代酸HX和卤化物的示例来说明：HX的酸性从上到下增强，而其共轭碱X⁻的碱性则从上到下减弱。

![](_page_106_Figure_4.jpeg)

The acidity of the H in thiol SH group is also stronger than the corresponding alcohol OH group, following the same trend. For example, the p*K*a of CH3CH2SH is ~10, which is much more acidic than ethanol CH3CH2OH with a p*K*a of ~16.

> 巯基（–SH）中的氢（H）的酸性也强于相应的羟基（–OH） group，遵循相同的趋势。例如，乙硫醇（CH₃CH₂SH）的pKa值约为10，其酸性远强于乙醇（CH₃CH₂OH）的pKa值约为16。

In order to make sense of this trend, we will once again consider the stability of the conjugate bases. When moving vertically in the same group of the periodic table, the *size* of the atom overrides its electronegativity with regards to basicity. The atomic radius of iodine is approximately twice that of fluorine, so in an iodide ion, the negative charge is spread out over a significantly larger volume, so I– is more stable and less basic, making HI more acidic.

> 为了理解这一趋势，我们再次考虑共轭碱的稳定性。在元素周期表的同一主族中，随着原子序数的增加，原子的大小对其碱性的影响超过了其电负性。碘原子的原子半径大约是氟原子的两倍，因此在碘离子（I⁻）中，负电荷分布在更大的体积上，使得I⁻更加稳定，碱性更弱，从而使HI表现出更强的酸性。

![](_page_106_Picture_7.jpeg)

*Figure 3.4a Stability of fluorine and iodide ion*

> 图3.4a 氟离子与碘离子的稳定性

The relative acidity of elements in the same group is:

> 同一主族元素的相对酸性强弱为：

**For elements in the same group, the larger the size of the atom, the stronger the acid is; the acidity increases from top to bottom along the group.**

> 同一主族中的元素，原子半径越大，其对应的酸性越强；同主族中酸性随原子序数的增加，自上而下逐渐增强。

### 0.4 **3.4.2. Resonance Effect**

> 0.4 3.4.2 共轭效应

The resonance effect accounts for the acidity difference between ethanol and acetic acid. For both ethanol and acetic acid, the hydrogen is bonded with the oxygen atom, so there is no element effect that matters. However, the p*K*a values (and the acidity) of ethanol and acetic acid are very different. What makes a carboxylic acid so much more acidic than an alcohol? As stated before, we begin by considering the stability of the conjugate bases, remembering that a more stable (weaker) conjugate base corresponds to a stronger acid.

> 共振效应可以解释乙醇与乙酸之间酸性强弱的差异。对于乙醇和乙酸来说，氢原子都是与氧原子相连的，因此不存在影响酸性的元素效应。然而，乙醇和乙酸的pKa值（以及酸性）却存在显著差异。是什么使得羧酸的酸性比醇类强得多呢？正如之前所述，我们首先应考虑共轭碱的稳定性，记住：共轭碱越稳定（即越弱），对应的酸就越强。

![](_page_107_Figure_3.jpeg)

For acetate, the conjugate base of acetic acid, two resonance contributors can be drawn and therefore the negative charge can be delocalized (shared) over two oxygen atoms. However, no other resonance contributor is available in the ethoxide ion, the conjugate base of ethanol, so the negative charge is localized on the oxygen atom. As we have learned in **section 1.3**, **the species that has more resonance contributors gains stability**, therefore acetate is more stable than ethoxide, and is weaker as the base, so acetic acid is a stronger acid than ethanol.

> 对于乙酸根离子（乙酸的共轭碱），可以画出两种共振结构，因此负电荷可以在这两个氧原子之间离域（共享）。然而，在乙醇的共轭碱——乙氧基离子中，没有其他共振结构可供贡献，因此负电荷局限于一个氧原子上。正如我们在第1.3节所学，具有更多共振结构的物种更加稳定，因此乙酸根比乙氧基离子更稳定，作为碱的能力也更弱，所以乙酸比乙醇的酸性强。

The charge delocalization by resonance has a very powerful effect on the reactivity of organic molecules, enough to account for the big difference of over 10 p*K*a units between ethanol and acetic acid. Because p*K*a = –log *K*a, that means that there is a factor of about 10<sup>10</sup> between the K<sup>a</sup> values for the two molecules!

> 共振引起的电荷离域对有机分子的反应性具有非常显著的影响，足以解释乙醇与乙酸之间超过10个pKa单位的差异。由于pKa = –log Ka，这意味着这两种分子的Ka值之间相差约10<sup>10</sup>倍！

The p*K*a of the OH group in alcohol is about 15, however OH in phenol (OH group connected on a benzene ring) has a pKa of about 10, which is much stronger in acidity than other alcohols. Explain the difference.

> 醇中羟基（OH）的pKa值约为15，然而酚羟基（连接在苯环上的羟基）的pKa值约为10，其酸性比其他醇强得多。请解释这种差异。

$$\begin{array}{c|ccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccc$$

> 

#### 0.4.1 **Solution**:

> 0.4.1 解法：

The difference can be explained by the resonance effect. There is no resonance effect on the conjugate base of ethanol, as mentioned before. However, the conjugate base of phenol is stabilized by the resonance effect with four more resonance contributors, and the negative is delocalized on the benzene ring, so the conjugate base of phenol is much more stable and is a weaker base. Therefore phenol is much more acidic than other alcohols.

> 这种差异可以通过共轭效应来解释。如前所述，乙醇的共轭碱没有共轭效应。然而，酚的共轭碱由于共轭效应有四个额外的共振结构，负电荷被分散到苯环上，因此酚的共轭碱更加稳定，是一个更弱的碱。因此，酚的酸性比其他醇强得多。

$$\begin{array}{c} \text{phenol} \\ \text{pK}_{a} \sim 10 \end{array}$$
 conjugate bases: 
$$\begin{array}{c} \vdots \\ \vdots \\ \vdots \\ \vdots \\ \vdots \\ \vdots \\ \vdots \\ \vdots \\ \vdots \\ \vdots$$

> 共轭碱：

#### 0.4.2 *Exercises 3.2*

> 0.4.2 习题 3.2

- Practice drawing the resonance structures of the conjugate base of phenol by yourself!
- It is because of the special acidity of phenol (and other aromatic alcohols), that NaOH can be used to deprotonate phenol effectively, but not to normal alcohols, like ethanol. Show the reaction equations of

> 请自行练习绘制苯酚共轭碱的共振结构！  
这是因为苯酚（以及其他芳香醇）具有特殊的酸性，因此可以用 NaOH 有效脱去苯酚的质子，而不能用于普通的醇，如乙醇。请写出相应的反应方程式。

these reactions and explain the difference by applying the p*K*a values.

> 这些反应并解释它们的差异，通过应用pKa值来说明。

Answers to Practice Questions Chapter 3

> 第三章练习题答案

#### 0.4.3 **3.4.3 Inductive Effect**

> 0.4.3 3.4.3 诱导效应

Let's compare the p*K*a values of acetic acid and its mono-, di-, and tri-chlorinated derivatives:

> 让我们比较乙酸及其一氯代、二氯代和三氯代衍生物的pKa值：

$$\begin{array}{c|ccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccc$$

> 

*Figure 3.4b Acetic acid and its mono-, di-, and tri-chlorinated derivatives*

> 图3.4b 乙酸及其一氯、二氯和三氯取代衍生物

The presence of the chlorine atoms clearly increases the acidity of the carboxylic acid group, and the argument here apparently does not have to do with the element effect. The resonance effect does not have to do with it either, because no additional resonance contributors can be drawn for the chlorinated molecules. Rather, the explanation for this phenomenon involves something called the **inductive effect**. A chlorine atom is more electronegative than hydrogen, and is thus able to 'induce', or 'pull' electron density towards itself via σ bonds in between, and therefore helps to spread out the electron density of the conjugate base, the carboxylate, and stabilize it. The chlorine substituent can be referred to as an **electron-withdrawing group** because of the inductive effect.

> 氯原子的存在显然增强了羧酸基团的酸性，而此处的解释显然与元素效应无关。共振效应也与此无关，因为氯化物分子无法再引入额外的共振结构。相反，这种现象的解释涉及一种称为诱导效应（inductive effect）的因素。氯原子的电负性比氢原子强，因此能够通过σ键“诱导”或“拉取”电子云密度向自身聚集，从而有助于分散羧酸根（共轭碱）的电子密度，使其更加稳定。由于诱导效应，氯取代基可以被称为一个吸电子基团。

**The inductive effect** is the charge dispersal effect of electronegative atoms through σ bonds. The inductive effect is addictive; more chlorine atoms have an overall stronger effect, which explains the increasing acidity from mono, to di-, to tri-chlorinated acetic acid. The following diagram shows the inductive effect of trichloro acetate as an example.

> 诱导效应是指通过σ键，电负性原子对电荷的分散作用。诱导效应具有叠加性；氯原子越多，整体效应越强，这解释了单氯乙酸、二氯乙酸和三氯乙酸酸性依次增强的现象。下图以三氯乙酸的诱导效应为例进行了说明。

*Figure 3.4c Trichloro acetate was stabilized by inductive effect*

> 图3.4c 三氯乙酸因诱导效应而稳定

Because the inductive effect depends on electronegativity, fluorine substituents have a stronger inductive effect than chlorine substituents, making trifluoroacetic acid (TFA) a very strong organic acid.

> 由于诱导效应取决于电负性，氟取代基的诱导效应强于氯取代基，因此三氟乙酸（TFA）是一种非常强的有机酸。

$$pK_a = 0.64$$
  $pK_a = -0.2$

> 

*Figure 3.4d trichloroacetic acid (pKa = 0.64) and trifluoroacetic acid (TfOH) (pKa = -0.25)*

> 图3.4d 三氯乙酸（pKa = 0.64）和三氟乙酸（TfOH）（pKa = -0.25）

In addition, because the inductive effect takes place through covalent bonds, its influence decreases significantly with distance — thus a chlorine that is two carbons away from a carboxylic acid group has a weaker effect compared to a chlorine just one carbon away.

> 此外，由于诱导效应是通过共价键传递的，因此其影响会随着距离的增加而显著减弱——因此，与羧酸基团相隔两个碳原子的氯原子，其效应会比仅相隔一个碳原子的氯原子弱得多。

#### 0.4.4 **3.4.4 Hybridization Effect**

> 0.4.4 3.4.4 杂化效应

To introduce the hybridization effect, we will take a look at the acidity difference between alkane, alkene and alkyne.

> 为了介绍杂化效应，我们将观察烷烃、烯烃和炔烃之间酸性强弱的差异。

![](_page_111_Figure_1.jpeg)

The hydrogen atom is bonded with a carbon atom in all the three functional groups, so the element effect does not invoke. Also considering about the conjugate base of each, there is no extra resonance contributor possible.

> 在所有这三个官能团中，氢原子均与碳原子相连，因此元素效应不会起作用。同时考虑到每个基团的共轭碱，也不存在其他可能的共振贡献体。

The key difference between the conjugate base anions is the hybridization of the carbon atom, that is sp<sup>3</sup> , sp<sup>2</sup> and sp respectively for alkane, alkene and alkyne. Different hybridizations leads to different *s* **character**, that is the percent of *s* orbitals out of the total amount of orbitals. The sp<sup>3</sup> hybridization means 25% *s* character (one *s* and three *p* orbitals, so *s* character is 1/4 = 25%), sp<sup>2</sup> hybridization has 33.3% *s* character, and the number is 50% for sp hybridization. Electrons of 2*s* orbitals are in the lower energy level than those of 2*p* orbitals because 2*s* is much closer to the nucleus. So for the anion with more *s* character, the electrons are closer to the nucleus and experience stronger attraction, therefore the anion has lower energy and is more stable.

> 共轭碱阴离子之间的主要区别在于碳原子的杂化方式。具体而言，烷烃、烯烃和炔烃的共轭碱阴离子中，碳原子的杂化方式分别为 sp³、sp² 和 sp。不同的杂化方式会导致不同的 s 成分，即 s 轨道在总轨道中的百分比。sp³ 杂化意味着 25% 的 s 成分（一个 s 轨道和三个 p 轨道，因此 s 成分是 1/4 = 25%）；sp² 杂化具有 33.3% 的 s 成分；而 sp 杂化则具有 50% 的 s 成分。由于 2s 轨道比 2p 轨道更靠近原子核，因此 2s 轨道中的电子处于更低的能量水平。因此，对于具有更多 s 成分的阴离子，其电子更靠近原子核，受到更强的吸引，因此该阴离子能量更低，更加稳定。

The relative stability of the three anions (conjugate bases) can also be illustrated by the electrostatic potential map, in which the lighter color (less red) indicate less electron-density of the anion, and the higher stability.

> 三种阴离子（共轭碱）的相对稳定性也可以通过静电势图来说明，在该图中，颜色较浅（红色较不明显）表示该阴离子的电子密度较低，稳定性更高。

![](_page_111_Figure_5.jpeg)

*Figure 3.4e Electrostatic potential map of the conj. bases*

> 图3.4e 共轭碱的静电势图

This can also be stated in a more general way that more *s* character in the hybrid orbitals make the atom more electronegative. *For the same atom, an sp hybridized atom is more electronegative than sp***<sup>2</sup>** *hybridized atom, which is more electronegative than sp***<sup>3</sup>** *hybridized atom.*

> 这也可以更一般地表述为：杂化轨道中s成分越多，原子的电负性就越强。对于同一种原子，sp杂化的原子比sp<sup>2</sup>杂化的原子更具电负性，而sp<sup>2</sup>杂化的原子又比sp<sup>3</sup>杂化的原子更具电负性。

# 3.5 Lewis Acids and Lewis Bases

> 3.5 路易斯酸与路易斯碱

The Brønsted-Lowry definition works well for the reactions we learned so far, however it also limits the scope of acidbase reactions in a way where the proton H<sup>+</sup> must be involved. Lewis acids and Lewis bases are defined in a more inclusive way that was first introduced by G. N. Lewis in 1923.

> 布朗斯特-劳里（Brønsted-Lowry）定义对于目前为止我们学习的反应具有很好的适用性，但它在一定程度上限制了酸碱反应的范围，即要求反应中必须涉及质子 H⁺。而路易斯酸和路易斯碱的定义更为广泛，这一概念最早由 G. N. 路易斯于 1923 年提出。

**Lewis Acid**: a species that can accept an electron pair; **Lewis Base**: a species that can donate an electron pair.

> 路易斯酸：能够接受电子对的物种；路易斯碱：能够提供电子对的物种。

All Brønsted-Lowry acids and bases fit into the Lewis definition, because the proton transfer process is essentially the reaction where the base uses its electron pair to accept a proton, as indicated by the mechanism arrow that we learned earlier. Therefore in the following reaction, the BL acid, H<sup>+</sup> , is also the Lewis acid, and BL base, NH3, also fits to the definition of the Lewis base.

> 所有的布朗斯特-劳里（Brønsted-Lowry，简称BL）酸和碱都符合路易斯（Lewis）定义，因为质子转移过程本质上就是碱利用其电子对接受质子的反应，正如我们之前所学的反应机理箭头所指示的那样。因此，在以下反应中，BL酸H⁺同时也是路易斯酸，而BL碱NH₃也符合路易斯碱的定义。

![](_page_113_Figure_4.jpeg)

*Figure 3.5a Lewis base & Lewis acid reaction*

> 图3.5a 路易斯碱与路易斯酸反应

However, the Lewis definition is broader and covers more situations. For the following reaction, B(CH3)3 is the Lewis acid because boron has an incomplete octet, and the empty 2p orbital on boron is able to accept electrons. (CH3)3N behaves as the Lewis base with the lone pair electron on N that is able to be donated.

> 然而，路易斯（Lewis）定义的范围更广，可以涵盖更多情况。对于以下反应，B(CH3)3 是路易斯酸，因为硼原子具有不完整的八电子结构，其上的空 2p 轨道能够接受电子。而 (CH3)3N 则作为路易斯碱，其氮原子上的孤对电子能够被提供出来。

![](_page_113_Figure_7.jpeg)

*Figure 3.5b LA-LB adduct*

> 图3.5b LA-LB加合物

The product between Lewis acids and Lewis bases is usually a species that has the acid and base joined together, and the product is called the "LA-LB adduct".

> 路易斯酸与路易斯碱反应生成的产物通常是酸和碱结合在一起的物种，这种产物被称为“LA-LB加合物”。

Other examples of Lewis acids include electron-deficient species, such as H<sup>+</sup> , M<sup>+</sup> , M2+, BH3, BF3, AlCl<sup>3</sup> etc. Lewis bases can be: amine, ether or other species that have lone pair electrons to donate.

> 其他勒沙特列酸（Lewis酸）的例子包括缺电子物种，如 H⁺、M⁺、M²⁺、BH₃、BF₃、AlCl₃ 等。勒沙特列碱（Lewis碱）可以是：胺、醚或其他具有孤对电子可供捐赠的物种。

> 0.1.1 习题 3.3

> 写出下列LA-LB反应的产物：

# CHAPTER 4 CONFORMATIONS OF ALKANES AND CYCLOALKANES

> 第四章 烷烃和环烷烃的构象

The structure and naming of alkanes and cycloalkanes have been discussed in **Chapter 2**. Here we are going to learn another property of alkanes and cycloalkanes that comes from the bond rotation.

> 烷烃和环烷烃的结构与命名已在第2章中讨论过。在这里，我们将学习烷烃和环烷烃的另一个性质，这一性质来源于键的旋转。

# 4.1 Conformation Analysis of Alkanes

> 4.1 烷烃的构象分析

#### 0.1.1 **4.1.1 Conformation**

> 0.1.1 4.1.1 构象

At a molecular level, a property of σ (sigma) bonds in alkane is that the bonds keep on rotating. For the example of ethane (CH3CH3), one methyl (CH3) group is able to rotate around the C-C bond freely without any obstacles.

> 在分子层面，烷烃中σ（西格玛）键的一个特性是，这些键可以持续旋转。以乙烷（CH₃CH₃）为例，一个甲基（CH₃）基团可以围绕C-C键自由旋转，而不会受到任何阻碍。

It is highly recommended that the molecular model is used here to "see" the bond rotation. With a molecular model on hand, you can hold one methyl group steady, and rotate the other methyl group.

> 在此处使用分子模型有助于“看到”键的旋转。手头若有分子模型，你可以固定一个甲基，然后旋转另一个甲基。

The C-C bond is formed by the sp<sup>3</sup> -sp<sup>3</sup> orbitals overlapping and the bond is cylindrically symmetrical, so rotation about the bond can occur easily and the molecule does not seem to change. However, a closer look indicates that the rotation of the C-C bond **does** result in a different spatial arrangement of hydrogen atoms in the molecule, as shown below:

> C-C 键是由 sp³-sp³ 轨道重叠形成的，该键呈圆柱形对称，因此围绕该键的旋转可以很容易地发生，分子似乎没有发生变化。然而，仔细观察可以发现，C-C 键的旋转实际上会导致分子中氢原子的空间排列发生变化，如下图所示：

![](_page_120_Figure_5.jpeg)

*Figure 4.1a Two conformers of ethane in perspective formulas*

> 图4.1a 乙烷的两种构象（透视式）

The different spatial arrangements of the atoms/groups that result from the single bond rotation are called **conformations**. Molecules with different conformations are called **conformational isomers** or **conformers**. The two extreme conformations of ethane coming from the C-C rotation shown above are: the *staggered conformation* with all of the H atoms spread out, and the *eclipsed conformation* with all of the H atoms overlapped.

> 由于单键旋转所导致的原子/基团不同的空间排列称为构型。具有不同构型的分子称为构型异构体或构体。上述所示乙烷因碳-碳单键旋转而产生的两种极端构型分别为：所有氢原子呈分散状态的锯齿形构型，以及所有氢原子重叠的重叠构型。

In the study of conformation, it is convenient to use certain types of structural formulas. The formula used in the drawing above is the **perspective formula** (see **section 2.1.1**) that shows the side-view of the molecule. In perspective formulas, solid and dashed wedges are used to show the spatial arrangement of atoms (or groups) around the sp<sup>3</sup> carbons.

> 在构象的研究中，使用某些类型的结构式会更为方便。上述图中所使用的公式是透视式结构（参见第2.1.1节），它展示了分子的侧视图。在透视式结构中，使用实线和虚线楔形来表示围绕sp³碳原子的原子（或基团）的空间排列。

Another structural formula is the **sawhorse formula** that shows the tilted top-view of the molecule.

> 另一种结构式是锯架式结构式，它展示了分子的倾斜俯视图。

![](_page_121_Figure_0.jpeg)

*Figure 4.1b Two conformers of ethane in sawhorse formulas*

> 图4.1b 乙烷的两种构象（锯架式结构）

The most commonly applied formula in conformation analysis is the **Newman projection** formula.

> 构象分析中最常应用的公式是纽曼投影式。

![](_page_121_Figure_3.jpeg)

*Figure 4.1c Two conformers of ethane in Newman projections*

> 图4.1c 乙烷的两种构象（Newman投影）

#### 0.1.2 **How to draw a Newman projection**

> 0.1.2 如何绘制纽曼投影

To draw a **Newman projection,** we will imagine **viewing** the molecule *from one carbon to the next carbon atom directly along a selected C–C bond*, as shown below, and follow the rules:

> 为了绘制纽曼投影式，我们将想象从一个碳原子直接沿选定的C–C键看向下一个碳原子，如下面所示，并遵循以下规则：

![](_page_121_Picture_7.jpeg)

*Figure 4.1d Viewing of the molecule*

> 图4.1d 分子的观察视角

• The front carbon atom is shown as a point with three other bonds:

> • 前面的碳原子被表示为一个点，带有三个其他键：

![](_page_121_Picture_10.jpeg)

• The rear carbon atom is shown as a circle with three other bonds:

> • 后面的碳原子显示为一个带有三个其他键的圆圈：

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_122_Picture_1.jpeg)

• Put the two carbons together to get the Newman projection of the staggered conformation:

> • 将两个碳原子连在一起，得到锯齿构象的纽曼投影：

![](_page_122_Picture_3.jpeg)

• From the staggered conformation, fix the front carbon in place, and rotate the rear carbon by 60° to get the eclipsed conformation:

> • 从锯齿构象出发，固定前方碳原子的位置，将后方碳原子旋转60°，即可得到重叠构象：

![](_page_122_Picture_5.jpeg)

**Note: In eclipsed conformers,** *the C-H bonds are supposed to be completed overlapped; however, to make the rear groups still visible, the bonds on the rear carbon are intentionally drawn slightly tilted.*

> 注意：在重叠构象中，C-H 键应完全重叠；然而，为了使后方的基团仍然可见，后方碳原子上的键被有意地略微倾斜绘制。

#### 0.1.3 **4.1.2 Conformation Analysis of Ethane**

> 0.1.3 4.1.2 乙烷的构象分析

Next, we will do a conformation analysis of ethane by using the Newman projections. **A conformation analysis** is an investigation of energy differences and relative stabilities of the different conformations of a compound.

> 接下来，我们将使用纽曼投影法对乙烷进行构象分析。构象分析是对化合物不同构象之间的能量差异及其相对稳定性进行研究。

The two conformations of ethane, staggered and eclipsed, are different and therefore should be in different energy levels. You may also predict intuitively that the staggered conformation is more stable and is lower energy, because the C-H bonds are arranged as far apart as possible in that conformation. That is correct! In eclipsed conformations, the H atoms on the front carbon are overlapping with the H atoms on the rear carbon, and this arrangement causes the repulsion between the electrons of C-H bonds of the two carbons. This type of repulsion is called the **torsional strain,** also known as the eclipsing strain. Due to the torsional strain, the eclipsed conformer is in the energy level that is 12 kJ/mol (or about 2.9 kcal/mol) higher than the staggered one. This can be represented graphically in a potential energy diagram as shown in Figure 4.1f.

> 乙烷存在两种构象：对位（staggered）和重叠（eclipsed），它们的能量不同，因此应处于不同的能量水平。你也可以直观地预测，对位构象更加稳定，能量更低，因为在该构象中，C-H键的排列尽可能远离，从而减少了相互作用。这种说法是正确的！在重叠构象中，前面碳原子上的H原子与后面碳原子上的H原子重叠，这种排列会导致两个碳原子上的C-H键电子之间的排斥作用。这种排斥作用被称为扭转张力（torsional strain），也称为重叠张力（eclipsing strain）。由于扭转张力的存在，重叠构象的能量比对位构象高约12 kJ/mol（约合2.9 kcal/mol）。这种能量差异可以以势能图的形式表示，如图4.1f所示。

![](_page_123_Figure_0.jpeg)

*Figure 4.1e Staggered vs. eclipsed conformation*

> 图4.1e 反式与重叠式构型

![](_page_123_Figure_2.jpeg)

*Fig. 4.1f Potential Energy of Ethane vs the Angle of Rotation about the C-C bond*

> 图4.1f 乙烷的势能与碳-碳键旋转角度的关系

Because of this energy difference, an energy barrier must be overcome when the rotation about the C-C bond occurs. However, this energy difference in ethane is rather small, and the kinetic energy of molecules at room temperature is high enough to cover it. So at room temperature, the changes from staggered to eclipsed conformers occur millions of times per second. Because of these continuous interconversions, these two conformers cannot be separated from each other. However, at any given moment, about 99% of the ethane molecules will be in a staggered conformation because of their higher stability.

> 由于这种能量差异，在围绕碳-碳单键旋转时必须克服一个能量障碍。然而，在乙烷中，这种能量差异相对较小，常温下分子的动能足以克服这一能量障碍。因此，在常温下，乙烷分子从锯齿构象转变为重叠构象的构象异构体每秒会发生数百万次。由于这些连续的相互转化，这两种构象异构体无法被分离。然而，在任意某一时刻，约有99%的乙烷分子处于锯齿构象，这是因为锯齿构象具有更高的稳定性。

#### 0.1.4 **4.1.3 Conformation Analysis of Propane**

> 0.1.4 4.1.3 丙烷的构象分析

A similar analysis can be applied to propane as well. We will find that there are still two types of conformations, staggered and eclipsed, resulting from the rotation. The difference between propane and ethane is that there is a methyl (CH3) group connected on the rear carbon for propane. However, that does not affect the relative stability, and the staggered conformer is more stable and in lower energy.

> 类似的分析也可以应用于丙烷。我们会发现，丙烷同样存在两种构象，即交叉式和重叠式，这是由于旋转所导致的。丙烷与乙烷的不同之处在于，丙烷的后一个碳原子上连接了一个甲基（CH₃）基团。然而，这并不会影响相对稳定性，交叉式构象更加稳定，能量也更低。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_124_Figure_0.jpeg)

*Figure 4.1g Staggered and eclipsed conformation of propane*

> 图4.1g 丙烷的锯齿形与重叠式构象

#### 0.1.5 **4.1.4 Conformation Analysis of Butane**

> 0.1.5 4.1.4 正丁烷的构象分析

There are three C-C bonds in butane, and rotation can occur about each of them. If we pick up C1-C2 (or C3-C4) for the study, the situation is almost the same as propane, with the ethyl CH2CH3 group replace the CH3 group. However, if we consider the rotation about the C2-C3 bond, the situation will be much more complex.

> 丁烷分子中有三个碳-碳单键，且每个单键均可绕其旋转。如果我们选取C1-C2（或C3-C4）键作为研究对象，其情况几乎与丙烷相同，只是用乙基CH₂CH₃取代了甲基CH₃。然而，如果我们考虑绕C2-C3键的旋转，情况将变得复杂得多。

![](_page_124_Figure_4.jpeg)

*Figure 4.1h Conformation analysis of butane by viewing along C2-C3 bond*

> 图4.1h 从C2-C3键视角分析丁烷的构象

For both carbon atoms, C2 and C3, there are two hydrogen atoms and one methyl CH3 group bonded with. We can start with the conformer in which the two CH3 groups are **opposite** to each other, then fix the front carbon and do 60° rotations of the rear carbon to investigate **all** the possible conformations.

> 对于这两个碳原子C2和C3，每个原子都连接有两个氢原子和一个甲基CH₃基团。我们可以从两个CH₃基团彼此相对的构象开始，固定前方的碳原子，然后对后方的碳原子进行60°的旋转，以考察所有可能的构象。

*Exercises 4.1: Draw all the possible conformers of butane from viewing along the C2-C3 bond. Finish this practice by yourself before continue reading!*

> 练习 4.1：从 C2-C3 键的方向观察，画出丁烷的所有可能构象。在继续阅读之前，请先自己完成此练习！

**Tips** for drawing all the possible conformers about a certain C-C bond:

> 关于某一个C-C键的所有可能构象的绘制技巧：

- View along that C-C bond; circle and decide what atoms/groups are connected on each carbon;
- Start with the staggered conformation in which the largest groups on each carbon are opposite (far away) to each other (this is called the "*anti"*conformation as we will learn later);
- Keep the groups on one carbon "fixed", and rotate the groups on the other carbon at 60° angles. Repeat the rotation five times, and you should get total of six conformers.

> 沿该C-C键观察；用圆圈标出并判断每个碳原子上连接的是哪些原子或基团；  
从一种锯齿构象开始，其中每个碳原子上最大的基团彼此相对（相距较远）（这种构象我们之后会称为“反式”构象）；  
固定一个碳原子上的基团，以60°的角度旋转另一个碳原子上的基团。重复此旋转五次，你应该得到总共六种构象。

Answers to Practice Questions Chapter 4

> 第四章练习题答案

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_125_Figure_5.jpeg)

*Figure 4.1i All the conformers of butane by viewing along C2-C3 bond*

> 图4.1i 从C2-C3键方向观察丁烷的所有构象

Among all the six conformers obtained, there are three staggered and three eclipsed. Staggered conformations **C** and **E** should be in the same energy level because the groups are arranged in equivalent way between these two conformers. Similarly, eclipsed conformations **F** and **B** are also in the same energy level. So our studies can be focused on the four conformers, **A, B, C** and **D**, that are different in terms of energy and stability.

> 在所得到的六个构象中，有三个是锯齿形构象，另外三个是重叠形构象。锯齿形构象C和E应处于相同的能量水平，因为在两个构象之间，取代基的排列方式是等效的。同样，重叠形构象F和B也处于相同的能量水平。因此，我们的研究可以集中在四个能量和稳定性不同的构象上，即A、B、C和D。

Between the two staggered conformers **A** and **C**, **A** is more stable than **C** because the two methyl CH3 groups in **A** are as far apart as possible. This most stable staggered conformation is called the **anti** conformation (*anti* is Greek for "opposite"). In **anti** conformations, the largest groups on the front and rear carbon are 180° opposite to each other. The other staggered conformation **C** is called a **gauche** conformation, in which the two large groups are adjacent and are 60° to each other. With the large groups being close to each other in gauche conformers, the molecule experiences **steric strain**. **Steric strain** is the strain that is caused when atoms (or groups) are close enough together that their electron clouds repel each other. Steric strain only matters when the groups are close to each other (less or equal to 60°), so steric strain does not apply in anti conformations. The magnitude of steric strain also depends on the size of group; the larger the size, the higher the steric strain. As a result, there is no steric strain between two small hydrogen atoms, even if they are close to each other.

> 在两个交错构象A和C之间，A比C更稳定，因为A中的两个甲基（CH₃）基团彼此相距最远。这种最稳定的交错构象被称为反式构象（anti，源自希腊语“相反”）。在反式构象中，前碳和后碳上较大的基团彼此相对，夹角为18.0°。另一种交错构象C被称为邻位构象（gauche），其中两个较大的基团相邻，夹角为60°。在邻位构象中，较大的基团彼此接近，导致分子产生空间张力（steric strain）。空间张力是指当原子（或基团）彼此距离足够近时，其电子云之间产生排斥作用所导致的张力。空间张力只有在基团彼此接近（夹角小于或等于60°）时才会产生，因此在反式构象中不会出现空间张力。空间张力的大小还取决于基团的大小，基团越大，空间张力也越大。因此，即使两个小的氢原子彼此接近，也不会产生空间张力。

![](_page_126_Figure_0.jpeg)

*Figure 4.1j Anti and gauche conformations*

> 图4.1j 反式与 gauche 构象

Between the two eclipsed conformers **B** and **D**, **D** is less stable than **B**, because the two CH3 groups are eclipsing (overlapping) each other in **D**, causing both torsional and steric strains.

> 在两个顺式构象B和D之间，D比B更不稳定，因为在D中，两个CH₃基团相互重叠，导致了扭转应力和位阻应力。

![](_page_126_Figure_3.jpeg)

*Figure 4.1k Comparison between the two eclipsed conformations*

> 图4.1k 两种重叠构象的比较

The energy difference of all the conformers obtained from the rotation about the C2-C3 bond are shown in the potential energy diagram **Fig. 4.1l**. The curve is more complex than that of ethane since there are four different energy levels corresponding to four conformers with different stabilities. Even the energy barriers for the rotations are larger than that of ethane, but they are still not high enough to stop rotation at room temperature.

> 通过C2-C3键的旋转所得到的所有构象的能级差如图4.1l所示的势能图所示。该曲线比乙烷的更为复杂，因为存在四个不同的能量水平，分别对应于稳定性不同的四种构象。即使旋转所需的能垒比乙烷更高，但在常温下这些能垒仍然不足以阻止旋转的发生。

![](_page_127_Figure_1.jpeg)

*Figure 4.1l Potential Energy of Butane vs the Angle of Rotation about the C2-C3 bond*

> 图4.1l 正丁烷相对于C2-C3键旋转角度的势能

### 0.2 *Exercises 4.2*

> 0.2 习题 4.2

Draw all conformers for 3-methylpentane by viewing along the C2-C3 bond, and order them from the most stable to least stable.

> 沿C2-C3键观察3-甲基戊烷的所有构象，并按稳定性由高到低排列。

Answers to Practice Questions Chapter 4

> 第四章练习题答案

# 4.2 Cycloalkanes and Their Relative Stabilities

> 4.2 环烷烃及其相对稳定性

While the open chain alkanes have conformational isomers because of bond rotation, will this apply to cycloalkanes as well? In this section, we will take a look at properties of cycloalkanes first, and then investigate how the different conformers of cycloalkanes contribute to the different stabilities.

> 尽管开链烷烃由于单键的旋转而存在构象异构体，但环烷烃是否也具有类似的情况呢？在本节中，我们将首先探讨环烷烃的性质，然后研究环烷烃的不同构象体如何影响其不同的稳定性。

The short line structural formulas of cycloalkenes simply look like shapes such as a triangle, square etc. The internal angles of the shapes can be calculated with geometry, as shown below.

> 环烯烃的短线结构式看起来像三角形、正方形等形状。这些形状的内角可以通过几何方法计算，如下所示。

![](_page_128_Figure_3.jpeg)

*Figure 4.2a Short line structural formula of cycloalkanes*

> 图4.2a 环烷烃的短线结构式

An interesting fact about the cycloalkanes is that they have different relative stabilities, and the stability depends on the size of the ring. It has been observed that cyclic compounds found in nature usually are in 5- or 6-membered rings, and the 3- or 4-membered rings are rather rare.

> 环烷烃的一个有趣事实是，它们具有不同的相对稳定性，而稳定性取决于环的大小。人们观察到，自然界中常见的环状化合物通常为五元环或六元环，而三元环或四元环则较为罕见。

To explain this stability difference, German chemist Adolf von Baeyer proposed the "Bayer Strain Theory". By assuming all the rings are in a *flat* (or planar) shape, Bayer Theory suggests that the difference between the ideal bond angle (which is 109.5° for sp<sup>3</sup> carbon) and the angle in the planer cycloalkane causes the strain, which is called **angle strain**. According to the Bayer Theory, cyclopentane would be the most stable because its bond angles, 108°, are closest to the ideal angle of 109.5°. Cyclopropane would be the least stable one since it has the largest angle deviation of 49.5° (60° vs 109.5°). It was also predicted that cyclohexane would be less stable than cyclopentane because of the larger angle deviation (10.5° deviation for cyclohexane vs 1.5° for cyclopentane), and as the number of sides in the cycloalkanes increases beyond six the stability would decrease.

> 为了解释这种稳定性差异，德国化学家阿道夫·冯·拜尔（Adolf von Baeyer）提出了“拜尔应变理论”。该理论假设所有的环都是平面（或共平面）结构，认为环烷烃中理想键角（sp³碳的理想键角为109.5°）与平面环烷烃中实际键角之间的差异导致了应变，这种应变被称为“角应变”。根据拜尔理论，环戊烷是最稳定的，因为其键角为108°，最接近理想键角109.5°。而环丙烷则是最不稳定的，因为它键角偏离最大，偏离值为49.5°（60°与109.5°之间的差异）。此外，拜尔理论还预测环己烷的稳定性会比环戊烷低，因为环己烷的键角偏离值更大（环己烷偏离值为10.5°，而环戊烷仅为1.5°）。随着环烷烃的环数超过六元环，其稳定性还会继续下降。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_128_Figure_7.jpeg)

*Figure 4.2b Which cyclo is stable?*

> 图4.2b 哪个环状结构更稳定？

However, experimental results show a different trend. It turns out that **cyclohexane** is the most stable ring that is strainfree, and is as stable as a chain alkane. Furthermore, cyclic compounds do not become less and less stable as the number of rings increases.

> 然而，实验结果却显示出不同的趋势。事实上，环己烷是唯一一个无张力的稳定环状结构，其稳定性与链状烷烃相当。此外，环状化合物的稳定性并不会随着环数的增加而逐渐降低。

To measure the relative stability of cycloalkanes, the heat of combustion (ΔHcomb) for each cycloalkane was measured. The heat of combustion is the amount of heat released when the compounds burns completely with oxygen. The cycloalkanes will be in higher energy levels than corresponding chain alkanes because of strain energy. Therefore, when cycloalkane burns, more heat will be released, so the difference of ΔHcomb between cycloalkane vs the "strainless" chain alkane is just the amount of strain energy, as shown below. The larger the difference, the higher the strain energy of the cycloalkane. The strain energy for different cycloalkanes measured by this method are listed in **Table 4.1**.

> 为了衡量环烷烃的相对稳定性，测量了每种环烷烃的燃烧热（ΔHcomb）。燃烧热是指化合物在氧气中完全燃烧时释放的热量。由于存在应变能，环烷烃的能量水平高于相应的直链烷烃。因此，当环烷烃燃烧时，会释放更多的热量。环烷烃与“无应变”的直链烷烃之间的ΔHcomb差值，即为该环烷烃的应变能，如下面所示。差值越大，说明环烷烃的应变能越高。通过这种方法测得的不同环烷烃的应变能列于表4.1中。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_129_Figure_1.jpeg)

combustion reaction: (CH2)n + 3n/2 O2 → n CO2 + n H2O + heat

> 燃烧反应：(CH₂)ₙ + ₃ₙ/₂ O₂ → n CO₂ + n H₂O + 热量

*Figure 4.2c The relationship between heat of combustion and strain energy*

> 图4.2c 燃烧热与应变能的关系

|                        | cyclopropane | cyclobutane | cyclopentane | cyclohexane |
|------------------------|--------------|-------------|--------------|-------------|
| Strain Energy (KJ/mol) | 114          | 110         | 25           | 0           |

> |                        | 环丙烷 | 环丁烷 | 环戊烷 | 环己烷 |
|------------------------|------|------|------|------|
| 应力能 (kJ/mol)        | 114  | 110  | 25   | 0    |

**Table 4.1 Strain Energies of Cycloalkanes**

> 表4.1 环烷烃的应变能

The major drawback of the Baeyer Theory was that we must assume that all the rings are flat. The highest stability of cyclohexane from experimental results indicate that the rings may not be in a planar shape. We will have a closer look at the actual shape and conformation of 3-, 4-, 5- and 6-membered cycloalkanes.

> 巴耶尔理论的主要缺陷在于我们必须假设所有的环都是平面的。从实验结果来看，环己烷的最高稳定性表明环可能并不是平面结构。我们将更仔细地探讨三元、四元、五元和六元环烷烃的实际形状和构象。

#### 0.1.1 **Cyclopropane**

> 0.1.1 环丙烷

With three carbons for the ring, cyclopropane must be planar.

> 环丙烷由于环上有三个碳原子，因此必须是平面结构。

![](_page_129_Figure_9.jpeg)

*Figure 4.2d Cyclopropane*

> 图4.2d 环丙烷

The bond angle in cyclopropane is 60°, derived significantly from the optimal angle of 109.5°, so it has very high angle strains. The sp<sup>3</sup> -sp<sup>3</sup> orbitals can only overlap partially because of the angle deviation, so the overlapping is not as effective as it should be, and as a result the C-C bond in cyclopropane is relatively weak.

> 环丙烷中的键角为60°，远低于理想四面体角度109.5°，因此其具有非常高的角张力。由于键角偏离了sp³-sp³轨道的最佳重叠角度，这些轨道只能部分重叠，导致重叠效果不如预期，因此环丙烷中的C-C键相对较为脆弱。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_130_Picture_1.jpeg)

Because of the poor overlapping of sp<sup>3</sup> -sp<sup>3</sup> orbitals, the bonds formed in cyclopropane resemble the shape of a banana, and are sometimes called banana bonds.

> 由于sp³-sp³轨道重叠程度较差，环丙烷中形成的键呈现出香蕉状的形状，因此有时被称为“香蕉键”。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_130_Picture_3.jpeg)

*Figure 4.2e "Banana bonds" of cyclopropane*

> 图4.2e 环丙烷的“香蕉键”

Other than the angle strains, all the adjacent C-H bonds are eclipsed in cyclopropane, therefore the torsional strains are applied as well. Such a strain can be "viewed" more clearly from the Newman projection of cyclopropane.

> 除了角张力之外，环丙烷中所有相邻的C-H键均处于对位交叉式，因此也存在扭转张力。这种张力可以通过环丙烷的纽曼投影更清晰地观察到。

![](_page_130_Figure_6.jpeg)

**The Newman projection of cyclopropane might seems weird at first glance. For cyclopropane, there are three carbons, so the CH2 group connects with both front and rear carbons of the Newman projection.**

> 环丙烷的纽曼投影在初看时可能会显得有些奇怪。对于环丙烷而言，它有三个碳原子，因此CH₂基团同时连接着纽曼投影中前方和后方的碳原子。

Because of the high level of angle strains and torsional strains, 3-membered rings are unstable. They rarely exist in nature and undergo ring-opening reaction easily to release the strains.

> 由于存在较高的角张力和扭转张力，三元环结构不稳定。它们在自然界中很少存在，容易发生开环反应以释放张力。

#### 0.1.2 **Cyclobutane**

> 0.1.2 环丁烷

Cyclobutane is not planar. The ring puckers (or folds) slightly due to the efforts of releasing some torsional strain. Meanwhile, cyclobutane still has a considerable amount of angle strains as the internal angles become about 88° with the folded shape. Overall, cyclobutane is an unstable structure with rather high level of strains.

> 环丁烷并非平面结构。由于释放部分扭转张力的作用，环丁烷环会略微 puckering（或折叠）。同时，环丁烷在折叠结构下，内角约为88°，仍然存在相当大的角度张力。总体而言，环丁烷是一种不稳定结构，具有较高程度的张力。

#### 0.1.3 **Cyclopentane**

> 0.1.3 环戊烷

Cyclopentane is not planar as well and the total level of strain is lowered quite a lot. It also puckers and adopts a bent conformation where one carbon atom sticks out of the plane of the others, which helps to release the torsional strain by allowing some hydrogen atoms to become almost staggered.

> 环戊烷同样不是平面结构，其总应变水平降低了很多。它还会发生扭曲，采取一种弯曲构象，其中有一个碳原子突出于其他碳原子所在的平面，这种结构有助于通过使一些氢原子几乎呈反式排列来释放扭转应变。

$$\begin{array}{cccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccc$$

> 

This bent shape of cyclopentane is also called the "envelope" conformation. The envelope conformation can undergo a process called "ring flipping" as a result of C-C bond rotation. More discussions about ring flipping will be included in the section of cyclohexane.

> 环戊烷的这种弯曲构型也被称为“信封式”构象。信封式构象可以通过碳-碳单键的旋转经历一个称为“环翻转”的过程。关于环翻转的更多内容将在环己烷一节中进行讨论。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_131_Picture_9.jpeg)

# 4.3 Conformation Analysis of Cyclohexane

> 4.3 环己烷的构象分析

#### 0.1.1 **Chair conformation of cyclohexane**

> 0.1.1 环己烷的椅式构象

Cyclohexane is the **most stable** cycloalkane. It is strain-free, meaning neither angle strains nor torsional strains apply, and it shows the same stability as chain alkanes. This special stability is due to a unique conformation that it adopts. The most stable conformation of cyclohexane is called "**chair**" **conformation**, since it somewhat resembles a chair.

> 环己烷是最稳定的环烷烃。它没有环张力，也就是说既不存在角张力，也不存在扭转张力，其稳定性与链状烷烃相同。这种特殊的稳定性是由于环己烷采取了一种独特的构象。环己烷最稳定的构象称为“椅式构象”，因为其形状与椅子有些相似。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_132_Picture_3.jpeg)

In the chair conformation of cyclohexane, all the carbons are at 109.5º bond angles, so no angle strain applies. The hydrogens on adjacent carbons are also arranged in a perfect staggered conformation that makes the ring free of torsional strain as well. This will be illustrated more clearly later when we learn about the Newman projection of the chair conformation.

> 在环己烷的椅式构象中，所有碳原子的键角均为109.5º，因此不存在角张力。此外，相邻碳原子上的氢原子也排列成完美的反式构象，使环不存在扭转张力。这一点将在我们学习椅式构象的纽曼投影时更加清晰地展示出来。

#### 0.1.2 **Properties of the chair conformation**

> 0.1.2 椅式构型的特性

In the chair conformation of cyclohexane, the total twelve C-H bonds can be divided into two categories based on the orientations, which are *axial ("a")* and *equatorial ("e")*. In the structure below, the six red coloured bonds are *axial* and the six blue coloured bonds are *equatorial*. Axial bonds are vertical and perpendicular to the average plane of the ring, while the equatorial bonds are more "flat" and extend from the perimeter of the ring. For both "*a*" and "*e*", they can either point up ↑(above the ring), or point down ↓(below the ring). The trending of "*a*" and "*e*" bonds in the chair conformation can be summarized as:

> 在环己烷的椅式构象中，总共十二个C-H键可以根据其取向分为两类，即轴向（“a”）和赤道（“e”）。在下面的结构中，六个红色的键为轴向键，六个蓝色的键为赤道键。轴向键是垂直的，并且与环的平均平面垂直；而赤道键则更加“平展”，从环的边缘延伸出来。对于“a”和“e”键来说，它们既可以指向上方（↑，环的上方），也可以指向下方（↓，环的下方）。在椅式构象中，“a”和“e”键的取向趋势可以总结为：

• Each carbon has one "*a"* bond and one "*e"* bond; if one bond points up ↑(above the ring), the other has to point down ↓(below the ring);

> • 每个碳原子各有一个“a”键和一个“e”键；如果一个键指向上方 ↑（环的上方），另一个键就必须指向下方 ↓（环的下方）；

- For the same type of bonds, the orientation up ↑ and down ↓ alternates from one carbons to the adjacent carbon, meaning if a certain carbon has a ↑, then the adjacent carbon must has a ↓;
- For the total twelve C-H bonds: 3*a*↑ , 3 *a*↓, 3 *e*↑ , 3 *e*↓.

> 对于同类型的化学键，相邻碳原子上的取向（向上↑ 和向下↓）交替变化，即如果一个碳原子上是↑，那么相邻的碳原子上必须是↓；  
对于总共十二个C-H键：3a↑，3a↓，3e↑，3e↓。

### 0.2 **How to draw chair conformation**

> 0.2 如何绘制椅式构象

It is important to be able to understand and recognize all the bonds in the chair conformation, and you are also expected to be able to draw the conformation correctly and quickly. The procedure is:

> 能够理解并识别椅式构象中的所有键是非常重要的，你也被期望能够迅速而正确地画出构象。具体步骤如下：

1. Draw two parallel lines of the same length both point slightly down (if connected, they would form a parallelogram

> 画两条长度相同的平行线，两条线都略微向下倾斜（如果连接起来，它们会形成一个平行四边形）

with an internal angle of about 60°/120°).

> 具有约60°/120°的内角。

2. Connect the right ending points of the two lines with a "V" shape, so that the vertex of the V points to the upper

> 将两条线的右端点用“V”形连接起来，使“V”形的顶点指向上方。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_133_Picture_7.jpeg)

3. Connect the left starting points of the two lines with another "V" shape, so that the vertex of the V points to the

> 将两条线的左侧起点用另一个“V”形连接起来，使V形的顶点指向

bottom left Add up all of the "a" bonds on each carbon as the **vertical** lines, follow the alternating trend on adjacent carbons

> 左下角 将每个碳原子上的所有“a”键（即σ键）数起来，以垂直线表示，遵循相邻碳原子上的交替趋势

![](_page_133_Picture_10.jpeg)

4. Add all of the "e" bonds by following the trend in which on a certain carbon, if an "a" bond points up, then an "e" bond must point down, and vice versa. Also notice that the "e" bond is parallel to the C-C bond which is one bond away, as shown below. The "**green e**" is parallel to the "**green C-C bond"**, and the "**blue e**" is parallel to the "**blue C-C bond".** (It is more challenging to draw "e" bonds, and following the above trend makes it easier).

> 按照一定的趋势添加所有“e”键：在某一碳原子上，如果“a”键指向上方，则“e”键必须指向下方，反之亦然。同时请注意，“e”键与相邻的C-C键平行，如下面所示。“绿色的e键”与“绿色的C-C键”平行，“蓝色的e键”与“蓝色的C-C键”平行。（绘制“e”键较为困难，遵循上述规律会使绘制更加容易。）

![](_page_133_Picture_12.jpeg)

**It is highly recommended that a molecular model set is used as a study tool in this section. Assemble a cyclohexane ring with the model, and get familiar with all the bonds in chair conformation.**

> 在本节中，建议使用分子模型套件作为学习工具。用模型搭建一个环己烷环，并熟悉椅式构象中的所有键。

**Practice makes perfect! A lot of practice is required to become skilled in drawing and understanding the chair conformation.**

> 熟能生巧！要熟练地绘制和理解椅式构象，需要大量的练习。

### 0.3 **Ring flipping**

> 0.3 环翻转

When a cyclohexane ring undergoes a chair-chair conformation conversion, that is known as **ring flipping**. Ring flipping comes from C-C bond rotation, but since all of the bonds are limited within the ring, the rotation can only occur *partially,* which leads to the ring "flipping". Cyclohexane rapidly interconverts between two stable chair conformations because of the ease of bond rotation. The energy barrier is about 45 kJ/mol, and the thermal energies of the molecules at room temperature are great enough to cause about 1 million interconversions to occur per second.

> 当环己烷环从一种椅式构象转换为另一种椅式构象时，这种现象被称为环翻转。环翻转来源于C-C单键的旋转，但由于所有键都受到环结构的限制，因此旋转只能部分发生，从而导致环“翻转”。由于单键旋转较为容易，环己烷能够在两种稳定的椅式构象之间快速相互转化。其能量障碍约为45 kJ/mol，在室温下分子的热能足以使每秒发生约一百万次的构象转换。

For cyclohexane, the ring after flipping still appears somewhat identical to the original ring, however there are some changes happening on the C-H bonds. Specifically, all the **"a" bonds become "e" bonds** and all the **"e" bonds become "a" bonds**, however their relative positions in terms of the ring, up or down, remain the same. The ring flipping is shown in the equation below. Compare the carbon with the same numbering in the two structures to see what happened to the bonds due to ring flipping.

> 对于环己烷而言，环翻转后，环的结构仍然与原环在整体上看起来有些相似，但C-H键会发生一些变化。具体来说，所有的“a”键会变为“e”键，所有的“e”键会变为“a”键，但它们相对于环的位置（即上下方向）保持不变。环翻转过程如下面的方程式所示。将两个结构中编号相同的碳原子进行对比，可以观察到由于环翻转所导致的键的变化。

![](_page_134_Picture_4.jpeg)

Taking C #1 as an example, you will notice that the red **a**↓ converted to a red **e**↓, and the blue **e**↑ converted to a blue **a**↑ after ring flipping.

> 以C#1为例，你会注意到在环翻转后，红色的a↓转化为红色的e↓，蓝色的e↑则转化为蓝色的a↑。

#### 0.3.1 **Summary of ring flipping for chair conformation:**

> 0.3.1 椅式构型的环翻转总结：

- This is **NOT** rotation, but ring flipping
- The two structures are conformation isomers (or conformers)
- all "a" bonds become "e" bonds and all "e" bonds become "a" bonds
- These two conformations are **equivalent** for the cyclohexane ring itself (without any substituents), with the same energy level

> 这不是旋转，而是环翻转。  
这两种结构是构象异构体（或称构象体）。  
所有的“a”键变为“e”键，所有的“e”键变为“a”键。  
对于环己烷环本身（没有取代基）来说，这两种构象是等价的，具有相同的能量水平。

A molecular model is very useful in understanding ring flipping.

> 分子模型在理解环翻转过程中非常有用。

#### 0.3.2 **Newman projection of chair conformation**

> 0.3.2 椅式构型的纽曼投影

The chair conformation is strain free, with all the C-H bonds in staggered position. However, it is not that easy to see the staggered conformation in the drawings we have so far, and Newman projection help for this purpose.

> 椅式构象没有张力，所有C-H键均处于反式位置。然而，我们目前的图示中不容易看出反式构象，纽曼投影有助于说明这一问题。

To draw Newman projections for the chair conformation of cyclohexane, we also need to pick up the C-C bond to view along, just as we did for alkanes. Since there are a total of six C-C bonds, we will pick two of them, and these two need to be parallel to each other.

> 为了绘制环己烷椅式构象的纽曼投影，我们也需要选择一个C-C键作为观察方向，这与我们观察烷烃时的方法相同。由于环己烷中共有六个C-C键，我们只需选择其中两个，并且这两个键需要彼此平行。

$$\begin{array}{cccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccc$$

> 

For the chair conformation example here, the two blue parallel C-C bonds are picked up for viewing, which are C1-C2 and C5-C4. (There are 3 pairs of parallel bonds in the chair conformation, any pair can be picked with the resulting Newman projection looking the same).

> 在此椅式构象的例子中，我们选取了两个蓝色平行的C-C键用于观察，即C1-C2和C5-C4键。（椅式构象中共有三对平行键，任选其中一对所得的纽曼投影式均相同。）

For the C1-C2 bond, C1 is the 'front" carbon and C2 is the "rear" carbon; for the C5-C4 bond, C5 is the 'front" carbon and C4 is the "rear" carbon. These two bonds will be represented by two "Newman projections" that we are familiar with (two circle things) and each represents two carbons, as shown below:

> 对于C1-C2键，C1是“前面”的碳原子，C2是“后面”的碳原子；对于C5-C4键，C5是“前面”的碳原子，C4是“后面”的碳原子。这两条键将用我们熟悉的两种“纽曼投影”来表示（即两个圆形结构），每种投影表示两个碳原子，如下所示：

$$\begin{array}{cccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccc$$

> 

Keep in mind that there are a total of six carbons in the ring, and the the drawing above only shows four of them with C3 and C6 being left out. Additionally, the two "separated" Newman projections above are actually connected to both C3 and C6, so the overall Newman projection of the chair conformation of cyclohexane looks like this:

> 请注意，环上总共有六个碳原子，而上面的图示仅展示了其中的四个，C3和C6被省略了。此外，上面所说的两个“分离”的纽曼投影实际上都连接到C3和C6上，因此环己烷椅式构象的整体纽曼投影看起来如下：

The *staggered* conformation of hydrogens are shown clearly in the Newman projection here! Notes for Newman projections of the chair conformation (refer to the drawing below):

> 此处的纽曼投影清晰地展示了氢原子的 staggered（错位）构型！纽曼投影中椅式构型的注意事项（参见下图）：

- The "a" or "e" bonds on four carbons (C1, C2, C4 and C5) are shown explicitly, while the bonds on C3 and C6 are just shown as CH2.
- The vertical red C-H bonds are the "a" bonds, the "flat" blue C-H bonds are the "e" bonds.
- The dashed line in the drawing below can be regarded as the average plane of the ring. Those above the line are the bonds point up ↑, those below the line are the bonds point down ↓.

> 四个碳原子（C1、C2、C4 和 C5）上的 "a" 或 "e" 键被明确地表示出来，而 C3 和 C6 上的键则仅表示为 CH₂。

图中垂直的红色 C-H 键为 "a" 键，平坦的蓝色 C-H 键为 "e" 键。

下面图中的虚线可视为环的平均平面。位于虚线以上的键指向上方（↑），位于虚线以下的键指向下方（↓）。

#### 0.3.3 **Other conformation of cyclohexane**

> 0.3.3 环己烷的其他构象

•

> •

The chair conformation is the most stable one with the lowest energy, but it is not the only conformation for cyclohexane. During the ring flipping from one chair conformation to another chair conformation, the ring goes through several other conformations, and we will only talk briefly about the boat conformation here.

> 椅式构象是最稳定的一种，具有最低的能量，但它并不是环己烷的唯一构象。在从一种椅式构象翻转到另一种椅式构象的过程中，环会经过几种其他的构象，这里我们仅简要介绍船式构象。

![](_page_136_Picture_7.jpeg)

*Figure 4.3a Boat conformation of cyclohexane*

> 图4.3a 环己烷的船式构象

The boat conformation comes from partial C-C bond rotations (only flipping one carbon up to convert the chair to a boat) of the chair conformation, and all the carbons still have 109.5º bond angles, so there are no angle strains. However, the hydrogens on the base of the boat are all in eclipsed positions, so there are torsional strains. This can be illustrated by the Newman projection below. The Newman projection is drawn by viewing along C6-C5 and C2-C3 bonds of the above boat conformation.

> 船式构象来源于椅式构象中部分C-C键的旋转（仅翻转一个碳原子，将椅式构象转变为船式构象），所有碳原子的键角仍保持109.5º，因此没有角张力。然而，船式构象中船底的氢原子均处于重叠位置，因此存在扭转张力。这可以通过下面的纽曼投影图来说明。纽曼投影图是从上述船式构象的C6-C5和C2-C3键方向观察所得。

![](_page_137_Picture_1.jpeg)

*Figure 4.3b Newman projection of boat conformation*

> 图4.3b 船型构象的纽曼投影

Other than that, the two hydrogen atoms on C1 and C4 are very close to each other and causes steric strain. This is also called the "flagpole" interaction of the boat conformation. The two types of strains make the boat conformation have considerably higher energy (about 30 kJ/mol) than the chair conformation.

> 除此之外，C1 和 C4 上的两个氢原子彼此非常接近，从而导致了空间位阻。这种现象也被称为船式构象的“旗杆”相互作用。这两种类型的张力使得船式构象的能量显著高于椅式构象（约高 30 kJ/mol）。

# 4.4 Substituted Cyclohexanes

> 4.4 取代环己烷

#### 0.1.1 **Monosubstituted cyclohexane**

> 0.1.1 单取代环己烷

For the cyclohexane ring itself, the two conformers from the ring flipping are equivalent in terms of energy since there are always six hydrogens in *axial* position and six hydrogens in *equatorial* position. For substituted cyclohexane however, the two chair conformations are **not** equivalent any more. Let's see the example of methylcyclohexane.

> 对于环己烷环本身，由于环翻转后总是存在六个轴向氢原子和六个赤道向氢原子，因此两种构象在能量上是等价的。然而，对于取代的环己烷来说，两种椅式构象就不再等价了。让我们以甲基环己烷为例进行说明。

![](_page_138_Figure_3.jpeg)

*Figure 4.4a (Left one) I, less stable & (Right one) II, more stable*

> 图4.4a（左图）I，较不稳定；（右图）II，更稳定

Methylcyclohexane has two chair conformations that are interconvertible through the ring flipping. In conformation **I** the methyl group occupies an *axial* position, and in conformation **II** the methyl group occupies an *equatorial* position. Studies indicate that the **conformer II** with the *equatorial*-methyl is more stable, with the energy of about 7.6 kJ/mol lower than the other conformer.

> 甲基环己烷有两种椅式构象，它们可以通过环翻转相互转化。在构象I中，甲基处于轴向位置，而在构象II中，甲基处于赤道位置。研究表明，具有赤道甲基的构象II更为稳定，其能量比另一种构象低约7.6 kJ/mol。

This difference is due to the "**1,3-diaxal interaction**". In *axial-*methyl conformation, the methyl CH3 group (regarded as #1 position) is very close to the *axial* hydrogens that is one carbon away (regarded as #3 position), and it causes the repulsion between each other that is called the 1,3-diaxal interaction. This type of repulsion is essentially the same as the gauche steric strain because the CH3 group and the CH are in gauche position. While for *equatorial*-methyl conformer, no such strains applied because the CH3 group and the CH are in anti-position. This interaction could be illustrated more clearly by Newman projection.

> 这种差异是由于“1,3-轴向相互作用”所导致的。在轴向甲基构象中，甲基（CH₃，视为第1位）非常接近一个碳原子位置的轴向氢原子（视为第3位），这种相互靠近导致了彼此之间的排斥作用，称为“1,3-轴向相互作用”。这种排斥作用本质上与 gauche 空间位阻是相同的，因为 CH₃ 基团与 CH 基团处于 gauche 位置。而对于赤道甲基构象，由于 CH₃ 基团与 CH 基团处于反式位置，因此不会产生这种位阻效应。这种相互作用可以通过纽曼投影更清晰地加以说明。

![](_page_138_Picture_7.jpeg)

*Figure 4.4b 1,3-diaxial interaction*

> 图4.4b 1,3-轴向相互作用

$$\begin{array}{cccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccc$$

> 

**For mono-substituted cyclohexane, the** *equatorial***-conformer is more stable than the** *axial***-conformer because of the 1,3-diaxal interaction.**

> 对于单取代环己烷，赤道构象比轴向构象更为稳定，这是由于1,3-轴向相互作用所致。

Since 1,3-diaxal interaction is essentially the steric strain, so the larger the size of the substituent, the greater the interaction is. For *t*-butylcyclohexane, the conformation with the *t*-butyl group in the equatorial position is about 21 kJ/ mol more stable than the axial conformation.

> 由于1,3-直立相互作用本质上是立体阻碍，因此取代基的体积越大，这种相互作用就越显著。对于叔丁基环己烷来说，取代基位于赤道位置的构象比轴向构象稳定约21 kJ/mol。

Because of the stability difference between the two chair conformers, the *equatorial*-conformation is always the predominant one in the equilibrium mixture. The larger the size of the substituent, the larger the energy difference and the equilibrium constant *K*, so the equilibrium lies more toward the "equatorial" side. For methylcyclohexane, there is about 95% of *equatorial-*conformer in the mixture, and the percentage is about 99.9% for *t*-butylcyclohexane.

> 由于两种椅式构象之间的稳定性差异，椅式构象中赤道构型始终是平衡混合物中的主要形式。取代基的体积越大，能量差也越大，平衡常数K也越大，因此平衡更倾向于“赤道”一侧。对于甲基环己烷，混合物中约有95%的分子处于赤道构型；而对于叔丁基环己烷，这一比例约为99.9%。

#### 0.1.2 **Disubstituted cyclohexane**

> 0.1.2 双取代环己烷

When there are two substituents on different carbons of a cycloalkane, there are two possible relative position between the two groups, they can be either on the same side, or opposite side, of the ring, that are called **geometric isomers**, a type of **stereoisomers** (more discussions in **Chapter 5**). The isomer with two groups on the same side of the ring is the "*cis*" isomer, and the one with two groups on opposite side is called the "*trans*" isomer. Because the C-C bond can not rotate freely due to the restriction of the ring, the two geometric isomers can not be interconverted.

> 当环烷烃分子中存在两个取代基位于不同碳原子上时，这两个取代基在环上的相对位置有两种可能：它们可以位于环的同侧，也可以位于环的异侧。这两种情况称为几何异构体，是立体异构体的一种（更多讨论见第5章）。其中，两个取代基位于环同侧的异构体称为“顺式”异构体，而两个取代、基位于环异侧的异构体称为“反式”异构体。由于环的存在使碳-碳单键不能自由旋转，因此这两种几何异构体之间不能相互转化。

![](_page_140_Figure_2.jpeg)

*Figure 4.4c cis-1,2-dimethylcyclohexane (same side) & trans-1,2-dimethylcyclohexane (opposite side)*

> 图4.4c cis-1,2-二甲基环己烷（同侧）& trans-1,2-二甲基环己烷（异侧）

So now when considering about the conformational isomer, the stereoisomers should be taken into account as well. The general guideline for determining the relative stability of conformers for a certain isomer is:

> 因此，现在在考虑构象异构体时，也应同时考虑立体异构体。确定某一异构体的构象体相对稳定性的总体指导原则是：

- The steric effects of all substituents are *cumulative*, more substituents in *equatorial* positions, when possible, the more stable the conformation isomer will be.
- For different substituents, the conformer with *larger* substituent in *equatorial* positionis more stable.

> 所有取代基的立体效应是累积的，当更多的取代基处于赤道位置时，构象异构体将更加稳定。  
对于不同的取代基，处于赤道位置的较大取代基所对应的构象更加稳定。

Let us start with *cis*-1,2-dimethylcyclohexane, and compare between the two possible chair conformations:

> 让我们从顺式-1,2-二甲基环己烷开始，并比较两种可能的椅式构象：

![](_page_140_Figure_8.jpeg)

For both conformations, there is one methyl group in *equatorial* and the other methyl group in *axial*, so the two conformers are **equivalent**, have same energy and stability level.

> 对于这两种构象，有一个甲基处于赤道位置，另一个甲基处于轴向位置，因此这两种构象是等同的，具有相同的能量和稳定性。

How to tell a isomer in chair conformation is *cis* or *trans*? A general way to recognize is to check that whether a group attached by the bond is above the ring (↑, point up), or below the ring (↓, point down). If both groups point to the same side, the compound is *cis* isomer; otherwise it is *trans* isomer.

> 如何判断椅式构象中的异构体是顺式还是反式？一种通用的方法是检查连接基团相对于环的位置：如果一个基团通过键连接在环的上方（↑，向上指），另一个基团在环的下方（↓，向下指）。如果两个基团指向同一侧，则该化合物为顺式异构体；若指向不同侧，则为反式异构体。

How about the *trans*-1,2-dimethylcyclohexane? There are also two possible chair conformations:

> 反式-1,2-二甲基环己烷的情况又如何呢？同样也存在两种可能的椅式构象：

In one conformation both methyl groups are *axial*, in the other conformation both methyl groups are *equatorial*. These two conformers are **not** equivalent, and the di-*equatorial* one is the more stable conformation as we would expect.

> 在一种构象中，两个甲基都是轴向的；在另一种构象中，两个甲基都是赤道的。这两种构象并不等同，正如我们所预期的那样，二个甲基均为赤道的构象更为稳定。

*cis*-1-fluoro-4-isopropylcyclohexane is the structure with two different substituents. Both chair conformations have one *axial* substituent, and one *equatorial* substituent. According to the guideline, the conformer with *larger* substituent in *equatorial* is more stable because if the large group is axial, stronger steric strain will be generated and it is less stable.

> 顺式-1-氟-4-异丙基环己烷是一种具有两个不同取代基的化合物。两种椅式构象中，各有一个轴向取代基和一个赤道取代基。根据指导原则，赤道方向上取代基较大的构象更为稳定，因为如果大基团处于轴向位置，会产生更强的立体阻碍，从而使该构象不够稳定。

![](_page_141_Figure_6.jpeg)

#### 0.1.3 *Exercises 4.3*

> 0.1.3 习题 4.3

Determine which is the more stable isomer, *cis*-1-ethyl-2-methylcyclohexane or *trans*-1-ethyl-2-methylcyclohexane?

> 确定以下两种异构体中哪一种更稳定：顺-1-乙基-2-甲基环己烷还是反-1-乙基-2-甲基环己烷？

**Tips**: draw all the chair conformers of each isomer, and decide which is the most stable one.

> 提示：请画出每种异构体的所有椅式构象，并判断哪种最稳定。

Answers to Practice Questions Chapter 4

> 第四章练习题答案

# Answers to Practice Questions Chapter 4

> 第四章练习题答案

#### 0.1.1 **4.1** Solutions included in the section.

> 0.1.1 4.1 本节包含的溶液内容。

**4.2** Draw all conformers for 3-methylpentane by viewing along C2-C3 bond, and order them from the most stable to least stable.

> 4.2 以 C2-C3 键为轴，画出 3-甲基戊烷的所有构象，并按稳定性从高到低排列。

$$\begin{array}{cccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccc$$

> 

**4.3** Determine which is the more stable isomer, *cis*-1-ethyl-2-methylcyclohexane or *trans*-1-ethyl-2-methylcyclohexane?

> 4.3 确定下列两种异构体中哪一种更稳定：顺-1-乙基-2-甲基环己烷还是反-1-乙基-2-甲基环己烷？

The *trans*-isomer has the most stable conformer with both substituents are at equatorial positions, therefore *trans*-isomer is the more stable one.

> 顺式异构体具有两个取代基均处于赤道位置的最稳定构象，因此顺式异构体更为稳定。

# CHAPTER 5 STEREOCHEMISTRY

> 第五章 立体化学

The term stereoisomer has been introduced in **Chapter 4,** in the topic of cis/trans isomer of disubstituted cycloalkane. Stereoisomers are interesting phenomenon that exist in nature, also have great impact on the properties of organic molecules. In this chapter, we will have in depth discussions on stereoisomers and stereochemistry.

> 立体异构体这一术语在第4章中引入，当时讨论的是二取代环烷烃的顺反异构体。立体异构体是自然界中存在的有趣现象，对有机分子的性质也有重大影响。在本章中，我们将深入探讨立体异构体及立体化学。

# 5.1 Summary of Isomers

> 5.1 同分异构体总结

In stereochemistry topic, we will learn more different types of isomers. To clarify the concepts, it is a good idea to have a summary about the isomers in organic chemistry. There are two major types of isomers, **constitutional isomers** and **stereoisomers**. We have had detailed discussions on constitutional isomers in **Chapter 2**, and will focus on stereoisomers in this chapter. Stereoisomers are molecules with same bonding, but groups are in different spatial arrangement. At beginning of this chapter, we will learn more about geometric isomers in alkenes and the E/Z naming system. Then we will move on to a brand new category of stereoisomers, the isomers with chirality center. The flowchart here (**Fig. 5.1a**) show the correlation and difference between different types of isomers (pay attention to the definitions included) and provides useful guideline for the learning.

> 在立体化学这一主题中，我们将学习更多不同类型的异构体。为了明确概念，对有机化学中的异构体进行总结是一个很好的方法。异构体主要分为两大类：结构异构体和立体异构体。我们在第2章中已经对结构异构体进行了详细讨论，而本章将重点介绍立体异构体。立体异构体是指具有相同连接方式，但基团在空间中的排列方式不同的分子。在本章开始时，我们将进一步学习烯烃中的几何异构体以及E/Z命名系统。接着，我们将介绍一种全新的立体异构体类型——具有手性中心的异构体。此处的流程图（图5.1a）展示了不同类型异构体之间的关系与区别（请注意其中包含的定义），并为学习提供了有用的指导。

![](_page_148_Figure_2.jpeg)

*Fig. 5.1a Summarization of Isomers*

> 图5.1a 同分异构体总结

# 5.2 Geometric Isomers and E/Z Naming System

> 5.2 几何异构体与E/Z命名法

#### 0.1.1 **Geometric Isomers of Alkenes**

> 0.1.1 烯烃的几何异构体

In the discussions about 1,2-dimethylcyclohexane in **Chapter 4**, we have learned that there are two **geometric isomers** possible for that compound, that are *cis* and *trans*. The restricted C-C bond rotation of cyclic structure result in the *cis* or *trans* isomer of 1,2-dimethylcyclohexane. Restricted rotation also can be caused by a double bond, so geometric isomers apply to some alkenes as well.

> 在第4章关于1,2-二甲基环己烷的讨论中，我们已经了解到该化合物存在两种几何异构体，即顺式（cis）和反式（trans）。环状结构中碳-碳单键的旋转受到限制，从而导致了1,2-二甲基环己烷的顺式或反式异构体。同样，双键也会导致旋转受限，因此几何异构现象也适用于某些烯烃。

![](_page_149_Figure_3.jpeg)

*Figure 5.2a Geometric isomers of disubstituted cycloalkanes*

> 图5.2a 双取代环烷烃的几何异构体

For the example of 2-butene, the condensed structural formula CH3-CH=CH-CH3 does not really represent the trigonal planar shape of the sp<sup>2</sup> carbons with double bonds. To show the shape explicitly, we need to draw the Kekulé structure that show all the bond angles. Then it will be noticed that there are two different shapes of 2-butene, with the CH3 groups on either the same side or opposite side of the double bond.

> 以2-丁烯为例，其缩写结构式CH₃-CH=CH-CH₃并不能真正反映出sp²杂化碳原子（含双键）的三角形平面结构。为了明确展示这种结构，我们需要绘制凯库勒结构，以显示所有的键角。这时就会发现，2-丁烯有两种不同的构型，即两个CH₃基团位于双键的同侧或异侧。

![](_page_149_Figure_8.jpeg)

*Figure 5.2b Geometric isomers of some alkenes*

> 图5.2b 某些烯烃的几何异构体

They are geometric isomers and can be labelled as *cis* or *trans* in a similar way as disubstituted cycloalkane. *Cis*/*trans* is the common designation for geometric isomers and might be ambiguous for some structures, here we will learn the IUPAC naming system for geometric isomers of alkene, that is the *E/Z* naming system.

> 它们是几何异构体，可以像二取代环烷烃一样，用cis或trans进行标记。cis/trans是几何异构体的常见表示方法，但对某些结构可能产生歧义。在这里，我们将学习用于烯烃几何异构体的IUPAC命名系统，即E/Z命名法。

#### 0.1.2 *E/Z* **Naming System**

> 0.1.2 E/Z命名体系

To do the *E/Z* designation, at first, the groups connected on each sp<sup>2</sup> double bond carbon will be assigned the priority based on the atomic number (see following guidelines for details), then the isomer with same priority group on the same side of double bond is assigned as "*Z*", and the isomer with the same priority group on the opposite side of double bond is called "*E*". Both *E* and Z come from German, "**Zusammen**" means same side and "**Entgegen**" means opposite.

> 进行E/Z标记时，首先需要根据原子序数为每个sp²杂化碳原子上连接的基团确定优先级（详见以下指南），然后将双键两侧相同优先级基团位于同一侧的异构体标记为“Z”，将相同优先级基团位于双键两侧相反位置的异构体标记为“E”。E和Z均源自德语，“Zusammen”表示同侧，“Entgegen”表示异侧。

![](_page_150_Figure_0.jpeg)

### 0.2 **The guidelines for assigning group priority in E/Z naming system**

> 0.2 E/Z命名体系中基团优先级的判定规则

1. Priority is assigned based on the **atomic number** of the atoms bonded *directly* to the sp<sup>2</sup> double bond carbon, the larger the atomic number, the higher the priority (isotopes with higher mass number has higher priority). For example: S > O > N > C > H.

> 优先级的确定依据直接连接到 sp<sup>2</sup> 双键碳原子的原子序数，原子序数越大，优先级越高（同位素中质量数较大的优先级更高）。例如：S > O > N > C > H。

For the above structure of 2-penetene: on the left side sp<sup>2</sup> carbon, methyl group CH3 is higher than hydrogen atom because C > H; on the right side sp<sup>2</sup> carbon, ethyl group CH2CH3, is also higher than hydrogen. With higher priority group on both side of the double bond, this is the *Z* isomer**,** the complete name of the compound is **(***Z***)-2-pentene.**

> 对于上述的2-戊烯结构：在双键左侧的sp²杂化碳原子上，甲基CH₃的优先级高于氢原子，因为C > H；在双键右侧的sp²杂化碳原子上，乙基CH₂CH₃的优先级也高于氢原子。由于双键两侧都有较高优先级的取代基，因此该化合物为Z型异构体，其完整名称为(Z)-2-戊烯。

**The group with***higher* **priority is labelled as #1, and the group with** *lower* **priority is labelled as #2 in this book.**

> 在本书中，优先级较高的基团标记为#1，优先级较低的基团标记为#2。

2. If the two groups bonded directly on an sp<sup>2</sup> carbon start with the same atom, means there is a tie from step 1, then we move on to the atoms that connected to the "tied" atom, priority increases as the atomic number of the next attached atom increases.

> 如果两个基团直接连接在同一个sp²杂化碳原子上，并且起始原子相同，则说明在第一步中存在平级关系，此时应继续比较与“平级原子”相连的下一级原子，原子序数更大的原子具有更高的优先级。

For the above structure, it is obvious that Cl is higher than C (C of CH2CH<sup>3</sup> group) on the right side sp<sup>2</sup> carbon.

> 对于上述结构，显然氯原子（Cl）的电负性高于右侧sp²杂化碳原子（CH₂CH₃基团中的碳原子）。

On the left side sp<sup>2</sup> carbon, we need to compare between methyl CH3 group and ethyl CH2CH3 group. Both groups has carbon atom attached directly on the sp<sup>2</sup> carbon, that is a tie. In CH3 group, the carbon atom is bonded to **H**, **H**, **H**; while in CH2CH3 group, the carbon atom is bonded with **H**, **H**, **C**. So ethyl CH2CH3 is higher than methyl CH3 (see **Note** below). With higher priority group on opposite side of the double bond, this is the *E* isomer**,** the complete name of the compound is: **(***E***)-3-chloro-4-methyl-3-hexene.**

> 在双键左侧的 sp<sup>2</sup> 碳原子上，我们需要比较甲基（CH<sub>3</sub>）和乙基（CH<sub>2</sub>CH<sub>3</sub>）基团。这两个基团都直接连接到 sp<sup>2</sup> 碳原子上，因此平分秋色。在甲基中，碳原子连接的是三个氢原子（H、H、H）；而在乙基中，碳原子连接的是两个氢原子和一个碳原子（H、H、C）。因此，乙基（CH<sub>2</sub>CH<sub>3</sub>）的优先级高于甲基（CH<sub>3</sub>）（见下方注释）。当较高优先级的基团位于双键的两侧时，该化合物为 E 异构体，该化合物的完整名称为：(E)-3-氯-4-甲基-3-己烯。

**Note #1**: For this round of comparison between **H, H, H** and **H, H, C**, compare the single atom with the greatest number in one group *verse* the single atom with the greatest number in the other group. So **H** in one group verse **C** in the other group, since C > H, therefore CH2CH3 is higher than CH3. Remember do **not** add the atomic numbers. For example, if one group has **C**, **C**, **C**, and the other group has **C, O, H**, then the C, O, H side is higher because O is higher than C.

> 注 #1：在这次 H、H、H 与 H、H、C 的比较中，应将一组中出现次数最多的单原子与另一组中出现次数最多的单原子进行比较。例如，将一组中的 H 与另一组中的 C 进行比较，由于 C 的优先级高于 H，因此 CH₂CH₃ 的优先级高于 CH₃。请注意，不要将原子序数相加。例如，若一组中有 C、C、C，另一组中有 C、O、H，则 O 所在的一组优先级更高，因为 O 的优先级高于 C。

**Note #2**: The above compound is *cis*-isomer if using the cis/trans naming system (both ethyl group are on the same side of double bond), but is *E*-isomer for E/Z system. So the cis/trans and E/Z are two different naming systems, don't always match.

> 注释 #2：上述化合物若使用 cis/trans 命名法（双键两侧的乙基位于同一侧），则为 cis-异构体；但若使用 E/Z 命名法，则为 E-异构体。因此，cis/trans 与 E/Z 是两种不同的命名体系，二者并不总是对应一致。

3. Repeat step 2 if necessary, until the priority is assigned.

> 如有必要，重复步骤2，直至优先级被分配。
