The basis for NMR is the phenomenon that some atomic nuclei spin about their axes and as a result generate their own magnetic field, or **magnetic moment**, therefore these nuclei are called **NMR-active**. Not all nuclei have a magnetic moment though, only those nuclei with an odd number of proton and/or neutron have. Fortunately nuclei that are important for organic compounds, such as the <sup>1</sup>H isotope of hydrogen, the <sup>13</sup>C isotope of carbon, the <sup>14</sup>N isotope of nitrogen, <sup>19</sup>F and the <sup>31</sup>P are all NMR-active and therefore can be observed by NMR. Other nuclei, such as the common <sup>12</sup>C isotopes of carbon and <sup>16</sup>O isotope of oxygen, do not have magnetic moments, and cannot be directly observed by NMR.

> 核磁共振（NMR）的基础是某些原子核围绕其轴旋转，并因此产生自身的磁场，或者说磁矩，因此这些原子核被称为NMR活性核。并非所有原子核都具有磁矩，只有那些质子和/或中子数目为奇数的原子核才具有磁矩。幸运的是，对于有机化合物而言，重要的原子核，如氢的<sup>1</sup>H同位素、碳的<sup>13</sup>C同位素、氮的<sup>14</sup>N同位素、氟的<sup>19</sup>F同位素以及磷的<sup>31</sup>P同位素，都是NMR活性核，因此可以通过核磁共振技术观察到。而其他一些原子核，如碳的常见同位素<sup>12</sup>C和氧的常见同位素<sup>16</sup>O，并没有磁矩，因此无法直接通过NMR观察到。

![](_page_211_Figure_4.jpeg)

*Figure 6.5a The magnetic field*

> 图6.5a 磁场

In practice, the <sup>1</sup>H and <sup>13</sup>C nuclei are most commonly observed by NMR spectroscopy, and we will focus on these techniques in this chapter, beginning with <sup>1</sup>H NMR. <sup>1</sup>H NMR is usually called proton NMR, because the nucleus of 1H atom is actually a single proton. The name of 'proton' and 'hydrogen' will be used interchangeably in this chapter for <sup>1</sup>H NMR purpose.

> 在实际应用中，<sup>1</sup>H 和 <sup>13</sup>C 核最常通过核磁共振（NMR）光谱进行观察，本章将重点介绍这两种技术，首先从 <sup>1</sup>H NMR 开始。由于 <sup>1</sup>H 原子的核实际上是一个单独的质子，因此 <sup>1</sup>H NMR 通常也被称为质子 NMR。在本章中，为了 <sup>1</sup>H NMR 的目的，“质子”和“氢”这两个术语将交替使用。

#### 0.1.2 **Spin State and Magnetic Resonance**

> 0.1.2 自旋态与磁共振

We will take proton, the nucleus of <sup>1</sup>H atom, as an example for the discussions here.

> 我们将以质子（<sup>1</sup>H原子的原子核）作为此处讨论的例子。

When a sample of an organic compound is sitting in a flask on a laboratory bench, the magnetic moments of all of its protons are oriented randomly. However, when the same sample is placed within the field of a strong magnet in an NMR instrument (this field is referred to as the **applied external magnetic field, B0,** in NMR), each proton will assume one of two possible orientations with respect to the external magnetic field. These two orientations corresponds to the two spin states that can be labelled as α and β. In the α spin state, the proton's magnetic moment is aligned *with* the direction of external magnetic field B0, while in the β spin state it is aligned *opposed to* the direction of B0 (**Fig. 6.5b**).

> 当一个有机化合物样品放置在实验台上的烧瓶中时，其所有质子的磁矩都是随机取向的。然而，当同一样品被置于核磁共振（NMR）仪器的强磁场中时（该磁场在NMR中被称为外加磁场，记作B0），每个质子将相对于外加磁场采取两种可能的取向之一。这两种取向对应于两种自旋状态，分别标记为α和β。在α自旋状态下，质子的磁矩与外加磁场B0的方向一致；而在β自旋状态下，质子的磁矩方向则与B0相反（见图6.5b）。

![](_page_212_Figure_1.jpeg)

*Figure 6.5b Orientations of magnetic moments of protons without and with external magnetic field*

> 图6.5b 无外加磁场和有外加磁场时质子磁矩的取向

The α spin state is slightly lower in energy than the β state, and the energy gap between them, ΔE, depends upon the strength of B0: a stronger applied external magnetic field results in a larger ΔE. For a large population of organic molecules in an external magnetic field, slightly *more* than half of the protons will occupy the lower energy α spin state, while slightly *less* than half will occupy the higher energy β spin state. It is this population difference between the two spin states that is exploited by NMR, and the difference increases with the strength of the applied magnetic field B0.

> α自旋态的能量略低于β态，两者之间的能量差ΔE取决于外加磁场B0的强度：外加磁场越强，ΔE越大。在外部磁场中，大量有机分子的自旋态中，略多于一半的质子会处于较低能量的α自旋态，而略少于一半的质子会处于较高能量的β自旋态。核磁共振（NMR）正是利用了这两种自旋态之间的这种粒子数差异，且这种差异随外加磁场B0的强度增加而增大。

Energy is required to excite the proton from the lower energy state (α spin state) to the higher energy state (β spin state). In an NMR spectrometer the energy is supplied by electromagnetic radiation in the radio frequency (RF) region. When a proton in an external magnetic field is exposed to RF radiation with the energy that matches the energy gap ΔE, the energy of the RF is absorbed and the proton will flip its magnetic moment from the lower energy state (α spin state) to the higher energy state (β spin state), the nuclei are said to be in **resonance** with the electromagnetic radiation.

> 激发质子从较低能量状态（α自旋态）跃迁到较高能量状态（β自旋态）需要能量。在核磁共振（NMR）谱仪中，这种能量由射频（RF）区域的电磁辐射提供。当处于外部磁场中的质子受到与能量差ΔE相对应的射频辐射时，质子会吸收射频能量，其磁矩从较低能量状态（α自旋态）跃迁到较高能量状态（β自旋态），此时核被称作与电磁辐射产生共振。

![](_page_212_Figure_5.jpeg)

*Figure 6.5c Resonance*

> 图6.5c 共轭

The frequency of radiation absorbed by a proton (or any other nucleus) during a spin transition in the NMR experiment is called its **resonance frequency, ν**. As a result, the resonance frequency also depends on B0, the larger B0 the higher resonance frequency, and the relationship fits to the specific formula: (**Formula 6.4** is for your information purpose only)

> 在核磁共振（NMR）实验中，质子（或其他任何原子核）在自旋跃迁过程中所吸收的电磁辐射的频率称为其共振频率，记作 ν。因此，共振频率也取决于静磁场 B₀，B₀ 越强，共振频率越高，这种关系符合特定的公式：（公式 6.4 仅用于说明）

$$u = \frac{\gamma B_0}{2\pi}$$
 Formula 6.4

> 式 6.4

γ is the magnetogyric (or gyromagnetic) ratio, different nucleus has different value of γ. For a proton, the γ value is 26.753 rad · s-1 · tesla-1 .

> γ 是磁旋比（或称旋磁比），不同原子核具有不同的 γ 值。对于一个质子，其 γ 值为 26.753 rad·s⁻¹·tesla⁻¹。

Calculations indicate that if external magnetic field B0≅1.41 Tesla, the energy difference corresponds to RF with the frequency of 60×10<sup>6</sup> Hz (60 MHz) for proton; when B0≅7.04 Tesla, the corresponding RF frequency is 300×10<sup>6</sup> Hz (300 MHz) for proton. This frequency is the most important parameter for a NMR spectrometer (the instrument that run NMR experiments), the higher the frequency, the more sensitive the instrument and the higher resolution the resulting NMR spectrum is.

> 计算表明，当外加磁场 B0 ≅ 1.41 特斯拉时，质子的能级差对应于频率为 60×10<sup>6</sup> Hz（60 MHz）的射频（RF）波；当 B0 ≅ 7.04 特斯拉时，对应频率为 300×10<sup>6</sup> Hz（300 MHz）的射频波。这一频率是核磁共振（NMR）谱仪（用于进行核磁共振实验的仪器）最重要的参数之一。频率越高，仪器的灵敏度越高，所获得的核磁共振谱的分辨率也越高。

### 0.2 **The NMR Experiment**

> 0.2 核磁共振实验

In this book we will just explain how the NMR experiment and NMR spectrometer work in a simplified way (again with proton as an example), the full version is out of the scope of this course.

> 在本书中，我们将以简化的形式（仍以氢核为例）简要介绍核磁共振（NMR）实验和核磁共振仪的工作原理，完整的内容超出了本课程的范围。

When a sample of compound is placed in the strong applied external magnetic field **B0** of the instrument, the protons begin to spin with one of the two spin states. Initially, slightly more than half of the protons have the magnetic moments in aspin states (aligned with **B0**), and slightly less than half are in bspin states (aligned against **B0**). Then, the sample is exposed to a range of radio frequencies. Out of all of the frequencies which hit the sample, only the frequencies that matches the resonance frequency of the protons are absorbed, causing those protons which are aligned with **B0** to 'spin flip' so that they align themselves against **B0**. When the 'flipped' protons flip back down to their ground state, they emit energy, again in the form of radio-frequency radiation. The NMR instrument detects and records the frequency and intensity of this radiation by making using of a mathematical technique known as a Fourier transform (FT). Fourier Transform convert the signal from a time *versus* amplitude signals to a frequency *versus* amplitude signals, that is what we observe in a NMR spectrum.

> 当样品被置于仪器的强外部磁场 $ B_0 $ 中时，质子开始以两种自旋状态之一进行自旋。最初，略多于一半的质子处于 $ a $ 自旋态（磁矩与 $ B_0 $ 方向一致），而略少于一半的质子处于 $ b $ 自旋态（磁矩与 $ B_0 $ 方向相反）。随后，样品被暴露在一系列射频范围内。所有照射到样品的频率中，只有与质子共振频率相匹配的频率才会被吸收，导致那些与 $ B_0 $ 方向一致的质子发生“自旋翻转”，从而使其磁矩方向变为与 $ B0 $ 相反。当这些“翻转”的质子重新回到基态时，它们会以射频辐射的形式释放能量。核磁共振（NMR）仪器通过一种称为傅里叶变换（FT）的数学技术检测并记录这种辐射的频率和强度。傅里叶变换将信号从时间与振幅的关系转换为频率与振幅的关系，这就是我们在核磁共振谱中所观察到的内容。

![](_page_213_Figure_6.jpeg)

*Figure 6.5d Simplified diagrams to illustrate NMR experiment*

> 图6.5d NMR实验的简化示意图

Most modern FT-NMR spectrometers use superconducting magnets that have very high magnetic fields, therefore operate with high resonance frequency from 100 MHz to 800 MHz. Superconducting magnets operate in a bath of liquid nitrogen or liquid helium at very low temperature.

> 大多数现代傅里叶变换核磁共振（FT-NMR）光谱仪使用超导磁体，其具有非常高的磁场，因此能够以100 MHz至800 MHz的高共振频率运行。超导磁体在液氮或液氦的低温环境中运行。

![](_page_214_Picture_0.jpeg)

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_214_Picture_1.jpeg)

*Figure 6.5e FT-NMR with superconducting magnet and a model of bench top NMR: NMReady-60*

> 图6.5e FT-NMR配备超导磁体及台式NMR模型：NMReady-60

Despite the powerfulness and high resolution of the high frequency NMR spectrometers, it is very costly for purchase and maintenance of the instrument. For teaching purpose, the bench top NMR are becoming more and more popular recently. The frequency of bench top NMR are usually in the range of 60-90 MHz, however, they can provide spectra with good resolution for lots basic organic structures that are used for undergraduate organic chemistry class. With the low-cost bench top NMR available, students have chance to gain hand-on NMR experiences in sample preparation, instrument operation and spectrum processing.

> 尽管高频核磁共振（NMR）光谱仪具有强大的性能和高分辨率，但其购置和维护成本非常高。为了教学目的，近年来台式NMR仪器正变得越来越流行。台式NMR仪器的频率通常在60-90 MHz之间，然而它们仍能为许多用于本科生有机化学课程的基本有机结构提供具有良好分辨率的谱图。随着低成本台式NMR仪器的出现，学生有机会在样品制备、仪器操作和谱图处理等方面获得实际的NMR实验经验。

#### 0.2.1 **Shielding and Deshielding**

> 0.2.1 屏蔽与去屏蔽

If all hydrogen atoms (and protons) in organic molecules had the same resonance frequency, then they all show the same signal, NMR spectroscopy would not be that useful for chemists. Fortunately, however, resonance frequencies are different for different protons in a molecule. Specifically, the resonance frequency varies according to the electronic environment that a given proton inhabits.

> 如果有机分子中的所有氢原子（和质子）都具有相同的共振频率，那么它们都会表现出相同的信号，核磁共振（NMR）光谱学对化学家来说就不会那么有用。幸运的是，分子中不同质子的共振频率是不同的。具体来说，某一质子的共振频率会根据它所处的电子环境而有所不同。

For hydrogen atoms in any bonds, such as C-H, O-H etc, the external magnetic field **B0** causes the s electrons to circulate in a way that generate an induced **local magnetic field** (**Blocal**) at the proton, and the direction of the local field Blocal is opposite to the external field B0. The proton thus experiences a net magnetic field, which is called **Beff**, that is smaller than the applied magnetic field:

> 对于任何化学键中的氢原子，例如C-H、O-H等，外加磁场B0会使s电子产生循环运动，从而在质子处产生一个诱导的局部磁场（Blocal）。该局部磁场Blocal的方向与外加磁场B0的方向相反。因此，质子所经历的净磁场（称为Beff）比外加磁场要小：

**Beff= B0 – Blocal**

> Bₑff = B₀ – Bₗₒₐₗ

As a result, the proton responses to a lower frequency (resonance frequency is proportional to the magnetic field as mentioned early). This Blocal, to a small but significant degree, shield the proton from experiencing the full force of **B0**, so this effect is called **shielding effect**. Different hydrogen atoms in organic structures are in different electronic environment, have different selectron density, therefore have different Blocal and different Beff as well. That is why different hydrogens (and protons) are in different resonance frequency and show different signals in the spectrum.

> 因此，质子对较低频率的响应（共振频率如前所述与磁场成正比）。这种局部磁场 Blocal 在一定程度上（虽然较小但具有显著性）屏蔽了质子，使其无法完全感受到 B0 的作用，因此这种效应被称为屏蔽效应。有机分子中不同的氢原子处于不同的电子环境中，具有不同的电子密度，因此它们的 Blocal 也不同，导致 Beff 不同。这就是为什么不同的氢原子（和质子）具有不同的共振频率，并在谱图中表现出不同的信号。

![](_page_215_Picture_0.jpeg)

*Figure 6.5f Shielding effect*

> 图6.5f 屏蔽效应

For hydrogen atoms close to electronegative groups, electronegative groups withdraw electron density from nearby atoms, so diminishing the shielding of the protons by circulating electrons. The hydrogen atoms near an electronegative groups are said to be **deshielded** from the external magnetic field, and have a higher resonance frequency than those shielded protons. As the electronegativity of the substituent increase, so does the extent of the deshielding effect (and so the chemical shift, see **section 6.6.2** for more discussions about chemical shift) as shown in the examples below.

> 对于靠近电负性基团的氢原子，电负性基团会从邻近的原子中拉出电子密度，从而减弱环流电子对质子的屏蔽作用。靠近电负性基团的氢原子被认为是从外部磁场中去屏蔽的，因此它们的共振频率比被屏蔽的质子更高。随着取代基的电负性增加，去屏蔽效应的程度也随之增加（因此化学位移也会增大，有关化学位移的更多讨论请参见第6.6.2节）。以下示例展示了这一点。

*Figure 6.5g H atoms get more deshielded with electronegativity of substituent increase*

> 图6.5g 取代基的电负性增加时，氢原子的屏蔽效应减弱

*Figure 6.5h H atoms get more deshielded with more electronegativity substituents involved*

> 图6.5h 氢原子随着参与的电负性取代基增多而变得更为去屏蔽

# 6.6 ¹H NMR Spectra and Interpretation (Part I)

> 6.6 ¹H 核磁共振谱及其解析（第一部分）

Understanding the basics of NMR theory gets us ready to move on to the most important and practical part in this section, that is how to understand the 1H NMR spectrum and elucidate the structure of a compound from 1H NMR spectrum information. Let's first take a look at an actual 1H NMR spectrum.

> 理解NMR理论的基础知识，使我们能够进入本节中最重要且实用的部分，即如何理解1H NMR谱图，并从1H NMR谱图信息中推断化合物的结构。首先，让我们看一下一个实际的1H NMR谱图。

![](_page_217_Figure_2.jpeg)

*Fig. 6.6a The 1H NMR spectrum of methyl acetate*

> 图6.6a 甲乙酮的1H NMR谱图

Generally, the information about the structure of molecule can be obtained from four aspects of a typical <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectrum:

> 通常，可以从典型的<sup>1</sup>H NMR 谱图的四个方面获得有关分子结构的信息：

- Chemical equivalent and non-equivalent protons (total number of signals)
- Chemical shift
- Integration
- Signal splitting

> 化学等价与非等价质子（总信号数目）  
化学位移  
积分值  
信号分裂

### 0.1 **6.6.1 Chemical Equivalent and Non-Equivalent Protons**

> 0.1 6.6.1 化学等价与非等价质子

In the above <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectrum of methyl acetate (**Fig. 6.6a**), we can see that there are three signals. The peak at the far right is for the standard reference compound tetramethylsilane (TMS, more discussions in chemical shift section **6.6.2**), not for the compound. So the compound methyl acetate shows two signals in <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectrum. Why only two signals for a compound containing total six hydrogens?

> 在上述甲乙酸甲酯的<sup>1</sup>H NMR谱（图6.6a）中，我们可以看到有三个信号。最右侧的峰对应的是标准参考物质四甲基硅烷（TMS，有关化学位移的详细讨论见第6.6.2节），并非甲乙酸甲酯本身。因此，甲乙酸甲酯在<sup>1</sup>H NMR谱中显示两个信号。为什么一个含有六个氢原子的化合物在NMR谱中只显示两个信号？

This is because of chemical equivalence. The total six hydrogens can be divided to two groups, the three **Ha** protons in the methyl group that bonded with C=O are all in the same chemical environment, therefore they are chemical equivalent. All chemical equivalent hydrogens have the same resonance frequency with applied to an external magnetic field, so show only one signal in <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectrum. The three **<sup>H</sup><sup>b</sup>** protons in the methyl group bonded with O atom are chemical equivalent as well and show the other signal. That is why there are total two signals for compound methyl acetate.

> 这是因为化学等价性。总共有六个氢原子可以分为两组，甲基中与羰基（C=O）相连的三个Ha质子处于相同的化学环境，因此它们是化学等价的。所有化学等价的氢原子在施加外部磁场时具有相同的共振频率，因此在<sup>1</sup>H NMR谱中只显示一个信号。甲基中与氧原子相连的三个Hb质子同样也是化学等价的，显示另一个信号。这就是为什么乙酸甲酯这种化合物在<sup>1</sup>H NMR谱中总共显示两个信号的原因。

The ability to recognize chemical equivalent and non-equivalent protons in a molecule is very important in understanding NMR spectrum. For the compound with structure given, we should be able to predict how many signals are there in <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectrum. On the other side, if the <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectrum is available for an unknown compound, counting the number of signals in the spectrum tells us the number of different sets of protons in the molecule, and that is the very important information to determine the structure of the compound.

> 能够识别分子中化学等价和非等价质子的能力，对于理解核磁共振（NMR）谱非常重要。对于具有给定结构的化合物，我们应该能够预测其<sup>1</sup>H NMR谱中会出现多少个信号。另一方面，如果已知一个未知化合物的<sup>1</sup>H NMR谱，通过统计谱中信号的数量，就可以得知该分子中不同质子组的数量，这一信息对于确定化合物的结构具有非常重要的意义。

Here we will go through several examples for the first situation, that is to predict the number of signals in <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectrum with the structure of a compound given. To do that, we need to count how many distinct proton sets are included in the molecule.

> 在这里，我们将通过几个例子来分析第一种情况，即已知化合物的结构，预测其<sup>1</sup>H NMR谱中信号的数量。要做到这一点，我们需要统计分子中包含多少个不同的质子组。

For each of the following molecule, the chemically equivalent protons are labelled in the same *color* to facilitate the understanding.

> 以下各分子中，化学等价的质子均以相同颜色标记，以便于理解。

$$\begin{array}{cccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccc$$

> 

- Benzene: all six protons are chemical equivalent (have the same bonding and in the same chemical environment) to each other and have the same resonance frequency in an <sup>1</sup>H NMR experiment, therefore show only **one** signal.
- Acetone: both methyl groups (two CH3) bonded with C=O bond, so they are in the same chemical environment, and as a result all the six protons are chemical equivalent that show only **one** signal.

> 苯：所有六个质子在化学上等价（具有相同的键合方式且处于相同的化学环境），在<sup>1</sup>H NMR实验中它们具有相同的共振频率，因此只显示一个信号。  
丙酮：两个甲基（两个CH<sub>3</sub>）都与C=O键相连，因此它们处于相同的化学环境，结果六个氢原子在化学上等价，只显示一个信号。

**Notes: As you probably already realized, chemical equivalence or non-equivalence in NMR is closely related to** *symmetry***. The protons that are symmetric to each other by a certain plane of symmetry are chemical equivalent.**

> 注：正如你可能已经意识到的，核磁共振（NMR）中化学等价或非等价与对称性密切相关。若某些质子通过某一镜面对称，那么这些质子是化学等价的。

The molecules in the next figure contains more sets of chemically equivalent protons.

> 下图中的分子包含更多组化学等价质子。

$$\begin{array}{c} H_{a} & O \\ H_{a} - C - C - H_{b} \\ H_{a} \end{array} \qquad \begin{array}{c} H_{a} \\ C - C \\ H_{a} \end{array} \qquad \begin{array}{c} CH_{3} \\ C - C \\ H_{3} \end{array} \qquad \begin{array}{c} CH_{3} \\ C - C \\ H_{4} \end{array} \qquad \begin{array}{c} CH_{3} \\ C - C \\ H_{4} \end{array} \qquad \begin{array}{c} CH_{3} \\ C - C \\ H_{4} \end{array} \qquad \begin{array}{c} CH_{3} \\ C - C \\ H_{5} \end{array} \qquad \begin{array}{c} CH_{3} \\ C - C \\ H_{5} \end{array} \qquad \begin{array}{c} CH_{3} \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ H_{5} \end{array} \qquad \begin{array}{c} CH_{3} \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ H_{5} \end{array} \qquad \begin{array}{c} CH_{3} \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ H_{5} \end{array} \qquad \begin{array}{c} CH_{3} \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \end{array} \qquad \begin{array}{c} CH_{3} \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C - C \\ C -$$

> 

- Acetaldehyde: The three Ha protons in the methyl group are chemical equivalent, and they all bonded to an *sp* 3 -hybridized carbon; but they are different to the Hb proton that is bonded to an *sp* 2 *–*hybridized carbonyl carbon. **Two** signals total in <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectrum.
- 1,4-dimethylbenzene: all four aromatic protons in are chemically equivalent because of the symmetry. The two methyl groups are equivalent to each other as well. **Two** signals total in <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectrum.
- 1,2-dimethylbenzene: both Ha protons are adjacent to a methyl substituent, while both Hc protons are two carbons away. So the four aromatic protons are divided to *two* sets. Both methyl groups are in the same bonding and symmetric to each other, they are equivalent. **Three** signals total in <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectrum.
- 1,3-dimethylbenzene: Hb is situated between two methyl groups, the two Hc protons are one carbon away from a methyl group, and Hd is two carbons away from a methyl group. Therefore, the four aromatic protons can be divided to *three* sets. The two methyl groups are equivalent. **Four** signals total in <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectrum.

> 乙醛：甲基上的三个Ha质子化学等价，它们都连接在sp³杂化碳原子上；但它们与连接在sp²杂化羰基碳原子上的Hb质子不同。¹H NMR谱中出现两个信号。

1,4-二甲基苯：由于对称性，苯环上的四个芳香质子化学等价。两个甲基也彼此等价。¹H NMR谱中出现两个信号。

1,2-二甲基苯：两个Ha质子邻近甲基取代基，而两个Hc质子距离甲基取代基有两个碳原子。因此，四个芳香质子可分为两组。两个甲基在化学环境上相同且互为对称，因此等价。¹H NMR谱中出现三个信号。

1,3-二甲基苯：Hb质子位于两个甲基之间，两个Hc质子距离一个甲基有一个碳原子，而Hd质子距离一个甲基有两个碳原子。因此，四个芳香质子可分为三组。两个甲基等价。¹H NMR谱中出现四个信号。

# *Exercises 6.1*

> 练习 6.1

How many <sup>1</sup>H NMR signals would you predict for each of the following molecules?

> 你预计以下每个分子会产生多少个<sup>1</sup>H NMR信号？

$$A$$
  $B$   $A$   $C$   $C$   $C$   $C$   $C$   $C$   $C$   $C$   $C$   $C$

> 

Answers to Practice Questions Chapter 6

> 第六章练习题答案

### 0.1 **6.6.2 Chemical Shift**

> 0.1 6.6.2 化学位移

As seen in the <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectrum of methyl acetate (**Fig. 6.6a**), the *x*-axis units of NMR spectrum are in ppm (not in Hz as we would expect for frequency), and the two signals stand at different position along the *x*-axis. Let's explain how that works and what information can be obtained.

> 如图6.6a所示的甲乙酸甲酯的<sup>1</sup>H NMR谱图，NMR谱图的x轴单位为ppm（而非我们通常预期的频率单位Hz），谱图中两个信号在x轴上占据不同的位置。下面我们来解释这种现象是如何产生的，以及从中可以获得哪些信息。

The position of a signal along the *x*-axis of an NMR spectra is called **chemical shift,** or **δ,** of the signal. Chemical shift is determined by the structural electronical environment of the nuclei producing that signal. Protons in different chemical environments (non-equivalent) show signals at different chemical shift. The *direction* of chemical shift scale in *x*-axis is opposite to what we are familiar with, that is the smaller value is at right-hand side, and the larger value is at the lefthand side (**Fig. 6.6b**).

> 在核磁共振谱（NMR谱）的x轴上，信号的位置称为该信号的化学位移，或用δ表示。化学位移由产生该信号的核所处的结构电子环境决定。处于不同化学环境（非等价）的质子会表现出不同的化学位移。x轴上化学位移的标度方向与我们习惯的方向相反，即数值较小的位于右侧，数值较大的位于左侧（图6.6b）。

- Smaller chemical shift (**δ**) values correspond with lower resonance frequency;
- Larger chemical shift (**δ**) values correspond with higher resonance frequency.

> 较小的化学位移（δ）值对应较低的共振频率；较大的化学位移（δ）值对应较高的共振频率。

By **convention**, the right-hand side of an NMR spectrum with smaller chemical shift values is called **upfield**, and the left-hand direction is called **downfield** (**Fig. 6.6b**).

> 按照惯例，核磁共振（NMR）谱图中化学位移值较小的一侧称为上场区（upfield），而化学位移值较大的一侧则称为下场区（downfield）（见图6.6b）。

![](_page_220_Figure_7.jpeg)

*Figure 6.6b The chemical shift scale in H NMR spectra*

> 图6.6b 核磁共振氢谱的化学位移标尺

For protons that are **shielded**, because of the Blocal caused by circulating electrons, the magnetic field experienced by the proton, Beff, is smaller than applied external field, Bo, so the protons resonance at lower frequency and have smaller chemical shift values.

> 对于被电子环流产生的局部磁场（Blocal）屏蔽的质子来说，质子所经历的有效磁场（Beff）小于外加的外部磁场（Bo），因此这些质子在较低的频率下发生共振，并具有较小的化学位移值。

- Shielded protons have lower resonance frequency, and smaller chemical shift (**d**) values;
- Deshielded protons have higher resonance frequency, and larger chemical shift (**d**) values.

> 被屏蔽的质子具有较低的共振频率，且化学位移（δ）值较小；  
去屏蔽的质子具有较高的共振频率，且化学位移（δ）值较大。

In 1H NMR spectrum, the absorption of the protons of **TMS** (tetramethylsilane) is defined as "**zero**" on the chemical shift (**δ**) scale, and the absorption of other protons are reported as relative shift compared with that of TMS.

> 在1H NMR谱中，四甲基硅烷（TMS）的质子吸收被定义为化学位移（δ）标尺上的“零”，其他质子的吸收则以相对于TMS的化学位移进行报告。

**TMS** was chosen as a reference compound and defined as "**zero**" for several reasons. Since silicon is less

> TMS 被选作参考化合物，并被定义为“零”值，原因有以下几点。由于硅的电负性较低，

electronegative than carbon, the hydrogens of TMS are in high electron-density environment, therefore are highly shielded with very low resonance frequency and rarely interfere with the signals of other compounds. Also there are twelve equivalent hydrogens in TMS that show a *single* signal, so the signal is rather strong even with very little amount of TMS. TMS is also quite inert and easy to be removed with the boiling point of 27 ºC. A small amount of TMS was used to be added in the sample as an internal standard for NMR measurement, and removed by evaporation afterwards. However, for contemporary NMR spectrometer (including the bench top NMR), it is no longer necessary to actually add TMS since the computer can calibrate the chemical shift electronically based on resonance frequencies of the solvent used.

> 由于硅烷基三甲基硅烷（TMS）中的氢原子比碳更具电负性，因此这些氢原子处于高电子密度环境中，被强烈屏蔽，共振频率非常低，与其他化合物的信号干扰极少。此外，TMS中含有十二个等效的氢原子，表现出单一信号，因此即使仅加入少量TMS，其信号也非常强。TMS还具有良好的惰性，且沸点仅为27 ºC，易于通过蒸馏去除。过去常在样品中加入少量TMS作为核磁共振（NMR）测量的内标物，之后通过蒸馏将其去除。然而，对于现代核磁共振仪（包括便携式NMR仪器），已无需实际添加TMS，因为计算机可根据所用溶剂的共振频率，通过电子方式校准化学位移。

$$CH_3$$
 $CH_3$ 
 $CH_3$ 
 $CH_3$ 
 $CH_3$

> 

The unit of chemical shift (**δ**) is **ppm**. The 'ppm' label stands for 'parts per million'. The chemical shift relative to TMS in ppm is defined as the formula below.

> 化学位移（δ）的单位是 ppm。"ppm" 这个单位表示的是 "百万分之一"。相对于四甲基硅烷（TMS）的化学位移，以 ppm 表示，其定义如下公式所示。

$$S = \frac{\text{distance of peak from TMS in Hz}}{\text{spectrometer frequency in MHz}}$$

> 

The reason for using a relative value of chemical shift in ppm, rather than the actual resonance frequency in Hz is that every NMR instrument will have a different magnetic field strength, so the actual value of resonance frequencies expressed in Hz will be different on different instruments – remember that ΔE for the magnetic transition of a nucleus depends upon the strength of the externally applied magnetic field Bo. However, the chemical shift expressed in ppm will always be the same whether measured with an instrument operating at 400 MHz or 60 MHz. In the <sup>1</sup>H NMR of methyl acetate, the two signals are at 2.0 and 3.6 ppm represents the two sets of protons in methyl acetate have resonance frequencies about 2.0 and 3.6 parts per million higher than the resonance frequency of the TMS protons. If, for example, the spectrum is measured by the 400 MHz NMR spectrometer, then the chemical shift in Hz will be 800 Hz and 1440 Hz respectively.

> 使用化学位移的相对值（ppm）而不是实际共振频率（Hz）的原因在于，每台核磁共振（NMR）仪器的磁场强度都不同，因此以Hz为单位表示的实际共振频率在不同仪器上会有所不同——请记住，核素磁性跃迁的ΔE值取决于外加磁场的强度Bo。然而，以ppm表示的化学位移在使用400 MHz或60 MHz仪器测量时始终是相同的。在乙酸甲酯的<sup>1</sup>H NMR谱中，两个信号分别位于2.0和3.6 ppm处，表示乙酸甲酯中的两组质子的共振频率比四甲基硅烷（TMS）质子的共振频率分别高约2.0和3.6 ppm。例如，如果使用400 MHz的NMR仪器进行测量，则相应的化学位移以Hz为单位分别为800 Hz和1440 Hz。

Most protons in organic compounds have chemical shift values between 0 and 12 ppm relative to TMS, although values below 0 ppm and above 12 ppm are occasionally observed. The chemical shift value of hydrogens in certain structural environment, or common organic functional groups, are listed in chart (**Fig. 6.6c**) and table (**Table 6.2**) below.

> 有机化合物中的大多数质子化学位移值相对于TMS在0到12 ppm之间，尽管偶尔也会观察到低于0 ppm或高于12 ppm的数值。某些结构环境中氢原子或常见有机官能团的化学位移值列于下文的图表（图6.6c）和表格（表6.2）中。

![](_page_222_Figure_0.jpeg)

*Figure 6.6c Chart of Approximate proton Chemical Shifts*

> 图6.6c 近似质子化学位移图

| Type of Proton                       | Chemical Shift<br>(ppm) | Type of Proton                        | Chemical Shift (ppm) |
|--------------------------------------|-------------------------|---------------------------------------|----------------------|
| R—CH <sub>3</sub>                    | 0.9 – 1.2               | X—CH <sub>2</sub> R<br>(X: Cl, Br, I) | 3.1 – 3.8            |
| R<br>I<br>R—CH₂                      | 1.2 – 1.5               | R—OH                                  | variable, 1 – 5      |
| R<br> <br>  R—CH<br> <br>  R         | 1.4 – 1.9               | R—NH <sub>2</sub>                     | variable, 1 – 5      |
| R C=C CHR <sub>2</sub>               | 1.5 – 2.5               | R R R                                 | 4.5 – 6.0            |
| O<br>II<br>C<br>C<br>CH <sub>3</sub> | 2.0 – 2.6               | Ar— <b>H</b>                          | 6.0 – 8.5            |
| Ar — CH <sub>3</sub>                 | 2.2 – 2.5               | O II C H                              | 9.5 – 10.5           |
| R—C≡C—H                              | 2.5 - 3.0               | O<br>II<br>C<br>OH                    | 10 – 13              |
| (H)R—O—C <mark>H<sub>3</sub></mark>  | 3.3 - 4.0               | 3                                     |                      |

> | 质子类型                       | 化学位移（ppm） | 质子类型                        | 化学位移（ppm） |
|--------|----------------|----------------|----------------|
| R—CH₃                         | 0.9 – 1.2       | X—CH₂R<br>(X: Cl, Br, I)         | 3.1 – 3.8       |
| R<br>I<br>R—CH₂                | 1.2 – 1.5       | R—OH                              | 可变，1 – 5     |
| R<br> <br>R—CH<br> <br>R        | 1.4 – 1.9       | R—NH₂                             | 可变，1 – 5     |
| R C=C CHR₂                    | 1.5 – 2.5       | R R R                             | 4.5 – 6.0       |
| O<br>II<br>C<br>C<br>CH₃      | 2.0 – 2.6       | Ar—<b>H</b>                       | 6.0 – 8.5       |
| Ar — CH₃                      | 2.2 – 2.5       | O II C H                          | 9.5 – 10.5      |
| R—C≡C—H                       | 2.5 - 3.0       | O<br>II<br>C<br>OH                | 10 – 13         |
| (H)R—O—C<mark>H₃</mark>        | 3.3 - 4.0       | 3                                 |                |

*Table 6.2: Approximate Proton Chemical Shifts of Common Functional Groups*

> 表6.2：常见官能团的近似质子化学位移

The importance of chemical shift information is that it gives critical clues about *molecular structures*. Several highlights here:

> 化学位移信息的重要性在于它能提供关于分子结构的关键线索。以下是一些重点：

- Usually the hydrogens in C-H bond, without any other functional groups nearby, are in the range of 1-2 ppm;
- For hydrogen in C-H bond beside double bond, like C=C or C=O bond, the signal goes downfield to 2-2.5 ppm;
- With electronegative atoms connected on the carbon, like O-C-H, the hydrogens get deshielded and chemical shift move further downfield to 3-4 ppm;
- The hydrogens bonded directly to double bond carbon have the chemical shift at around 4.5-6 pm;
- The aromatic hydrogens (H on benzene ring) show chemical shift around 7 ppm;
- The chemical shift of hydrogens in OH (alcohol) or NH (amine) group vary in a rather large range, from 1-5 ppm;
- The hydrogen in aldehyde (-CHO) and carboxylic acid (COOH) group has the chemical shift rather downfield at about 9-10 ppm and 10-12 ppm respectively.

> 通常，C-H 键中的氢原子（没有其他官能团邻近）的化学位移范围在 1-2 ppm 之间；  
当 C-H 键邻近双键（如 C=C 或 C=O 键）时，氢的信号向低场移动，化学位移在 2-2.5 ppm 之间；  
当碳原子连接有电负性原子（如 O-C-H）时，氢原子被去屏蔽，化学位移进一步向低场移动，范围在 3-4 ppm 之间；  
直接与双键碳原子相连的氢原子的化学位移大约在 4.5-6 ppm 之间；  
芳香族氢原子（苯环上的氢）的化学位移大约在 7 ppm 左右；  
羟基（OH，醇）或氨基（NH，胺）中的氢原子的化学位移范围较大，通常在 1-5 ppm 之间；  
醛基（-CHO）和羧酸基（COOH）中的氢原子的化学位移分别在约 9-10 ppm 和 10-12 ppm 的低场区域。

When referring to the chemical shift table (or chart) for a certain compound, it is useful to keep in mind that the exact value may vary a bit to the given range, sometimes the difference up to 0.5 ppm unit may happen depends on the specific structure and the solvent used.

> 在查阅某一化合物的化学位移表（或图谱）时，应注意实际数值可能会在给定范围内略有变化，有时甚至可能相差高达0.5个ppm单位，这取决于具体的分子结构和所使用的溶剂。

With chemical shift information available, we can now assign the signals in the <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectrum of methyl acetate. According to **Fig. 6.6c**, the protons in CH3 group beside C=O bond are supposed to be in the range of 2-3 ppm, and protons in CH3 group connected with O directly have δ value of about 3-4 ppm. So the 2.0 ppm signal is for the Ha group and 3.6 ppm signal is for Hb group.

> 在获得化学位移信息后，我们现在可以将甲乙酸甲酯的<sup>1</sup>H NMR谱中的信号进行归属。根据图6.6c，与C=O键相邻的CH<sub>3</sub>组的质子应位于2～3 ppm范围，而直接连接氧原子的CH<sub>3</sub>组的质子化学位移约为3～4 ppm。因此，2.0 ppm处的信号对应Ha组，3.6 ppm处的信号对应Hb组。

![](_page_223_Figure_10.jpeg)

*Fig. 6.6d The 1H NMR spectrum of methyl acetate with signals assignment*

> 图6.6d 甲乙酸甲酯的1H NMR谱图及信号归属

### 0.2 **Chemical Shift of Protons Near π Electrons — Anisotropy Effect**

> 0.2 接近π电子的质子化学位移——各向异性效应

The chemical shift values of aromatic protons and vinylic protons (those directly bonded to an alkene carbon) resonate much further downfield (higher frequency, higher chemical shift) than can be accounted for simply by the deshielding effect of nearby electronegative atoms. These chemical shifts result from the anisotropy effect.

> 芳香族质子和烯丙质子（直接连接到烯烃碳原子的质子）的化学位移值远低于场（即频率更高，化学位移值更大），这种现象不能仅仅用邻近电负性原子的去屏蔽效应来解释。这些化学位移是由于各向异性效应所致。

Let's investigate the aromatic protons first. In benzene ring (and many other aromatic structures), the total six π electrons form delocalized big π bond around the ring (more discussions in Organic II). When the molecule is exposed to the external magnetic field **Bo**, these π electrons begin to circulate in a ring current and generating their own **induced magnetic field** Binduced. Whether shielding or deshielding occurs depends on the *location* of the protons in the induced magnetic field, and this is called **anisotropy** (means "non-uniformity") **effect**. This can be illustrated specifically in the figure below by comparing between point **A** and **B**.

> 让我们首先研究芳香族质子。在苯环（以及许多其他芳香族结构）中，总共有六个π电子形成一个环状的离域大π键（更多内容将在有机化学II中讨论）。当分子置于外加磁场Bo中时，这些π电子开始在环中形成环流，并产生自身的感应磁场Binduced。发生屏蔽或去屏蔽效应取决于质子在感应磁场中的位置，这种现象称为各向异性（即“非均匀性”）效应。这种效应可以通过下图中A点和B点的比较来具体说明。

![](_page_224_Figure_2.jpeg)

*Figure 6.6e Anisotrophy effect of the induced magnetic field B(induced)*

> 图6.6e 感应磁场的各向异性效应

If a proton is at point **A**, it feels the induced magnetic field pointing to the opposes direction of Bo, sothe proton experiences **shielding** effect. For the proton at point **B**, however, it feels the induced magnetic field to the same direction as Bo, so the proton experiences **deshielding** effect.

> 如果一个质子位于点A，它会感受到一个方向与Bo相反的感应磁场，因此该质子经历屏蔽效应。然而，对于位于点B的质子，它会感受到一个方向与Bo相同的感应磁场，因此该质子经历去屏蔽效应。

The protons on benzene ring are at the position equivalent of 'point **B**', that means that the induced current in this region of space is oriented in the *same* direction as B0, so it *adds* to B0 and result in a deshilelding effect and the benzene protons resonance at a higher frequency and have larger chemical shifts.

> 苯环上的质子位于与“点B”等效的位置，这意味着该空间区域中诱导电流的方向与B0方向相同，因此会叠加在B0上，产生去屏蔽效应。苯环质子的共振频率更高，化学位移值也更大。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_225_Picture_0.jpeg)

*Figure 6.6f Anisotrophy effect of Benzene ring: aromatic protons are at the location with deshielding effect, where the B(induced) is in the same direction as the B(O)*

> 图6.6f 苯环的各向异性效应：芳香质子位于去屏蔽效应的位置，此时诱导磁场B(induced)的方向与外加磁场B(O)相同

As a result, due to the anisotropy of the induced field generated by the circulating π electrons, the benzene protons are highly deshielded. Their chemical shift is far downfield, in the range of 6.5–8.5 ppm.

> 因此，由于环流π电子所产生的诱导场具有各向异性，苯环上的质子被高度去屏蔽。它们的化学位移远在高场区域，范围在6.5–8.5 ppm之间。

Anisotropy is also responsible for the downfield (high frequency) chemical shifts of vinylic protons (4–6.5 ppm) and aldehyde protons (9.5–11 ppm). The π electrons in these groups also circulate in such a way to generate an induced magnetic field that *adds* to external field Bo in the spots occupied by the protons. Carboxylic acid protons are even further downfield (9.5–12 ppm) due to the combined influence of the electronegative oxygen atom and the nearby π bond.

> 各向异性也导致烯丙质子（4–6.5 ppm）和醛质子（9.5–11 ppm）出现化学位移向高场（即频率更高）的现象。这些基团中的π电子以某种方式循环流动，产生一个附加的感应磁场，从而在质子所处的区域增强外部磁场B₀。由于吸电子氧原子和邻近的π键的共同作用，羧酸质子的化学位移进一步向高场移动（9.5–12 ppm）。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_226_Picture_0.jpeg)

*Figure 6.6g Anisotrophy Effect of Alkene: Vinylic protons are at the location with deshielding effect, where the Binduced is in the same direction as the Bo*

> 图6.6g 双键的各向异性效应：烯丙质子位于去屏蔽效应的位置，其中诱导的磁场方向与B的方向一致。

# 6.7 ¹H NMR Spectra and Interpretation (Part II)

> 6.7 ¹H NMR 谱图与解析（第二部分）

#### 0.1.1 **6.7.1 Integration of Signal Areas**

> 0.1.1 6.7.1 信号区域的整合

The computer in the NMR instrument can be instructed to mathematically integrate the area under a signal or group of signals. The **signal integration** process is very useful in 1H NMR spectrum, because *the area under a signal is proportional to the number of protons to which the signal corresponds***.**

> 核磁共振仪中的计算机可以被指令对信号或一组信号下的面积进行数学积分。信号积分过程在¹H NMR 谱中非常有用，因为信号下的面积与该信号所对应的质子数目成正比。

The **Fig. 6.7a** is the <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectrum of 1,4-dimethylbenzene with integration line (blue lines). The integration line generated by the computer is always in curve shape that resemble steps. The integration numbers are also generated by the computer together with the curve, that show the relative area of each signal (the integration numbers in the actual spectra are usually with decimals, whole numbers are shown here for simplicity).

> 图6.7a是1,4-二甲基苯的<sup>1</sup>H NMR谱图，图中带有积分线（蓝色线条）。计算机生成的积分线总是呈曲线形状，看起来像阶梯状。积分数值也是由计算机与曲线一同生成的，它表示每个信号的相对面积（实际谱图中的积分数值通常为小数，此处为简化起见显示为整数）。

![](_page_227_Figure_4.jpeg)

*Figure 6.7a The 1H NMR spectrum of 1,4-dimethylbenzene with integration*

> 图6.7a 1,4-二甲基苯的1H NMR谱图（积分值）

As we discussed earlier, the molecule of 1,4-dimethylbenzene has two sets of equivalent protons: the four aromatic (Ha) protons and the six methyl (Hb) protons. The integration of the area under the peak at 2.6 ppm is 1.5 times greater than the area under the peak at 7.4 ppm. *Please note that the integration number show the relative ratio of the number of protons, not the actual number***.** The ratio 3 to 2 here matches the ratio of actual number 6 to 4. This integration information, along with the chemical shift knowledge we have learned before allow us to assign the peaks: peak at 7.4 ppm correspond to protons (Ha) on the benzene ring, and the peak at 2.6 ppm correspond to two methyl groups (Hb).

> 正如我们之前所讨论的，1,4-二甲基苯分子中有两组等价质子：四个芳香族质子（Ha）和六个甲基质子（Hb）。在2.6 ppm处峰面积的积分值是7.4 ppm处峰面积的1.5倍。请注意，积分数值表示的是质子数量的相对比例，而不是实际数量。此处的3:2比例正好对应实际数量的6:4。结合我们之前所学的化学位移知识，积分信息使我们能够确定各个峰的归属：7.4 ppm处的峰对应苯环上的质子（Ha），而2.6 ppm处的峰对应两个甲基（Hb）。

### 0.2 **6.7.2 Signal Splitting (Coupling)**

> 0.2 6.7.2 信号分裂（耦合）

In the <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectra that we have seen so far, each set of protons generates a *single* NMR signal. This is not that common for <sup>1</sup>HNMR actually. In fact, the <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectra of most organic molecules contain signals that are 'split' into two or more peaks that is called **splitting** (or **coupling**). The spectra with peak splitting may looked more complicated, however, this splitting behavior provides very useful information about the structure of a compound.

> 到目前为止，我们所看到的<sup>1</sup>H NMR谱中，每组质子通常产生一个单一的NMR信号。但实际上，这种情况并不常见。事实上，大多数有机分子的<sup>1</sup>H NMR谱中，信号会被分裂成两个或更多个峰，这种现象称为分裂（或耦合）。虽然具有峰分裂的谱图看起来可能更复杂，但这种分裂行为为化合物的结构提供了非常有用的信息。

Let's consider the spectrum for 1,1,2-trichloroethane (**Fig. 6.7b**). In this and in other spectra to follow, the expansions of individual signals are shown so that the signal splitting patterns are recognizable.

> 让我们来分析1,1,2-三氯乙烷的谱图（图6.7b）。在本图以及其他后续的谱图中，都对单个信号进行了扩展，以便能够清晰地识别信号的分裂模式。

![](_page_228_Figure_0.jpeg)

*Fig. 6.7b The 1H NMR spectrum of 1,1,2-trichloroethane with signal splitting*

> 图6.7b 1,1,2-三氯乙烷的1H NMR谱图及信号分裂

The signal at 3.96 ppm, corresponding to the two Ha protons, is split into two peaks of equal height (and area) – this is referred to as a **doublet.** The Hb signal at 5.76 ppm, on the other hand, is split into three peaks, with the middle peak higher than the two outside peaks and the integration ratio between the three peaks is 1:2:1, such splitting signal is called a **triplet**.

> 3.96 ppm处的信号对应于两个Ha质子，该信号被分裂为两个高度（面积）相等的峰——这种分裂信号称为双重峰（doublet）。另一方面，5.76 ppm处的Hb信号被分裂为三个峰，中间的峰比两侧的峰更高，三个峰的积分比例为1:2:1，这种分裂信号称为三重峰（triplet）。

Signal splitting is caused by **spin-spin coupling**, a term that describes the magnetic interactions between nonequivalent hydrogen atoms that are with 2 or 3 bonds of the hydrogens producing the signal. The nearby protons have magnetic moment that can be either against or with the external magnetic field, therefore splits the energy levels of the protons whose signal is being observed, and result in the splitting of the signal into multiple peaks (the terms 'splitting' and 'coupling' are often used interchangeably when discussing NMR).

> 信号分裂是由自旋-自旋耦合引起的，这一术语描述了非等价氢原子之间磁相互作用的现象，这些氢原子与产生信号的氢原子之间相隔两个或三个键。邻近的氢原子具有磁矩，其方向可以与外部磁场相反或一致，因此会分裂正在观察的氢原子的能量水平，导致信号分裂为多个峰（在讨论核磁共振（NMR）时，“分裂”和“耦合”这两个术语常常可以互换使用）。

The most typical coupling we observed in this course is from non-equivalent vicinal hydrogens that are 3 bonds away, that is the hydrogens on adjacent carbons. This is also called **vicinal coupling** or **three-bond coupling**.

> 本课程中我们观察到的最典型的耦合现象，来自于相隔三个键的非等价邻近氢原子，即相邻碳原子上的氢原子。这种现象也被称为邻近耦合或三键耦合。

![](_page_228_Figure_5.jpeg)

*Figure 6.7c Vicinal Coupling*

> 图6.7c 邻位耦合

A simple rule that applies for predicting the number of peaks (or splitting pattern) expected from coupling and the rule in <sup>1</sup>H NMRis:

> 用于预测耦合所产生的峰数（或分裂模式）的简单规则是：

### 0.3 number of peaks = **n + 1** (n is the number of vicinal non-equivalent hydrogens)

> 0.3 个峰数 = n + 1（n 为邻位非等价氢的数量）

We will exam the splitting pattern with different number of n:

> 我们将考察不同n值的分裂模式。

- When n=0, the signal is a **singlet**, or has only one peak, as the signals observed in **Fig. 6.6d** and **Fig. 6.7a**.
- When n=1, the signal is a **doublet** with two peaks. The area ratio of the two peaks for a doublet is 1:1. The space between the two peaks is called coupling constant, *J*ab, measured in Hz.

> 当n=0时，信号为单峰，即只有一个峰，如图6.6d和图6.7a中所观察到的。  
当n=1时，信号为双重峰，即有两个峰。双重峰的两个峰的面积比为1:1。两个峰之间的距离称为耦合常数Jab，单位为Hz。

For the example of compound 1,1,2-trichloromethane, the signal of **Ha** protons fits into this situation. With only one vicinal proton, Hb, on the adjacent carbon, the signal of **Ha** show as a doublet.

> 以化合物1,1,2-三氯甲烷为例，Ha质子的信号符合这一情况。由于相邻碳原子上只有一个邻位质子Hb，Ha质子的信号表现为一个双重峰。

![](_page_229_Figure_5.jpeg)

*Figure 6.7d 1,1,2-trichloromethane*

> 图6.7d 1,1,2-三氯甲烷

• When n=2, the signal is a **triplet** with three peaks. The three peaks of triplet has the ratio of the area as 1:2:1.

> • 当n=2时，信号表现为三重峰，共有三个峰。三重峰的面积比为1:2:1。

In the same compound 1,1,2-trichloromethane, the signal of **Hb** proton fits into this situation. With two vicinal protons, 2Ha, on the adjacent carbon, the signal of **Hb** show as a triplet.

> 在同一化合物1,1,2-三氯甲烷中，Hb质子的信号也符合这一情况。由于Hb质子相邻碳原子上有两个邻位质子（2Ha），Hb质子的信号表现为三重峰。

![](_page_230_Figure_0.jpeg)

• When n=3, the signal is a **quartet,** that means four peaks. The four peaks of quartet has the area ratio of 1:3:3:1.

> • 当 n=3 时，信号表现为四重峰，即四个峰。四重峰的面积比为 1:3:3:1。

For the spectrum of ethyl acetate (**Fig. 6.7e**), the signal of **Hb** is a quartet, because there are three vicinal protons 3Hc on the adjacent carbon. Please note that the carbon with **Hb** connected with oxygen on the other side, and there are no hydrogen atoms on that oxygen atom, so only the coupling with three vicinal protons apply.

> 乙酸乙酯的核磁共振谱（图6.7e）中，Hb的信号表现为四重峰，这是因为相邻碳原子上有三个邻位质子（3Hc）。请注意，Hb所在的碳原子另一侧连接的是氧原子，而该氧原子上没有氢原子，因此只有与三个邻位质子的耦合效应存在。

![](_page_230_Figure_3.jpeg)

*Figure 6.7e The 1H NMR spectrum of ethyl acetate with signals splitting*

> 图6.7e 乙酸乙酯的1H NMR谱图及信号分裂

• When n≥4, the signal can be called a **multiplet**. Theoretically, with n increase the signal split into more peaks and

> • 当 n≥4 时，该信号可以称为多重峰。理论上，随着 n 增大，信号会分裂为更多的峰。

the total number of peaks is "n+1". However, the small peaks on the sides may or may not be able to be observed since they might be merged into noise. The signal with more than four peaks are generally called as a multiplet, and it is not that critical to tell exactly how many peaks involved in a multiplet.

> 峰的总个数为“n+1”。然而，两侧的小峰可能无法被观察到，因为它们可能会被噪声所掩盖。一般来说，具有超过四个峰的信号被称为多重峰（multiplet），并不需要精确地确定多重峰中包含多少个峰。

#### 0.3.1 **Extra notes about signal splitting:**

> 0.3.1 关于信号分裂的额外说明：

1. Splitting (coupling) *only* occurs between *nonequivalent* protons. For equivalent protons, there is no coupling. In the spectrum of succinic acid **(Fig. 6.7f)** for example, the protons on the two middle carbons are equivalent (Ha), so there is no coupling between them and they show a singlet.

> 裂分（耦合）仅发生在非等价质子之间。对于等价质子，不会发生耦合。例如琥珀酸（图6.7f）的谱图中，两个中间碳原子上的质子是等价的（Ha），因此它们之间没有耦合，表现为单峰。

![](_page_231_Figure_3.jpeg)

*Figure 6.7f 1H NMR spectrum of succinic acid*

> 图6.7f 苯二甲酸的1H NMR谱图

2. Protons in OH or NH generally do not couple with vicinal hydrogens. OH and NH protons are acidic enough to rapidly exchange between different molecules, so the neighboring protons never actually 'feels' their influence. See the specific example of 1-heptanol spectrum in **Fig. 6.7g**.

> OH 或 NH 中的质子通常不会与邻近的氢原子发生耦合。OH 和 NH 质子酸性足够强，可以在不同分子间迅速交换，因此邻近的氢原子实际上从未真正“感受到”它们的影响。参见图 6.7g 中 1-庚醇的谱图，以获得具体示例。

![](_page_232_Figure_0.jpeg)

*Figure 6.7g The 1HNMR spectrum of 1-heptanol*

> 图6.7g 1-庚醇的1H NMR谱图

# **6.7.3 <sup>1</sup>H NMR Practice**

> 6.7.3 <sup>1</sup>H NMR 实践

#### 0.1.1 **Signal assignment based on the given structure**

> 0.1.1 根据给定结构进行信号归属

With the structure of a compound given, we can apply all the knowledge about <sup>1</sup>H NMR to assign the signals in the spectrum, that is to identify a certain signal comes from which hydrogen(s).

> 在给出化合物的结构后，我们可以运用所有关于<sup>1</sup>H NMR的知识来解析谱图中的信号，即确定某一信号来自于哪一个氢原子（或哪些氢原子）。

# *Examples*

> 示例

Match the <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectrum below to its corresponding compound, and assign all of the signals.

> 将下面的<sup>1</sup>H NMR谱图与其对应的化合物进行匹配，并对所有信号进行归属。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_233_Figure_0.jpeg)

- a) cyclopentanone b) 3-pentanone c) butaldehyde d) 2-pentanone
- e) 4-heptanone f) 1-butene

> a) 环戊酮  
b) 3-戊酮  
c) 丁醛  
d) 2-戊酮  
e) 4-庚酮  
f) 1-丁烯

**Approach**: It is good idea to draw the structure of each compound and try to see which matches to the spectrum.

> 方法：最好先画出每种化合物的结构，尝试找出与谱图相匹配的化合物。

The spectrum has four signals: triplet (~0.7 ppm), multiplet (~1.4 ppm), singlet ( ~1.9 ppm) and triplet (~2.2 ppm). Based on the structure of each compound, compound c), d) and f) should have four signals in the <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectrum.

> 该谱图中有四个信号：三重峰（约0.7 ppm）、多重峰（约1.4 ppm）、单峰（约1.9 ppm）和三重峰（约2.2 ppm）。根据每种化合物的结构，化合物c)、d)和f)在<sup>1</sup>H NMR谱中应出现四个信号。

- There is no signals at about 9 ppm for the aldehyde hydrogens in the spectra, so the spectrum is **not** for compound c) , butaldehyde.
- There is no signals at about 4~5 ppm for the alkene hydrogens in the spectra, so the spectrum is **not** for compound f) , 1-butene.
- The signals in the spectrum match with what are expected for compound d), 2-pentanone.

> 在约9 ppm处没有醛氢的信号，因此该谱图不是化合物c)（醛）的。  
在约4~5 ppm处没有烯烃氢的信号，因此该谱图不是化合物f)（1-丁烯）的。  
该谱图中的信号与化合物d)（2-戊酮）预期的信号相符。

**Solution:** The spectrum is for 2-pentanone.

> 解答：该谱图对应的是2-戊酮。

![](_page_234_Picture_4.jpeg)

# **Structure Determination based on <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectrum**

> 基于<sup>1</sup>H NMR谱的结构确定

For an advanced level of practice, we are supposed to be able to determine the exact structure of a compound with <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectrum given (and other necessary information). As we have learned, there are a lot valuable information about the structure of a compound can be obtained from an <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectrum. For a summary, analyzing the four features of the spectrum is critical to elucidate the structure of a compound:

> 对于更高层次的练习，我们应当能够根据给定的<sup>1</sup>H NMR谱图（以及其他必要的信息）确定化合物的准确结构。正如我们所学，可以从<sup>1</sup>H NMR谱图中获得关于化合物结构的大量有价值的信息。概括来说，分析谱图的四个特征对于阐明化合物的结构至关重要：

- The **number of signals** indicate how many different sets of protons there are in the molecule;
- The **chemical shift** of the signal tells us about the electronic environment of each set of protons;
- The **integration** under each signal provides information about how many protons there are in the set being measured (keep in mind that the integration values are for the *ratio*, not actual number of protons);
- The **splitting pattern** of each signal tells about the number of protons on atoms *adjacent*to the one whose signal is being measured.

> 信号的数量表明分子中存在多少种不同的质子组；  
信号的化学位移告诉我们每组质子所处的电子环境；  
每个信号下的积分值提供了该组质子的数量信息（请注意，积分值表示的是比例关系，而非实际的质子数目）；  
每个信号的分裂模式则说明了与被测量质子相邻原子上的质子数目。

**We'll see examples for structure determination at the end of this chapter.**

> 我们将在本章末尾看到一些结构确定的例子。

# 6.8 ¹³C NMR Spectroscopy

> 6.8 ¹³C 核磁共振波谱

For carbon element, the most abundant isotope <sup>12</sup>C (with ~99% natural abundance) does not have a nuclear magnetic moment, and thus is NMR-inactive. The C NMR is therefore based on the <sup>13</sup>C isotope, that accounts for about 1% of carbon atoms in nature and has a magnetic dipole moment just like a proton. The theories we have learned about <sup>1</sup>H NMR spectroscopy also applies to <sup>13</sup>C NMR, however with several important differences about the spectrum.

> 对于碳元素，最丰富的同位素是<sup>12</sup>C（自然丰度约为99%），它没有核磁矩，因此在核磁共振（NMR）中是不活跃的。因此，碳的核磁共振（<sup>13</sup>C NMR）是基于<sup>13</sup>C同位素的，该同位素在自然界中约占碳原子的1%，其磁偶极矩与质子类似。我们之前所学的关于<sup>1</sup>H NMR光谱的理论同样适用于<sup>13</sup>C NMR，不过在光谱上存在一些重要的差异。

The magnetic moment of a <sup>13</sup>C nucleus is much weaker than that of a proton, meaning that <sup>13</sup>C NMR signals are inherently much weaker than proton signals. This, combined with the low natural abundance of <sup>13</sup>C, means that it is much more difficult to observe carbon signals. Usually, sample with high concentration and large number of scans (thousands or more) are required in order to bring the signal-to-noise ratio down to acceptable levels for <sup>13</sup>C NMR spectra.

> 碳-13（<sup>13</sup>C）核的磁矩远小于质子的磁矩，这意味着碳-13核磁共振（<sup>13</sup>C NMR）信号本身比质子信号弱得多。再加上碳-13在自然界中的丰度较低，使得观察碳信号变得更加困难。通常需要高浓度的样品以及大量的扫描次数（数千次或更多），才能将碳-13核磁共振谱的信噪比降低到可接受的水平。

### 0.1 **Chemical Equivalent**

> 0.1 化学当量

For carbons that are chemical equivalent, they only show one signal in <sup>13</sup>C NMR as like protons for <sup>1</sup>HNMR. So it is very important to be able to identify equivalent carbons in the structure, in order to interpret <sup>13</sup>C NMR spectrum correctly. Taking toluene as an example, there are five sets of different carbon atoms (shown in different colors), so there are five signals in the <sup>13</sup>C NMR spectrum of toluene.

> 在化学等价的碳原子中，它们在<sup>13</sup>C核磁共振谱中只显示一个信号，就像<sup>1</sup>H核磁共振谱中的质子一样。因此，能够识别结构中的等价碳原子对于正确解释<sup>13</sup>C核磁共振谱非常重要。以甲苯为例，存在五组不同的碳原子（用不同颜色表示），因此甲苯的<sup>13</sup>C核磁共振谱中会出现五个信号。

$$c$$
  $c$   $c$   $c$   $c$

> 

#### 0.1.1 **Chemical Shift**

> 0.1.1 化学位移

<sup>13</sup>C nuclei has different value of g (the magnetogyric ratio) comparing to <sup>1</sup>H nuclei, so the resonance frequencies of <sup>13</sup>C nuclei is different to those of protons in the same applied field (referring to **formula. 6.4**, in section **6.5**). In an instrument with a 7.05 Tesla magnet, protons resonate at about 300 MHz, while carbons resonate at about 75 MHz. This allows us to look at <sup>13</sup>C signals using a completely separate 'window' of radio frequencies. Just like in <sup>1</sup>H NMR, tetramethylsilane (TMS) is also used as the standard compound in <sup>13</sup>C NMR experiments to define the 0 ppm, however it is the signal from the four equivalent **carbon** atoms in TMS that serves as the standard. Chemical shifts for <sup>13</sup>C nuclei in organic molecules are spread out over a much wider range of about 220 ppm (**see Table 6.3**)**.**

> ¹³C核的g值（磁旋比）与¹H核不同，因此在相同磁场下，¹³C核的共振频率与质子的共振频率不同（参见第6.5节中的公式6.4）。在一台7.05特斯拉磁场的仪器中，质子的共振频率约为300 MHz，而碳核的共振频率约为75 MHz。这使得我们可以使用完全独立的射频频率窗口来观察¹³C信号。正如在¹H NMR中所使用的那样，在¹³C NMR实验中也使用四甲基硅烷（TMS）作为标准化合物来定义0 ppm。不过，在TMS中，来自四个等效碳原子的信号被用作标准信号。有机分子中¹³C核的化学位移范围要宽得多，约为220 ppm（参见表6.3）。

| Type of Carbon                 | Chemical Shift (ppm) | Type of Carbon | Chemical Shift<br>(ppm) |
|--------------------------------|----------------------|----------------|-------------------------|
| R—CH <sub>3</sub>              | 0 – 35               | R<br>E         | 80 – 150                |
| R<br>I<br>R—CH <sub>2</sub>    | 15 – 55              | c              | 110 – 170               |
| R<br>R—CH<br>I<br>R            | 25 – 55              | O II<br>R OR   | 165 – 175               |
| R—C—R<br> <br>  R              | 30 – 40              | O II           | 175 – 185               |
| — C—X<br> <br>(X: Cl, Br or N) | 10 – 65              | O II<br>R C H  | 190 – 200               |
|                                | 50 – 90              | O II C R       | 200 – 220               |
| R <b>−C</b> ≡                  | 70 – 90              |                |                         |

> | 碳的类型                   | 化学位移（ppm）         | 碳的类型         | 化学位移<br>(ppm)         |
|--------------------------|------------------------|------------------|--------------------------|
| R—CH₃                   | 0 – 35                 | R<br>E           | 80 – 150                 |
| R<br>I<br>R—CH₂         | 15 – 55                | c                | 110 – 170                |
| R<br>R—CH<br>I<br>R     | 25 – 55                | O II<br>R OR     | 165 – 175                |
| R—C—R<br>               <br>R | 30 – 40               | O II             | 175 – 185                |
| —C—X<br>               <br>(X: Cl, Br 或 N) | 10 – 65             | O II<br>R C H    | 190 – 200                |
|                            | 50 – 90                | O II C R         | 200 – 220                |
| R <b>−C</b> ≡           | 70 – 90                |                  |                          |

*Table 6.3 Approximate 13C NMR chemical shifts of some common groups*

> 表6.3 一些常见基团的近似13C NMR化学位移

The chemical shift of a <sup>13</sup>C nucleus is influenced by essentially the same factors that influence the chemical shift a proton: the deshielding effect of electronegative atoms and anisotropy effects tend to shift signals downfield (higher resonance frequency, with higher chemical shifts). In addition, sp<sup>2</sup> hybridization results in a large downfield shift. The <sup>13</sup>C NMR signals for carbonyl carbons are generally the furthest downfield (170-220 ppm), due to both sp<sup>2</sup> hybridization and to the double bond to oxygen.

> 碳-13（<sup>13</sup>C）核的化学位移受与质子化学位移相同的基本因素影响：电负性原子的去屏蔽效应以及各向异性效应通常会使信号向高场（更高的共振频率，即更高的化学位移）移动。此外，sp<sup>2</sup>杂化会导致较大的高场位移。羰基碳的<sup>13</sup>C核磁共振信号通常位于最远的高场区域（170-220 ppm），这是由于sp<sup>2</sup>杂化以及与氧原子的双键所致。

# **Integration and Coupling in <sup>13</sup>C NMR**

> <sup>13</sup>C NMR 中的整合与耦合

Unlike <sup>1</sup>H NMR, the area under a <sup>13</sup>C NMR signal **cannot** easily be used to determine the number of carbons to which it corresponds. The signals for some types of carbons are inherently weaker than for other types, for example peaks corresponding to carbonyl carbons are much smaller than those for methyl or methylene (CH2) peaks. For this reason, signal integration is generally not useful in <sup>13</sup>C NMR spectroscopy.

> 与<sup>1</sup>H NMR不同，<sup>13</sup>C NMR信号下方的面积通常不能轻易用于确定其对应的碳原子数目。某些类型的碳信号本身强度较弱，例如羰基碳（C=O）对应的峰比甲基（CH<sub>3</sub>）或亚甲基（CH<sub>2</sub>）的峰要小得多。因此，在<sup>13</sup>C NMR谱学中，信号积分通常并不实用。

Because of the low natural abundance of <sup>13</sup>C nuclei, the spin-spin coupling between two nonequivalent <sup>13</sup>C atoms is negligible. <sup>13</sup>C nuclei are coupled to nearby protons, however, which results in complicated spectra. For clarity, chemists generally use a technique called **broadband decoupling**, which essentially 'turns off' C-H coupling, resulting in a spectrum in which *all carbon signals are singlets.* Below is the proton-decoupled <sup>13</sup>C NMR spectrum of ethyl acetate in CDCl3 (**Fig. 6.8a**), showing the expected four signals, one for each of the carbons.

> 由于<sup>13</sup>C核在自然界中的天然丰度较低，两个不等效的<sup>13</sup>C原子之间的自旋-自旋耦合可以忽略不计。然而，<sup>13</sup>C核会与邻近的质子发生耦合，从而导致谱图变得复杂。为了提高清晰度，化学家通常采用一种称为宽带去耦合（broadband decoupling）的技术，该技术基本上“关闭”了C-H耦合，从而得到一个所有碳信号均表现为单峰的谱图。下面所示是乙酸乙酯在CDCl<sub>3</sub>中的质子去耦合<sup>13</sup>C核磁共振谱（图6.8a），显示出预期的四个信号，分别对应每一个碳原子。

![](_page_237_Figure_0.jpeg)

*Figure 6.8a The 13C NMR spectrum of ethyl acetate*

> 图6.8a 乙酸乙酯的13C NMR谱图

For our class purpose, <sup>13</sup>C NMR spectra are usually used as supporting information to confirm the structure of a compound.

> 为了我们课程的目的，通常使用<sup>13</sup>C NMR谱作为辅助信息来确认化合物的结构。

#### 0.1.1 *Exercises 6.2*

> 0.1.1 习题 6.2

Below are <sup>13</sup>C NMR spectra for methylbenzene (common name toluene) and methyl methacrylate. Refer to **Table 6.3** to match the spectra to the correct structure.

> 以下是甲基苯（俗称甲苯）和甲基丙烯酸甲酯的<sup>13</sup>C NMR谱图。请参阅表6.3，将谱图与正确的结构对应起来。

Answers to Practice Questions Chapter 6

> 第六章练习题答案

# 6.9 Structure Determination Practice

> 6.9 结构解析练习

<sup>1</sup>H NMR provides a powerful tool for determining the structure of unknown compound. Other than that <sup>1</sup>H NMR, additional information includes molecular formula, IR and <sup>13</sup>C NMR spectrum are usually provided as well. Solving the structure of an unknown compound based on all the given information is an important type of question we will work on for this chapter. We will take the C5H12O constitutional isomer example to go through the strategy for solving this type of question.

> <sup>1</sup>H 核磁共振（NMR）为确定未知化合物结构提供了一个强有力的工具。除了<sup>1</sup>H NMR之外，通常还会提供分子式、红外光谱（IR）以及<sup>13</sup>C NMR谱图等额外信息。根据所提供的所有信息来解析未知化合物的结构，是我们本章将重点学习的一种重要题型。我们将以C<sub>5</sub>H<sub>12</sub>O的构造异构体为例，来讲解解决此类问题的策略。

### 0.1 **Example: Constitutional Isomers with Formula C5H12O**

> 0.1 示例：分子式为C5H12O的结构异构体

The <sup>1</sup>H NMR below are all for compounds with molecular formula of C5H12O (the relative integration area for each signal are given as numbers on the spectra). The IR spectra of these compounds do **not** have any strong band at above 3000 cm-1 , **nor** are there strong bands at 1700 cm-1 . Propose a reasonable structure for each compound that is consistent with the data given.

> 以下所示的<sup>1</sup>H NMR谱均为分子式为C<sub>5</sub>H<sub>12</sub>O的化合物（每组信号的相对积分面积在谱图中以数字标明）。这些化合物的红外光谱在3000 cm<sup>-1</sup>以上没有强吸收峰，1700 cm<sup>-1</sup>处也没有强吸收峰。请根据所给数据，为每种化合物提出一个合理的结构。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_239_Figure_4.jpeg)

![](_page_239_Figure_5.jpeg)

![](_page_240_Figure_0.jpeg)

![](_page_240_Figure_1.jpeg)

#### 0.1.1 **Approach:**

> 0.1.1 方法：

*Step 1:* Calculate the degree of unsaturation (or IHD, **section 2.3**) based on the given molecular formula, and get hints about structure/functional group according to the degree of unsaturation. **This is usually the first step to solving this type of question.**

> 步骤1：根据给定的分子式计算不饱和度（或称为IHD，参见第2.3节），并根据不饱和度获得有关结构或官能团的提示。这通常是解决此类问题的第一步。

$$\frac{(2n+2)-X}{2} = \frac{(2\times5+2)-12}{2} = 0$$
Degree of unsaturation =

> 不饱和度 =

From what we learned about the degree of unsaturation, zero degree means there is no any ring nor double bond in

> 从我们所学的不饱和度知识可知，零度不饱和意味着分子中没有环状结构，也没有双键。

the structure, that means all the compounds in this question have *open chain structures with single bonds* only. With one oxygen atom involved, the possible functional group therefore will be **open chain alcohol,** or **open chain ether**.

> 结构，也就是说，本题中所有化合物都具有开链结构，仅含有单键。由于涉及一个氧原子，因此可能的官能团只能是开链醇或者开链醚。

*Step 2:* Narrow down the possible functional groups with IR information.

> 步骤2：利用红外光谱信息缩小可能的官能团范围。

IR indicate that there is **no**any strong bands at above 3000 cm-1 for the compound, that exclude the option of alcohol, so the only choice left is the **open chain ether**.

> 红外光谱显示，该化合物在3000 cm⁻¹以上没有明显的强吸收峰，因此可以排除含有羟基的可能性，唯一剩下的选择就是开链醚。

*Step 3:* Use available spectroscopy data (mainly <sup>1</sup>H NMR, with <sup>13</sup>C NMR as supporting if available) to identify discrete parts of the structure.

> 步骤3：利用现有的光谱数据（主要为<sup>1</sup>H NMR，如有可用则辅以<sup>13</sup>C NMR）来识别结构中的各个片段。

*Step 4: Try to put the pieces of the puzzle together, and double check if everything fit the available data.*

> 第4步：尝试将这些线索拼合起来，并再次检查所有内容是否与现有数据相符。

Step 3 and 4 are the most challenging parts since there is no simple rule to follow about how to do that. It takes practices to do the interpretation of <sup>1</sup>H NMR signals and translating that into the structure of unknown compound. Checking the four aspects of <sup>1</sup>H NMR as we learned in section **6.6.5**. The relative integration areas are given for this question to make it bit easier.

> 步骤3和步骤4是最具挑战性的部分，因为在这两个步骤中没有简单规则可循。要进行<sup>1</sup>H NMR信号的解析，并将其转化为未知化合物的结构，需要大量的练习。我们在第6.6.5节中学习了如何检查<sup>1</sup>H NMR的四个方面。本题给出了相对积分面积，以便于解答。

### 0.2 **Solutions:**

> 0.2 解法：

### 0.3 **Compound 1:**

> 0.3 合成物 1：

We can start with the simplest spectrum that have least signals:

> 我们可以从具有最少信号的最简单光谱开始：

- There are only two signals (both are singlet) in this spectrum, indicate that there are two sets of non-equivalent hydrogens.
- The integrations of the two signals are 3 and 1, means the ratio of the number of hydrogens in these two sets are 3:1. And since there are total 12 hydrogens, the actual number of hydrogens should be 9 and 3 in each group.
- 3 hydrogens imply a CH3 methyl group, and 9 hydrogens could be three CH3 groups. Also since all the 9 hydrogens are equivalent, that means the three CH3 groups are equivalent. The only way to have three equivalent CH3 groups is that there is a *t*-butyl group.
- So the structure is the ether with a methyl group and a *t*-butyl group connected with the oxygen atom.
- The structure of **compound 1** is given below, with the chemical shift valued included.

> 该谱图中只有两个信号（均为单峰），说明存在两组非等价氢原子。  
两个信号的积分值分别为3和1，说明这两组氢原子的数量比为3:1。由于总共有12个氢原子，因此每组实际氢原子的数量应分别为9个和3个。  
3个氢原子表明为一个甲基（CH₃）基团，而9个氢原子可能为三个甲基基团。由于这9个氢原子是等价的，说明这三个甲基基团是等价的。要使三个甲基基团等价，只有存在叔丁基（t-丁基）结构。  
因此，该化合物的结构为一个醚基，其中甲基和叔丁基通过氧原子相连。  
化合物1的结构如下，其中包含化学位移值。

![](_page_241_Figure_14.jpeg)

For the remaining compounds, the integration for each signal could be a very good starting point, since generally the integration value indicates the possible structural unit like CH3, CH2 or CH. Then the structural units can be put together in a logical way like putting pieces of a puzzle together.

> 对于剩下的化合物，每个信号的积分值可以作为非常好的起点，因为通常积分值可以表明可能的结构单元，如CH₃、CH₂或CH。然后可以像拼图一样，以逻辑的方式将这些结构单元组合起来。

#### 0.3.1 **Compound 2:**

> 0.3.1 化合物 2：

- Based on the integration, it is determined that there are:
  - one CH3 group show a triplet;
  - two equivalent CH3 groups show a doublet;
  - one CH group show a multiplet;
  - one CH2 group show a quartet.

> 根据积分结果，确定以下情况：
一个 CH₃ 组显三重峰；
两个等价的 CH₃ 组显双重峰；
一个 CH 组显多重峰；
一个 CH₂ 组显四重峰。

- The triplet CH3 could connect with quartet CH2 as a CH2CH3 ethyl group, that makes sense based on the splitting pattern.
- Also, the two equivalent CH3 groups with a CH could give an isopropyl group, that is consistent to the splitting pattern.
- So the overall structure of **compound 2** is isopropyl ethyl ether.

> 三重峰的CH₃可能与四重峰的CH₂相连，形成CH₂CH₃乙基结构，这与分裂模式是一致的。  
此外，两个等价的CH₃基团与一个CH相连，可以形成异丙基，这也与分裂模式相符。  
因此，化合物2的整体结构为异丙基乙基醚。

![](_page_242_Figure_3.jpeg)

### 0.4 **Compound 3:**

> 0.4 化合物 3：

- Based on the integration, it is determined that there are:
  - one CH3 group show a triplet;
  - one CH3 groups show a doublet;
  - one CH2 group show a multiplet;
  - one CH group show a quartet;
  - one CH3 group show a singlet.
- The singlet means the CH3 has no any other hydrogens bonded on adjacent atoms, so the CH3 group should be bonded with the oxygen atom, and the value of chemical shift (about 3.2 ppm) confirms.
- The triplet CH3 could connect with quartet CH2 as a CH2CH3 ethyl group, that makes sense based on the splitting pattern.
- The doublet CH3 groups should connect with a CH group, that is consistent to the splitting pattern.
- The chemical shift (about 3 ppm) and splitting of the CH group (quartet) indicate it should connect to the oxygen atom.
- Put all the above pieces together, the structure of **compound 3** is sec-butyl methyl ether.

> 根据积分结果，可以确定以下情况：
- 一个 CH₃ 基团显示三重峰；
- 一个 CH₃ 基团显示双重峰；
- 一个 CH₂ 基团显示多重峰；
- 一个 CH 基团显示四重峰；
- 一个 CH₃ 基团显示单峰。

单峰表明该 CH₃ 基团没有与相邻原子上的氢原子相连，因此该 CH₃ 基团应连接到氧原子，其化学位移值（约 3.2 ppm）也证实了这一点。

三重峰的 CH₃ 基团可能与四重峰的 CH₂ 基团相连，形成 CH₂CH₃ 乙基结构，这与裂分模式是相符的。

双重峰的 CH₃ 基团应连接到 CH 基团，这也与裂分模式一致。

CH 基团的化学位移（约 3 ppm）及其裂分模式（四重峰）表明它应连接到氧原子。

将以上所有信息综合起来，化合物 3 的结构应为仲丁基甲醚。

![](_page_242_Figure_16.jpeg)

#### 0.4.1 **Compound 4**

> 0.4.1 化合物 4

•

> •

- Based on the integration, it is determined that there are:
  - one CH3 group show a triplet;
  - another CH3 groups show a triplet;
  - one CH2 group show a multiplet;
  - two CH2 groups with signals overlapping
- The two CH3 groups both as triplet indicate that they both connect with CH2, so there are two ethyl CH2CH3 groups in the structure, and they are not equivalent.

> 根据积分结果，可以确定以下情况：

- 一个 CH₃ 组显示三重峰；
- 另一个 CH₃ 组也显示三重峰；
- 一个 CH₂ 组显示多重峰；
- 两个 CH₂ 组的信号发生重叠。

两个 CH₃ 组均显示三重峰，表明它们均与 CH₂ 相连，因此结构中存在两个乙基（CH₂CH₃）基团，且这两个基团不等价。

- Therefore there is only one more CH2 group left.
- There is only one possible structure with two CH2CH3 groups, one CH2 group and one oxygen atom, so the structure of **compound 4** is ethyl methyl ether.

> 因此，还剩下一个CH₂基团。  
只有一种可能的结构包含两个CH₂CH₃基团、一个CH₂基团和一个氧原子，因此化合物4的结构是乙基甲基醚。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_243_Figure_2.jpeg)

# CHAPTER 7 NUCLEOPHILIC SUBSTITUTION REACTIONS

> 第7章 核亲核取代反应

With the foundations have been built on the basic concepts in organic chemistry, we are now ready to learn about organic reactions. Organic reaction is mainly about the transformation of one functional group to the other, that aims to introduce new functional group into the product. As the reactivity center of a compound, a functional group has its unique property and undergoes certain type of reaction. We will explore the certain rules that govern the reactivity of each functional group, and understand why different functional groups show different reactivities. In this chapter, we will start with substitution reaction of alkyl halide, and investigate further more from there.

> 在掌握了有机化学基本概念的基础上，我们现在可以开始学习有机反应。有机反应主要涉及一个官能团向另一个官能团的转化，其目的是在产物中引入新的官能团。作为化合物的反应中心，官能团具有其独特的性质，并会发生特定类型的反应。我们将探讨支配各类官能团反应性的规则，理解为什么不同的官能团表现出不同的反应性。在本章中，我们将从卤代烷的取代反应开始，然后进一步深入探讨相关反应。

# 7.1 Nucleophilic Substitution Reaction Overview

> 7.1 核亲核取代反应概述

Let's start with a simple substitution reaction example:

> 让我们从一个简单的取代反应例子开始：

*Figure 7.1a Substitution reaction*

> 图7.1a 取代反应

In this reaction, the Br in the reactant methylbromide (CH3Br) is replaced by the OH group, and the methanol (CH3OH) is produced as the major product, together with bromide Br-, the side product. It is easy to understand that this is a substitution reaction, because Br is substituted by OH.

> 在这个反应中，反应物溴甲烷（CH₃Br）中的溴（Br）被羟基（OH）取代，生成甲醇（CH₃OH）作为主要产物，同时生成溴离子（Br⁻）作为副产物。显然，这是一个取代反应，因为溴被羟基所取代。

Further discussions on this simple reaction require the introduction of some key terms that are critical in understanding why and how the reaction proceed in this way. These terms are electrophile, nucleophile and leaving group.

> 关于这一简单反应的进一步讨论，需要引入一些关键术语，这些术语对于理解反应为何以及如何以这种方式进行至关重要。这些术语包括亲电试剂（electrophile）、亲核试剂（nucleophile）和离去基团（leaving group）。

### 0.1 **Electrophile**

> 0.1 亲电试剂

The reactant CH3Br is an alkyl halide. The C-X bond (X: F, Cl and Br) in alkyl halide is polar because halogen is more electronegative than carbon, and as a result carbon has a partial positive charge and halogen has a partial negative charge.

> 反应物 CH₃Br 是一种烷基卤化物。烷基卤化物中的 C-X 键（X 为 F、Cl 和 Br）具有极性，这是因为卤素的电负性比碳强，导致碳原子带有部分正电荷，而卤素原子带有部分负电荷。

$$H_3C$$
  $H_3C$

> 

Because of the partial positive charge on carbon, the carbon atom in C-X bond is electron-deficient, and it is going to seek electron-rich reagent to connect with. Such electron-deficient species is called an **electrophile** *(phile* is the Greek suffix means "love"), means the species that loves electrons. The electron-deficient species are usually electrophiles. Other electrophile examples include positive charged ions and atom with incomplete octet, for example: H<sup>+</sup> , CH3 + ,BH3, BeF2, AlCl3.

> 由于碳原子带有部分正电荷，C-X 键中的碳原子电子不足，因此会寻求带有丰富电子的试剂与其结合。这类电子不足的物种被称为亲电试剂（“phile”是希腊后缀，意为“喜爱”），即那些喜爱电子的物种。通常，电子不足的物种都是亲电试剂。其他亲电试剂的例子包括带正电的离子以及具有不完整八电子结构的原子，例如：H⁺、CH₃⁺、BH₃、BeF₂、AlCl₃。

For CH3Br in this reaction, it is the **carbon** atom that act as the electrophile, and the carbon can be called as electrophilic carbon.

> 在该反应中，CH3Br中的碳原子作为亲电试剂，该碳原子可称为亲电碳原子。

The compound CH3Br that undergoes the substitution usually can be called the substrate.

> 通常发生取代反应的化合物CH3Br通常被称为底物。

#### 0.1.1 **Nucleophile**

> 0.1.1 核亲核试剂

The hydroxide, OH – , is another reactant in above reaction. It is shown clearly with the Lewis structure of OH – that the oxygen atom has three lone pair electrons and is negatively charged, so it is an electron-rich species with high electron density.

> 羟基（OH⁻）是上述反应中的另一种反应物。通过OH⁻的路易斯结构可以看出，氧原子具有三对孤对电子并带有负电荷，因此它是一个富电子物种，具有较高的电子密度。

An electron-rich species is called a **nucleophile** ("nucleo" comes from nucleus, that means positive charge), that is the reagent seeking positively charged or electron-poor species to react with. OH – is the nucleophile for above reaction. Generally, any species with the electron pair available for sharing could be nucleophile. Nucleophile can be either negatively charged (Nu:– ), or neutral (Nu:), for example: OR – , H2O, ROH, NH3, RNH2, RCOO– are all possible nucleophiles. Based on the understanding of the concepts of electrophile and nucleophile, you probably realize that a nucleophile

> 一种富含电子的物种被称为亲核试剂（“nucleo”源自“nucleus”，意为正电荷），也就是说，亲核试剂是寻找带正电荷或电子贫乏的物种进行反应的试剂。在上述反应中，OH⁻ 是亲核试剂。一般来说，任何具有可提供共享电子对的物种都可能成为亲核试剂。亲核试剂可以是带负电的（Nu:⁻），也可以是中性的（Nu:），例如：OR⁻、H₂O、ROH、NH₃、RNH₂、RCOO⁻ 等都是可能的亲核试剂。基于对亲电子试剂和亲核试剂概念的理解，你可能已经意识到，亲核试剂

could react with an electrophile! Yes, that is the very important and fundamental rule for organic reaction: *when electron-rich nucleophile meet with electron-deficient electrophile, organic reaction would occur*.

> 这可以与亲电试剂发生反应！是的，这就是有机反应的一个非常重要的基本规则：当电子富集的亲核试剂与电子贫乏的亲电试剂相遇时，有机反应就会发生。

#### 0.1.2 **Leaving Group**

> 0.1.2 离去基团

To ensure the above substitution occurs, another critical factor is that the Br must leave together with the electron pairs in C-Br bond, and the bromide, Br-, is called the leaving group. The leaving group (LG) leaves with the bonding pair of electrons, and is replaced by the nucleophile in the substitution reaction. Without a proper leaving group, even nucleophile is attracted to electrophile, the substitution reaction still cannot move forward. Leaving group can be negatively charged or neutral, as we will see in detailed discussions later.

> 为确保上述取代反应能够进行，另一个关键因素是溴离子（Br⁻）必须与C-Br键中的电子对一起离开，这种能够离开的基团被称为离去基团（LG）。离去基团在反应中随着成键电子对一起离去，并被亲核试剂所取代。如果没有合适的离去基团，即使亲核试剂被电子亲核试剂吸引，取代反应仍然无法进行。离去基团可以带负电荷，也可以是中性的，这一点将在后续的详细讨论中进一步阐明。

Applying the three key terms, the above substitution reaction can be summarized as: the nucleophile displaces the leaving group in a substrate, so such reaction is called **nucleophilic substitution reaction**. Nucleophilic substitution reaction could therefore be shown in a more general way:

> 应用上述三个关键术语，上述取代反应可以总结为：亲核试剂在底物中取代离去基团，因此这类反应被称为亲核取代反应。因此，亲核取代反应可以更一般地表示为：

**Note**: the nucleophile and leaving group are not necessary negatively charged, they could be neutral as mentioned earlier.

> 注意：亲核试剂和离去基团并不一定带负电荷，如前所述，它们也可能是中性的。

#### 0.1.3 **Kinetics of Nucleophilic Substitution Reaction**

> 0.1.3 核亲核取代反应的动力学

Kinetics is the study that concerns the rate of a chemical reaction, or how fast the reaction occurs. The reaction rate data helps to shine a light on the understanding of reaction mechanism, the step-by-step electron transfer process. Kinetic studies on nucleophilic substitution reactions indicate that there are *two* different rate law expressions for such reactions. For the two reactions below, reaction 1 is in second order while reaction 2 is in first order. The only reason behind the different kinetic rate is that the reactions go through different reaction mechanism.

> 动力学是研究化学反应速率的学科，即研究反应进行的快慢。反应速率的数据有助于揭示反应机理，即反应过程中逐步进行的电子转移过程。对亲核取代反应的动力学研究表明，这类反应存在两种不同的速率方程。对于以下两个反应，反应1为二级反应，反应2为一级反应。两种反应速率不同的唯一原因是它们经历了不同的反应机理。

*Figure 7.1b Reaction 1: second-order reaction*

> 图7.1b 反应1：二级反应

Reaction 1 is the substitution reaction we are familiar with already. It is a second-order reaction. That means the reaction rate depends on the concentration of *both* substrate CH3Br and nucleophile OH – . If the concentration of CH3Br doubled, the reaction rate get doubled, and if the concentration of OH – doubled, the reaction rate doubled as well. When the concentration of both CH3Br and OH – doubled, the reaction rate increased by a factor of *four*.

> 反应1是我们已经熟悉的取代反应。这是一个二级反应，也就是说反应速率取决于底物CH3Br和亲核试剂OH⁻的浓度。如果CH3Br的浓度加倍，反应速率也会加倍；如果OH⁻的浓度加倍，反应速率同样会加倍。当CH3Br和OH⁻的浓度同时加倍时，反应速率会增加四倍。

$$(CH_3)_3CBr + H_2O \longrightarrow (CH_3)_3COH + HBr$$

> 

Reaction Rate =  $k \times [(CH_3)_3Br]$  first-order reaction

> 反应速率 = 一级反应

*Figure 7.1c Reaction 2: first-order reaction*

> 图7.1c 反应2：一级反应

Reaction 2 is another substitution reaction example. The substrate here is a tertiary bromide and the nucleophile is neutral water molecule. As a first-order reaction, the reaction rate depends **only** on the concentration of substrate (CH3)3CBr and has nothing to do with nucleophile.

> 反应2是另一个取代反应的例子。这里的底物是叔溴化物，亲核试剂是中性的水分子。作为一级反应，反应速率仅取决于底物（CH₃）₃CBr的浓度，而与亲核试剂无关。

The two types of reactions correspond to two types of reaction mechanism:

> 这两种反应类型对应于两种不同的反应机理：

- The second-order reaction goes through the bimolecular reaction mechanism that is called **SN2** reaction, meaning **Substitution, Nucleophilic** and **Bimolecular.**
- The first-order reaction goes through the unimolecular reaction mechanism that is called **SN1** reaction, meaning **Substitution, Nucleophilic** and **Unimolecular.**

> 二级反应通过称为SN2反应的双分子反应机制进行，其中SN2代表取代（Substitution）、亲核（Nucleophilic）和双分子（Bimolecular）。  
一级反应则通过称为SN1反应的单分子反应机制进行，其中SN1代表取代（Substitution）、亲核（Nucleophil,ic）和单分子（Unimolecular）。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_250_Picture_11.jpeg)

| We will have detailed discussions on SN2 and SN1 mechanism respectively, and then compare the similarities and<br>differences in between. |  |  |
|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|--|--|
|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |
|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |
|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |

|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |
|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |
|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |
|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |
|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |
|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |
|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |
|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |
|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |
|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |
|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |
|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |
|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |
|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |
|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |
|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |
|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |
|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |

|                                                                                                                                           |  |  |
