> 我们将分别详细讨论SN2和SN1反应机理，然后比较它们之间的异同。

# 7.2 SN2 Reaction Mechanism, Energy Diagram and Stereochemistry

> 7.2 SN2反应机理、能量图与立体化学

## 1 **SN2 Reaction Mechanism**

> 1 双分子亲核取代反应机理

Let's still take the reaction between CH3Br and OH – as the example for SN2 mechanism.

> 让我们仍然以CH3Br与OH⁻之间的反应为例，来说明SN2机理。

![](_page_252_Figure_3.jpeg)

SN2 mechanism involves two electron pair transfers that occur at the same time, nucleophile attacking (red arrow) and leave group leaving (blue arrow). The nucleophile OH – approaches the electrophilic carbon from the back side, the side that is opposite to the direction that leaving group Br leaves. With the nucleophile OH – getting closer, the Br start to leave as well. The new C—OH bond formation and the old C—Br bond breaking occur *at the same time*. In a very short transient moment, the carbon atom is *partially* connected with *both* OH and Br, that gives a highest energy level state of the whole process called **transition state**. In the transition state of SN2 reaction, there are *five* groups around the carbon and the carbon can be called "pentacoordinated". As the OH – continues to get closer to the carbon, the Br moves further away from it with the bonding electron pair. Eventually, the new bond is completely formed and the old bond is completely broken that gives the product CH3OH.

> SN2反应机理涉及两个电子对的转移，这两个过程同时发生，即亲核试剂的进攻（红色箭头）和离去基团的离去（蓝色箭头）。亲核试剂OH⁻从碳原子的背面接近，也就是与离去基团Br离去方向相反的一侧。随着OH⁻逐渐靠近，Br也开始离去。新的C—OH键的形成与旧的C—Br键的断裂同时发生。在极短的过渡态瞬间，碳原子同时与OH⁻和Br部分连接，这一状态是整个反应过程中能量最高的状态，称为过渡态。在SN2反应的过渡态中，碳原子周围有五个基团，因此碳原子被称为“五配位”。随着OH⁻继续靠近碳原子，Br则带着成键的电子对逐渐远离碳原子。最终，新键完全形成，旧键完全断裂，生成产物CH₃OH。

In the mechanism, the reaction proceeds in a single step that involves both nucleophile and the substrate, so increasing the concentration of either of them makes the possibility of collision increase, that explains the **secondorder** kinetics of **SN2** reaction. With both nucleophile attacking and leaving group leaving happen at the same time, SN2 is also said to be a **concerted** mechanism, concerted means simultaneous.

> 在该反应机理中，反应在一个步骤中完成，涉及亲核试剂和底物同时参与，因此增加亲核试剂或底物的浓度都会使碰撞的可能性增加，这解释了SN2反应呈现二级反应动力学的原因。由于亲核试剂进攻和离去基团离去同时发生，SN2反应也被称为协同机理，协同意味着同时进行。

Notes for drawing SN2 mechanism:

> 绘制SN2反应机理的注意事项：

- The **two** arrows must be shown when drawing the SN2 mechanism. Both have to be shown with the proper direction: nucleophile attack from the direction that is **opposite** to the leaving group leaves, *i.e*., backside attack.
- The transition state is optional (depends on the requirement of the question). However it is important to understand that the reaction process goes through the transition state before producing the products.
- Please pay attention that for the product, the positions of the three hydrogens around carbon are all pushed to the other side, and the overall configuration of the carbon get *inverted*, like an umbrella flipped inside out in a windstorm. It seems does not really matter for product (CH3OH) in this reaction, however it does make a difference if the carbon is a chirality center.

> 在绘制SN2反应机理时，必须同时画出两条箭头。这两条箭头的方向必须正确：亲核试剂从离去基团离开的方向相反一侧进行攻击，即所谓的“背面进攻”。

过渡态可根据题目要求选择是否绘制。然而，重要的是要理解反应过程是经过过渡态后才生成产物的。

请注意，在产物中，碳原子周围三个氢原子的位置都被推到了另一侧，整个碳原子的构型发生了翻转，就像在风暴中伞面被翻转了一样。在本反应中，产物（CH₃OH）的构型似乎并不重要，但如果该碳原子是一个手性中心，则这种构型翻转将产生显著影响。

### 1.1 **Energy Diagram of SN2 Mechanism**

> 1.1 SN2反应机理的能量图

The energy changes for the above reaction can be represented in the energy diagram shown in **Fig. 7.1**. SN2 is a singlestep reaction, so the diagram has only one curve. The products CH3OH and Br – are in lower energy than the reactants CH3Br and OH – , indicates that the overall reaction is **exothermic** and the products are more stable.

> 上述反应的能量变化可以用图7.1所示的能量图表示。SN2反应是一个单步反应，因此该能量图中只有一条曲线。产物CH3OH和Br⁻的能量低于反应物CH3Br和OH⁻，这表明该反应整体为放热反应，产物比反应物更加稳定。

![](_page_253_Figure_5.jpeg)

The top of the curve corresponds to the **transition state**, which is the highest-energy structure involved in the reaction. Transition state always involves partial bonds, partially formed bond and partially broken bond, and therefore is very unstable with no appreciable lifetime. The transition state therefore can **never** been isolated. The structure of the transition states is usually shown in a square bracket with a double-dagger superscript.

> 曲线的顶端对应过渡态，这是反应过程中涉及的最高能量结构。过渡态总是包含部分键，既有部分形成的新键，也有部分断裂的旧键，因此过渡态非常不稳定，几乎没有可观的寿命。因此，过渡态永远无法被分离出来。过渡态的结构通常用带双 dagger 上标（ superscript double dagger ）的方括号表示。

### 1.2 **The Effect of Alkyl Halide Structure on SN2 Reaction Rate**

> 1.2 烷基卤化物结构对SN2反应速率的影响

For the discussions on SN2 mechanism so far, we focused on the reaction of methylbromide CH3Br. Other alkyl halides could undergo SN2 reactions as well. The studies on the reaction rate for SN2 indicate that the structure category of electrophilic carbon in alkyl halide affects the reaction rate dramatically.

> 到目前为止，我们关于SN2反应机理的讨论主要集中在甲基溴（CH3Br）的反应上。其他卤代烷也可以发生SN2反应。关于SN2反应速率的研究表明，卤代烷中亲电碳的结构类型对反应速率有显著影响。

| Type of Alkyl Halide               | Alkyl Halide<br>Structure | Relative Rate |
|------------------------------------|---------------------------|---------------|
| Methyl                             | CH3X                      | 30            |
| Primary (1°)                       | RCH2–X                    | 1             |
| Secondary (2°)                     |                           | 0.03          |
| Tertiary (3°)<br>(no SN2 reaction) |                           | negligible    |

> | 卤代烷类型               | 卤代烷<br>结构         | 相对反应速率 |
|--------------------------|------------------------|--------------|
| 甲基卤代烷               | CH₃X                   | 30           |
| 伯卤代烷（1°）           | RCH₂–X                 | 1            |
| 仲卤代烷（2°）           |                        | 0.03         |
| 叔卤代烷（3°）<br>（无SN2反应） |                        | 可忽略       |

**Table 7.1 Relative Reaction Rate of SN2 for Different Type of Alkyl Halide**

> 表7.1 不同类型卤代烷的SN2反应相对速率

As shown in **Table 7.1**, methyl and primary halides are the substrates with the highest rate, the rate decreases a lot for secondary halides, and the tertiary halides do not undergo SN2 reaction at all because the rate is too low to be practical. The **relative reactivity of alkyl halides towards SN2 reaction** can therefore be summarized as:

> 如表7.1所示，甲基和一级卤代烷的反应速率最高，二级卤代烷的反应速率明显降低，而三级卤代烷则根本不会发生SN2反应，因为其反应速率太低，无法实际应用。因此，烷基卤化物在SN2反应中的相对反应活性可以总结为：

Why the trend is like this? This can be explained by the mechanism of SN2 reaction. Actually this is one of the experiment evidences scientists based on for proposing the mechanism. A key feature in SN2 mechanism is that the *nucleophile attacks from the back side*. When nucleophile approaching to the carbon, it is easiest to getting close to the methyl carbon because the hydrogen atoms connected on carbon are small in size. With the size of the groups connected on the carbon getting larger, it is becoming more difficult to access to the carbon, and such approaching is totally blocked for tertiary carbon with three bulky alkyl groups connected. Therefore, the reactivity difference is essentially caused by the **steric effect. Steric effect** is the effect that based on the steric size or volume of a group. Because of the steric hinderance of bulky groups on the electrophilic carbon, it is less accessible for nucleophile to do back-side attack, so the SN2 reaction rate of secondary (2°) and tertiary (3°) substrates decreases dramatically. Actually the 3° substrates never go with SN2 reaction mechanism because the reaction rate too slow.

> 为什么会出现这样的趋势？这可以用SN2反应机理来解释。实际上，这是科学家提出该机理时所依据的实验证据之一。SN2反应机理的一个关键特征是亲核试剂从碳原子的背面进攻。当亲核试剂接近碳原子时，最容易接近甲基碳原子，因为连接在碳原子上的氢原子体积较小。随着连接在碳原子上的基团体积增大，亲核试剂接近碳原子的难度也随之增加，而对于连接有三个大体积烷基基团的叔碳原子，这种接近甚至完全被阻挡。因此，反应活性的差异本质上是由空间位阻效应引起的。空间位阻效应是指由于基团的空间体积或大小所造成的影响。由于连接在亲电碳原子上的大体积基团产生了空间位阻，亲核试剂难以从背面进攻，因此二级（2°）和三级（3°）底物的SN2反应速率会显著降低。事实上，三级底物根本不会通过SN
反应机理进行反应，因为反应速率太慢。

![](books/Organic-Chemistry/pic/_page_255_Picture_1.jpeg)

### 1.3 **The Stereochemistry of SN2 Reaction**

> 1.3 SN2 反应的立体化学

Another feature of SN2 reaction mechanism is that the overall configuration of the carbon in the product get inverted comparing to that of the reactant, like an umbrella flipped inside out. Such inversion of configuration is called *Walden inversion*. let's see what is the stereochemistry consequence for such inversion.

> SN2反应机理的另一个特征是，产物中碳原子的构型会与反应物相比发生翻转，就像一把伞被倒过来一样。这种构型的翻转被称为瓦尔登翻转（Walden inversion）。让我们来看看这种翻转对立体化学会产生什么样的影响。

OH 
$$CH_3$$
  $H$   $CH_3$   $HO$   $CH_2CH_3$   $CH_2CH_3$  (S)-2-butanol

> OH  
                (S)-2-丁醇

Start with the (**R**)-2-bromobutane, the SN2 reaction produces only one enantiomer of 2-butanol product, and it is predictable that the configuration of the product supposed to be **S** because of the configuration inversion.

> 以(R)-2-溴丁烷为反应物，SN2反应仅生成2-丁醇的一种对映体，由于构型翻转，产物的构型应为S型，这是可以预测的。

**Note: Inversion means the arrangement of the groups get inverted, not necessary means the absolute configuration, R/S, inverted. The product does get inverted R/S configuration comparing to the reactant for lot cases, but not guaranteed. The actual configuration of the product has to be determined accordingly.**

> 注意：构型翻转指的是取代基的排列顺序发生颠倒，不一定意味着绝对构型（R/S）发生翻转。在许多情况下，产物的R/S构型确实会与反应物相反，但并非绝对如此。产物的实际构型需根据具体情况加以确定。

#### 1.3.1 *Exercises 7.1*

> 1.3.1 习题 7.1

Show the product of the following SN2 reaction (CN– is the nucleophile):

> 写出下列 SN2 反应的产物（CN⁻ 是亲核试剂）：

Answers to Practice Questions Chapter 7

> 第七章练习题答案

# 7.3 Other Factors that Affect SN2 Reactions

> 7.3 影响SN2反应的其他因素

#### 0.1.1 **Leaving Group**

> 0.1.1 离去基团

When alkyl halides undergo nucleophilic substitution reactions, halogen is the leaving group. Not only halogens can be leaving group, other appropriate groups could be leaving groups as well. Generally speaking, nucleophilic substitution reaction requires good leaving group. How to determine whether a leaving group is good or not then? When leaving group departs, it takes the electron pair from the broken bondtogether it. So the good leaving group should be the one that can accommodate the electron pair very well with it, or it can be said the good leaving group should be stable with the pair of electrons.

> 当烷基卤化物发生亲核取代反应时，卤素是离去基团。不仅卤素可以作为离去基团，其他适当的基团也可以作为离去基团。一般来说，亲核取代反应需要良好的离去基团。那么如何判断一个离去基团是否优良呢？当离去基团离去时，它会连同断裂键中的电子对一起离去。因此，优良的离去基团应是能够很好地容纳该电子对的基团，或者说，优良的离去基团应是与电子对共存时比较稳定的基团。

The stability of a group with electron pair is related to the basicity of the group, since basicity means the ability of the species to share its electron pair. As a result, strong base has the high reactivity to share the electron pair, so it is not stable, and cannot be good leaving group. On the other side, weak base with low tendency to share the electron pair, is more stable base and therefore is good leaving group. So the general trend is:

> 具有孤对电子的基团的稳定性与其碱性有关，因为碱性意味着该物种共享其孤对电子的能力。因此，强碱由于具有较高的共享孤对电子的反应活性，因而不够稳定，也不适合作为良好的离去基团。另一方面，弱碱由于共享孤对电子的倾向较低，因此更加稳定，适合作为良好的离去基团。因此，总体趋势是：

#### 0.1.2 *The weaker the basicity of a group, the better leaving group it is.*

> 0.1.2 群体的碱性越弱，其离去能力越强。

Our knowledge in acid-base topic will be very helpful here to compare the strength between different leaving groups. For alkyl halides, the relative reactivities as leaving group is:

> 在讨论离去基团的离去能力时，我们关于酸碱反应的知识将非常有帮助。对于烷基卤化物，作为离去基团的相对反应性为：

> (best leaving group) **I – > Br – > Cl– > F–** (weakest leaving group)

> （最好的离去基团）I⁻ > Br⁻ > Cl⁻ > F⁻（最弱的离去基团）

This order matches with the relative basicity of halide anions, I– is the weakest base and also the best leaving group. Beside halides, other groups can be leaving groups as well. In acid-base chapter we have learned about some examples of strong organic acids, for example, tosylic acid, TsOH, etc. Since the conjugate base of strong acid is very weak bases, the conjugate bases of those acids are good choice of leaving group as well. Examples include (the leaving group is highlighted in blue color):

> 这一顺序与卤素阴离子的相对碱性强弱相一致，I⁻ 是最弱的碱，同时也是最好的离去基团。除了卤素外，其他基团也可以作为离去基团。在酸碱章节中，我们已经学习了一些强有机酸的例子，例如对甲苯磺酸（TsOH）等。由于强酸的共轭碱是非常弱的碱，因此这些酸的共轭碱也是良好的离去基团。例如（离去基团用蓝色突出显示）：

$$CH_3$$

> 

*Figure 7.3a Examples of good leaving groups: Conjugate bases of strong organic acids*

> 图7.3a 好的离去基团示例：强有机酸的共轭碱

Strong bases such as OH – , RO– , NH2 – , R– are therefore very poor leaving groups and **cannot** go with nucleophilic substitution reactions. For OH – or RO– however, upon protonation they can be converted to neutral H2O or ROH molecules, that are good leaving groups suitable to substitution. This topic will be covered in **section 7.6.**

> 像 OH⁻、RO⁻、NH2⁻、R⁻ 这样的强碱因此是非常差的离去基团，无法参与亲核取代反应。然而，对于 OH⁻ 或 RO⁻ 来说，通过质子化可以转化为中性的 H2O 或 ROH 分子，这些是良好的离去基团，适合进行取代反应。本部分内容将在第 7.6 节中详细讲解。

**Note: with the scope of leaving group expanded, the substitution reaction not only limited to alkyl halide. Any compounds** *with a good leaving group* **can undergo nucleophilic substitution.**

> 注意：随着离去基团范围的扩大，取代反应不仅限于卤代烷。任何含有良好离去基团的化合物都可以发生亲核取代反应。

### 0.2 **Nucleophile**

> 0.2 核亲核试剂

For SN2 reaction, nucleophile is one of the rate-determining factors, therefore strong nucleophile helps to speed up SN2 reactions.

> 对于SN2反应，亲核试剂是决定反应速率的关键因素之一，因此强亲核试剂有助于加快SN2反应的进行。

The relative strength of a nucleophile is called nucleophilicity. Nucleophilicity of a nucleophile is measured in terms of the relative rate of its SN2 reaction with the same substrate. Generally speaking, the nucleophilicity trend depends on several structural features of the nucleophile.

> 亲核试剂的相对强度称为亲核性。亲核性是通过亲核试剂与相同底物发生SN2反应的相对速率来衡量的。一般来说，亲核性的趋势取决于亲核试剂的几个结构特征。

- A nucleophile with negative charge is always stronger than the corresponding neutral one. For example: OH – > H2O; RO– > ROH.
- Nucleophilicity decrease across a period. For example: NH3 > H2O; RNH2 > ROH
- Nucleophilicity increase across a group. For example:

> 带负电荷的亲核试剂总是比相应的中性试剂更强。例如：OH⁻ > H₂O；RO⁻ > ROH。  
在同一周期中，亲核性随着原子序数的增加而降低。例如：NH₃ > H₂O；RNH₂ > ROH。  
在同一族中，亲核性随着原子序数的增加而增强。例如：

$$RSH > ROH;$$
  $RS^- > RO^-;$   $I^- > Br^- > Cl^- > F^-$  (protic solvent)

> （质子性溶剂）

• Smaller group is better nucleophile than bulky group.

> • 体积较小的基团比体积较大的基团更具亲核性。

For example, 
$$t$$
-BuO<sup>-</sup>  $\begin{pmatrix} cH_3 & C & C & C & C \\ CH_3 & C & C & C & C \\ CH_3 & C & C & C & C \\ CH_3 & C & C & C & C \\ CH_3 & C & C & C & C \\ CH_3 & C & C & C & C & C \\ CH_3 & C & C & C > 例如，
-BuO⁻

To make it more convenient for studying purpose, the commonly applied strong and weak nucleophiles are listed here: **Strong (good) nucleophile:** OH – , RO– (small alkoxide), RS– (thiolate), N3 – (azide), CN– (cyanide), Cl– , Br – , I– (halide), RCO2 – (carboxylate), RNH2 (amine)

> 为了便于学习，这里列出了一些常用的强（良好）亲核试剂：强（良好）亲核试剂：OH⁻、RO⁻（小的烷氧基负离子）、RS⁻（硫醇盐）、N₃⁻（叠氮化物）、CN⁻（氰化物）、Cl⁻、Br⁻、I⁻（卤化物）、RCO₂⁻（羧酸根）、RNH₂（胺）

**Weak (poor) nucleophile**: ROH, H2O, *t*-BuO –

> 弱（较差）亲核试剂：ROH、H₂O、t-BuO

With the structure of nucleophiles being so diverse, SN2 reaction can be used to synthesize the compounds with a variety of functional groups, as shown here.

> 由于亲核试剂的结构种类繁多，SN2反应可用于合成具有多种官能团的化合物，如图所示。

![](_page_259_Figure_0.jpeg)

*Figure 7.3b Functional group interconversions via SN2 reactions*

> 图7.3b 通过SN2反应实现官能团的相互转化

+    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O    +    O Answers to Practice Questions Chapter 7

> 第七章练习题答案

# 7.4 SN1 Reaction Mechanism, Energy Diagram and Stereochemistry

> 7.4 SN1反应机理、能量图与立体化学

### 0.1 **SN1 Reaction Mechanism**

> 0.1 SN1反应机理

The reaction between *tert*-butylbromide and water proceeds via the SN1 mechanism. Unlike SN2 that is a single-step reaction, SN1 reaction involves multiple steps. Reaction: (CH3)3CBr + H2O → (CH3)3COH + HBr

> 叔丁基溴与水的反应通过SN1机理进行。与SN2反应不同，SN2是单步反应，而SN1反应则涉及多个步骤。反应式：(CH₃)₃CBr + H₂O → (CH₃)₃COH + HBr

$$\begin{array}{cccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccc$$

> 

In **step 1**, C—Br bond breaks and Br departs with the bonding electron pair to produce a tertiary carbocation and bromide anion Br – . This step only involves a highly endothermic bond-breaking process, and this is the slowest step in the whole mechanism. In multiple-step mechanism, the overall reaction rate is determined by the slowest step, such step is therefore called the **rate-determining step**. In SN1 reaction, step 1 is the slowest step and therefore the ratedetermining step. The rate-determining step only involves the alkyl halide substrate, that is why the overall rate law is in first order, because nucleophile does not participate in the rate-determining step.

> 在第一步中，C—Br 键断裂，Br- 离去时携带一对共用电子对，生成一个叔碳正离子和溴离子 Br⁻。这一步仅涉及一个高度吸热的键断裂过程，是整个反应机理中最慢的一步。在多步反应机理中，整个反应的速率由最慢的那一步决定，因此这一步被称为速率决定步骤。在 SN1 反应中，第一步是最慢的步骤，因此也是速率决定步骤。速率决定步骤仅涉及卤代烷底物，这就是整个反应速率定律为一级反应的原因，因为亲核试剂并未参与速率决定步骤。

The product of step 1, carbocation, will be the reactant of next step and is called the **intermediate** for SN1 reaction. Intermediate is the unstable, highly-reactive species with very short lifetime. The carbocation intermediate is in trigonal planar shape, with the *empty* 2p orbital particular to the plane. The central carbon is sp<sup>2</sup> hybridized and has the incomplete octet, so carbocation is the highly reactive intermediate, that is also the electrophile.

> 第一步的产物，碳正离子，将成为下一步的反应物，被称为SN1反应的中间体。中间体是一种不稳定的、高反应活性的物种，具有非常短的寿命。碳正离子中间体呈三角平面结构，其空的2p轨道位于平面内。中心碳原子为sp²杂化，具有不完整的八电子结构，因此碳正离子是一种高反应活性的中间体，同时也是亲电试剂。

**Step 2** is the nucleophilic attack step, that the nucleophile H2O use its lone pair to react with the carbocation intermediate, and produces the protonated *t*-butyl alcohol (oxonium ion). Because of the planar shape of carbocation intermediate, there is same possibility for the nucleophile to attack from either side of the plane, so possible products are generated with the same amounts. For this reaction, attacking from either side gives the same product (both are still shown for the purpose to illustrate the concept); however it gives different stereoisomers if the electrophilic carbon is the chirality center.

> 第二步是亲核攻击步骤，亲核试剂 H₂O 利用其孤对电子与碳正离子中间体反应，生成质子化的叔丁醇（氧化onium 离子）。由于碳正离子中间体具有平面结构，亲核试剂可以从平面的两侧进行攻击，因此生成的产物具有相同的概率。对于该反应，从两侧进行攻击所得的产物相同（为便于说明概念，两种情况均被展示）；但如果电荷中心碳原子是手性中心，则会生成不同的立体异构体。

In **step 3**, a water molecule acting as a Bronsted base to accept the proton from the oxonium ion, and the final neutral product *t*-butyl alcohol is produced. This deprotonation step is very fast, and sometimes can be combined with step 2 together as one step (i.e. step 3 may not be regarded as an individual step).

> 在第三步中，一个水分子作为布朗斯特碱，接受氧化onium离子中的质子，最终生成中性的叔丁醇。这一脱质子化步骤非常迅速，有时可以与第二步合并为一个步骤（即第三步可能不被视为一个独立的步骤）。

### 0.2 **Energy diagram of SN1 mechanism**

> 0.2 SN1反应机理的能量图

Because SN1 is a multiple-step reaction, so the diagram has multiple curves, with each step can be represented by one curve. Out of the three steps, the activation energy for step 1 is the highest, therefore step 1 is the slowest step, that is the rate-determining step.

> 由于SN1反应是多步反应，因此图中会出现多条曲线，每一步都可以用一条曲线来表示。在三个步骤中，第一步的活化能最高，因此第一步是反应中最慢的步骤，也就是决速步骤。

![](_page_263_Figure_0.jpeg)

*Figure 7.4a Energy diagram for SN1 reaction between (CH3)3CBr and H2O*

> 图7.4a (CH3)3CBr与H2O发生SN1反应的能量图

The connection between the first two curves represent the **carbocation intermediate**. Generally, intermediate is the product of one step of a reaction and the reactant for the next step. Intermediate is at a relatively lower energy level comparing to transition state (which is at the peak of a curve), but intermediate is also highly reactive and unstable.

> 前两条曲线之间的连接部分代表的是碳正离子中间体。通常，中间体是反应中某一步的产物，同时也是下一步反应的反应物。与过渡态（位于曲线峰值处）相比，中间体的能量水平相对较低，但中间体通常也具有高度的反应活性和不稳定性。

### 0.3 **The Effect of Substrate Structure on SN1 Reaction Rate**

> 0.3 底物结构对SN1反应速率的影响

Different substrates have different reaction rates towards SN1 reaction, and the **relative reactivity of substrates towards SN1 reaction** can be summarized as:

> 不同的底物在SN1反应中表现出不同的反应速率，底物在SN1反应中的相对反应活性可总结为：

|                                                    | too unreactive              |
|----------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------|
| tertiary 3° > secondary 2° > primary 1° and methyl | to undergo S <sub>N</sub> 1 |
|                                                    | reaction                    |

> |                                                    | 太不活泼                     |
|----------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------|
| 三级 3° > 二级 2° > 一级 1° 和甲基               | 难以发生 S <sub>N</sub> 1 反应 |

*Figure 7.4b Relative reactivity of substrates towards SN1 reaction*

> 图7.4b 亲核取代反应（SN1反应）中底物的相对反应活性

Comparing this trend to that for SN2 reaction, you probably realize that they are just opposite. Tertiary substrate is most reactive towards SN1, but it does not undergo SN2 at all; primary and methyl substrate are unreactive for SN1, but they are the best substrates for SN2. This comparison is very important and useful for us to choose the proper reaction condition for different substrate as we will see in next section. For now, we will need to understand the reasoning of the trend for SN1.

> 将这一趋势与SN2反应的趋势进行比较，你可能会意识到它们正好相反。三级底物对SN1反应最敏感，但根本不发生SN2反应；而一级和甲基底物对SN1反应不敏感，却是SN2反应的最佳底物。这种比较对我们选择不同底物的合适反应条件非常重要，这将在下一节中看到。目前，我们需要理解SN1反应趋势背后的原因。

This is because of the stability of carbocation intermediate. The mechanism shows that a carbocation is formed in the rate-determining step, so the more stable the carbocation, the more easily it is formed, the more it facilitates the rate-determining step and speed up the whole reaction. Therefore the more stable the carbocation intermediate is, the faster the rate of a SN1 reaction.

> 这是因为碳正离子中间体的稳定性。反应机理表明，在决速步骤中会形成碳正离子，因此碳正离子越稳定，越容易形成，从而越有利于决速步骤，加快整个反应的进行。因此，碳正离子中间体越稳定，SN1反应的反应速率就越快。

The relative stability of carbocation is given below, that the tertiary carbocations are the most stable and methyl carbocation is the least stable.

> 下列内容说明碳正离子的相对稳定性：叔碳正离子最稳定，甲基碳正离子最不稳定。

![](_page_264_Figure_0.jpeg)

*Figure 7.4c The relative stability of carbocations*

> 图7.4c 烷基碳正离子的相对稳定性

The relative stability of carbocations can be explained by the hyperconjugation effect. **Hyperconjugation** is the partial orbital overlap between filled bonding orbital to an adjacent unfilled (or half-filled) orbital. Carbocation is the electrondeficient species that has the incomplete octet and empty 2p orbital. If there is an alkyl group connected with carbocation, then there are C-C or C-H sigma bonds beside the carbocation carbon, so the filled orbitals of sigma bonds will be able to partially overlap with the empty 2p orbital, therefore sharing the electron density to carbocation and to get the carbocation stabilized. The more R group involved, the stronger hyperconjugation effect is. So tertiary (3°) carbocation is the most stable one. While there is no any R group in methyl carbocation, CH3 + , it is least stable.

> 碳正离子的相对稳定性可以用超共轭效应来解释。超共轭效应是指填充的成键轨道与相邻的未填充（或半填充）轨道之间的部分轨道重叠。碳正离子是一种缺电子物种，具有不完整的八隅体和空的2p轨道。如果碳正离子连接有烷基基团，则碳正离子碳原子旁边会有C-C或C-H的σ键。这些σ键的填充轨道可以部分与碳正离子的空2p轨道重叠，从而将电子密度部分转移给碳正离子，使碳正离子得到稳定。参与超共轭效应的R基团越多，超共轭效应就越强。因此，三级（3°）碳正离子是最稳定的。而甲基碳正离子CH₃⁺由于没有R基团参与，是最不稳定的。

![](_page_264_Figure_4.jpeg)

*Figure 7.4d Hyperconjudation effect*

> 图7.4d 超共轭效应

### 0.4 **Stereochemistry of SN1 mechanism**

> 0.4 SN1反应机理的立体化学

The stereochemistry feature of the SN1 reaction is very different to that of SN2, and of course can be explained well with the SN1 mechanism.

> SN1反应的立体化学特征与SN2反应有很大不同，当然可以用SN1机理解释得很好。

$$\begin{array}{c} \text{CH}_2\text{CH}_2\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_2\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_2\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_2\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_2\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_2\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_2\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_2\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_2\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_2\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_2\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_2\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_2\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_2\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_2\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_2\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_2\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_2\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_2\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_2\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_2\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_2\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_2\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_2\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\ \\ \text{CH}_3\text{CH}_3\\$$

> 

Starting with (S)-3-bromo-3-methylhexane reactant, the SN1 reaction produces a 50:50 mixture of both R and S enantiomers of 3-methyl-3-hexanol, that is the **racemic mixture** product. This is because the carbocation formed in the first step of an SN1 reaction has the trigonal planar shape, when it react with nucleophile, it may react from either the front side or the back side, and each side gives one enantiomer. There is equal possibility for reaction to occur from either side, so the two enantiomers are formed with the same amount, and the product is a racemic mixture.

> 以(S)-3-溴-3-甲基己烷为反应物，SN1反应生成3-甲基-3-己醇的R和S两种对映体各占50%的混合物，即外消旋混合物。这是因为SN1反应的第一步生成的碳正离子具有三角平面结构，在与亲核试剂反应时，亲核试剂可以从正面或背面进攻碳正离子，每种进攻方式都会生成一种对映体。由于从正反两面进攻的可能性相等，因此两种对映体生成的量相同，最终产物为外消旋混合物。

A reaction that coverts an optically active compound into a racemic form is said to proceed with **racemization**. For SN1 reaction that start with (an optical active)one enantiomer as the reactant, and the chirality center is also the electrophilic carbon (i.e. the reaction occurs on the chirality center), it proceeds with racemization as shown above.

> 将一种光学活性化合物转化为外消旋体的反应被称为发生外消旋化。对于以（光学活性的）一种对映体作为反应物的SN1反应，且手性中心同时也是亲电碳原子（即反应发生在手性中心），则会发生如上所述的外消旋化。

#### 0.4.1 *Exercises 7.3*

> 0.4.1 习题 7.3

Show the detailed mechanism for above reaction of (S)-3-bromo-3-methylhexane and water.

> 展示(S)-3-溴-3-甲基己烷与水反应的详细反应机理。

#### 0.4.2 Answers to Practice Questions Chapter 7

> 0.4.2 第7章练习题答案

Please note that if the chirality center of the reactant is not the reaction center, or if there are more than one chirality center in the reactant, the SN1 reaction does not produce the racemic mixture as example below.

> 请注意，如果反应物的旋构中心并非反应中心，或者反应物中含有多个旋构中心，则SN1反应不会像下面例子那样生成外消旋混合物。

> 示例

Show product(s) of the following SN1 reaction:

> 写出下列 SN1 反应的产物：

**Solution:**

> 解法：

### 0.1 **Leaving Group Effect on SN1**

> 0.1 取代基效应对SN1反应的影响

Same as for SN2 reaction, a good leaving group is also required for SN1 mechanism, and all the discussions we had before in **section 7.3** apply.

> 与SN2反应相同，SN1机制也需要一个良好的离去基团，且我们之前在第7.3节中所讨论的所有内容同样适用。

#### 0.1.1 **Nucleophile**

> 0.1.1 核亲核试剂

Unlike a SN2 reaction, the rate-determining step of SN1 reaction does not include nucleophile, so theoretically the strength of nucleophile has no effect on SN1 reaction. However, a strong nucleophile has high tendency to go with SN2 reaction instead of SN1, so a weaker nucleophile is a better choice for SN1. For the examples we had so far, H2O is the nucleophile.

> 与SN2反应不同，SN1反应的决速步骤不包含亲核试剂，因此从理论上讲，亲核试剂的强弱对SN1反应没有影响。然而，强亲核试剂更倾向于进行SN2反应而不是SN1反应，因此在SN1反应中，选择较弱的亲核试剂更为合适。目前为止我们所举的例子中，水（H₂O）是亲核试剂。

In practice, neutral substances such as H2O, ROH, RCOOH are usually used as nucleophiles in SN1 reaction. When these substances are applied in the reaction, they serve for another function as solvents. So they are used as *both* nucleophiles and solvents for SN1 reaction, and such reaction is also called the solvolysis reaction. **Solvolysis reaction** is a nucleophilic substitution in which the nucleophile is a molecule of solvent as well. The term **solvolysis** comes from: *solvent*+*lysis*, that means cleavage by the solvent. A SN1 reaction is usually a **solvolysis** reaction.

> 在实际操作中，像 H₂O、ROH、RCOOH 这样的中性物质通常被用作 SN1 反应中的亲核试剂。当这些物质被用于反应中时，它们还同时充当溶剂，因此在 SN1 反应中，它们既作为亲核试剂又作为溶剂。这种反应也被称为溶溶反应（solvolysis reaction）。溶溶反应是一种亲核取代反应，其中亲核试剂本身就是溶剂分子。术语“溶溶”（solvolysis）来源于“solvent + lysis”，意为“由溶剂引起的裂解”。通常情况下，SN1 反应就是一种溶溶反应。

*Examples*

> 示例

Show the structures of the products for the following solvolysis reaction.

> 写出下列溶剂解反应产物的结构。

> 0.1.2 解法：

# 7.5 SN1 vs SN2

> 7.5 SN1 与 SN2 的比较

### 0.1 **7.5.1 Comparison Between SN1 and SN2 Reactions**

> 0.1 7.5.1 SN1与SN2反应的比较

Till now, we have finished the basic concepts about SN1 and SN2 reactions. You probably already noticed that the two type of reactions have some similarities, also quite different though. It will be very helpful to put them together for comparison. To help you get in-depth understanding of the two types of mechanism, it is highly recommended that you have a summary *in your own way*. The following comparison is provided here for your reference.

> 到目前为止，我们已经学习了关于SN1和SN2反应的基本概念。你可能已经注意到，这两种反应类型既有相似之处，也存在很大差异。将它们进行对比会非常有帮助。为了帮助你更深入地理解这两种反应机理，建议你用自己的方式做一个总结。以下的对比内容供你参考。

![](_page_268_Figure_3.jpeg)

### 0.2 **7.5.2 Solvent Effect on Sn1 and SN2 Reactions**

> 0.2 7.5.2 溶剂对SN1和SN2反应的影响

Other than the factors we have talked about so far, solvent is another key factor that affect nucleophilic substitution reactions. Proper solvent is required to facilitate a certain mechanism. For some cases, picking up the appropriate solvent is the effective way to control which pathway the reaction proceed.

> 除了我们之前讨论的因素之外，溶剂也是影响亲核取代反应的另一个关键因素。选择适当的溶剂有助于促进某一特定反应机理。在某些情况下，选择合适的溶剂是控制反应按特定路径进行的有效方法。

To understand the solvent effect, we first of all need to have more detailed discussions about solvents, then learn how to choose good solvent for a specific reaction.

> 为了理解溶剂效应，我们首先需要更详细地讨论溶剂，然后学习如何为特定的反应选择合适的溶剂。

Solvents can be divided into **three** major categories based on the structures and polarities, that is: non-polar, polar protic and polar aprotic solvents.

> 根据溶剂的结构和极性，可将其分为三大类，即：非极性溶剂、极性质子溶剂和极性非质子溶剂。

![](_page_269_Figure_0.jpeg)

**Non-polar** solvents are non-polar compounds. (hexane, benzene, toluene, etc.)

> 非极性溶剂是非极性化合物。（如己烷、苯、甲苯等）

**Polar protic** solvents are the compounds containing OH or NH group that is able to form hydrogen bonds. Polar protic solvents are highly polar because of the OH or NH group.

> 极性质子溶剂是指能够形成氢键的含有羟基（OH）或氨基（NH）的化合物。由于含有羟基或氨基，极性质子溶剂具有很强的极性。

**Polar aprotic solvents** is a group solvents with medium range of polarity. They are polar because of polar bonds like C=O or S=O, but the polarity is not as high as OH or NH group. Typical examples of polar aprotic solvents include acetone, DMSO, DMF, THF, CH2Cl2.

> 极性非质子溶剂是一类具有中等极性的溶剂。它们的极性来源于极性键，如C=O或S=O，但其极性强度不如OH或NH基团。常见的极性非质子溶剂包括丙酮、二甲亚砜（DMSO）、N,N-二甲基甲酰胺（DMF）、四氢呋喃（THF）和二氯甲烷（CH₂Cl₂）。

$$\begin{array}{c|ccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccc$$

> 

The general guideline for solvents regarding nucleophilic substitution reaction is:

> 关于亲核取代反应的溶剂一般指导原则是：

- SN1 reactions are favored by polar protic solvents (H2O, ROH etc), and usually are solvolysis reactions.
- SN2 reactions are favored by polar aprotic solvents (acetone, DMSO, DMF etc).

> SN1 反应通常在极性质子溶剂（如 H₂O、ROH 等）中进行，通常属于溶剂解反应。  
SN2 反应则更倾向于在极性非质子溶剂（如丙酮、DMSO、DMF 等）中进行。

### 0.3 **Polar Protic Solvents Favor SN1 Reactions**

> 0.3 极性质子溶剂 favor SN1 反应

In SN1 reaction, the leaving group leaves and carbocation formed in the first step, that is also the rate-determining step. The polar solvent, such as water, MeOH, is able to form hydrogen bonding with the leaving group in the transition state of the first step, therefore lowering the energy of the transition state that leads to the carbocation, and speed up the rate-determining step. As a result, polar protic solvents facilitate SN1 reactions. It is very common that the polar protic solvents serve as nucleophiles as well for SN1 reactions, so usually SN1 reactions are solvolysis reactions as we learned earlier.

> 在SN1反应中，离去基团首先离开，形成碳正离子，这一步也是整个反应的决速步骤。极性溶剂（如水、甲醇）能够在第一步过渡态中与离去基团形成氢键，从而降低形成碳正离子的过渡态能量，加快决速步骤。因此，极性质子溶剂有利于SN1反应的进行。极性质子溶剂在SN1反应中常常也充当亲核试剂，因此我们之前所学的SN1反应通常也被称为溶剂解反应。

$$\begin{array}{c} & & & & & & & & & & & & & & & & & & &$$

> 

*Figure 7.5a Protic solvent (ex. H2O) facilitates the formation of carbocation intermediate in SN1 reaction*

> 图7.5a 质子溶剂（例如H₂O）有利于SN1反应中碳正离子中间体的形成

#### 0.3.1 **Polar Aprotic Solvents Favor SN2 Reactions**

> 0.3.1 极性非质子溶剂有利于SN2反应

Strong nucleophiles are required in SN2 reactions, and strong nucleophile are usually negatively charged species, such as OH – , CH3O – , CN– etc. These anions must stay with cations in salt format like NaOH, CH3ONa etc. Since salts are insoluble in non-polar solvent, therefore non-polar solvents are not appropriate choices, and we need polar solvents that can dissolve the salts.

> SN2反应需要强亲核试剂，而通常强亲核试剂是带负电的物种，如OH⁻、CH₃O⁻、CN⁻等。这些阴离子必须以盐的形式与阳离子共存，例如NaOH、CH₃ONa等。由于盐在非极性溶剂中溶解度低，因此非极性溶剂不是合适的选择，我们需要使用能溶解盐的极性溶剂。

The issue for **polar protic** solvent is that the nucleophile anions will be surrounded by a layer of solvent molecules with hydrogen bonds, and this is called the solvation effect. The solvation effect stabilize (or encumber) the nucleophiles and hinder their reactivities in SN2 reaction. Therefore, polar protic solvents are not suitable for SN2 reactions.

> 极性质子溶剂的问题在于，亲核试剂的阴离子会被一层通过氢键结合的溶剂分子所包围，这种现象称为溶剂化效应。溶剂化效应会稳定（或阻碍）亲核试剂，从而抑制其在SN2反应中的反应活性。因此，极性质子溶剂不适合用于SN2反应。

*Figure 7.5b Protic solvent does not work for SN2: nucleophile is solvated and encumbered by protic solvent*

> 图7.5b 质子溶剂不适合SN2反应：亲核试剂被质子溶剂溶剂化并受到阻碍

As a result the **polar aprotic** solvents, such as acetone, DMSO etc are the best choice of SN2 reactions. They are polar enough to dissolve the salt format nucleophiles, and also not interact as strongly with anions to hinder their reactivities. The nucleophile anions still move around freely in polar aprotic solvent to act as nucleophile.

> 因此，极性非质子溶剂（如丙酮、DMSO等）是SN2反应的最佳选择。这类溶剂极性足够强，可以溶解盐形式的亲核试剂，同时又不会与阴离子发生强烈的相互作用，从而不会阻碍其反应活性。在极性非质子溶剂中，亲核试剂阴离子仍能自由地运动并发挥亲核作用。

The reaction rate for a SN2 reaction in different solvents are provided in the table below, and the polar aprotic solvent DMF proved to be the best choice that speed up the reaction significantly.

> 不同溶剂中SN2反应的反应速率见下表，极性非质子溶剂DMF被证明是最佳选择，能显著加快反应速率。

reaction: 
$$CH_3I + CI^- \rightarrow CH_3CI + I^-$$

> 反应：

solvent relative rate

> 溶剂相对反应速率

$$CH_3OH$$

> 

#### 0.3.2 **7.5.3 The Choice of Reaction Pathway: SN1 or SN2?**

> 0.3.2 7.5.3 反应路径的选择：SN1 还是 SN2？

With all the knowledge about SN1, SN2 reactions and reaction conditions, we should be able to determine that whether a given reaction go with SN1 or SN2 pathway, or design a proper reaction that will produce the desired product(s). The reaction pathway predominantlydepends on the nature of the substrates (primary, secondary or tertiary), and the choice of proper reaction condition serve as a way to facilitate the process.

> 在掌握了所有关于SN1和SN2反应及其反应条件的知识后，我们应能够判断某一反应是通过SN1途径还是SN2途径进行，或者设计出合适的反应条件以得到所需的产物。反应途径主要取决于底物的性质（伯、仲或叔），而选择适当的反应条件则是促进反应进行的一种方式。

- Primary and methyl substrates undergo SN2 reaction predominantly.
- Tertiary substrates go with SN1 process.
- The reaction of secondary substrates mainly rely on the conditions applied. The condition include nucleophile, solvent, etc. See examples for more detailed discussions.

> 一级和甲基底物主要通过SN2反应进行反应。  
三级底物则主要通过SN1过程进行反应。  
二级底物的反应主要取决于所施加的条件，例如亲核试剂、溶剂等。具体细节请参见示例。

Show the product(s) of the following reactions:

> 写出下列反应的产物：

- 1. (S)-2-iodobutane + CH3O –Na + (DMSO →\_
- 2. (S)-2-iodobutane (CH3OH →\_

> (S)-2-碘丁烷 + CH3O⁻ Na+ (DMSO →\
(S)-2-碘丁烷 (CH3OH →\

1. 
$$CH_2CH_3$$
  $DMSO$   $CH_3$   $CH_3O^-Na^+$

Answers to Practice Questions Chapter 7

> 第七章练习题答案

### 0.4 **Some practical tips for working on SN1, SN2 reactions:**

> 0.4 在进行SN1和SN2反应时的一些实用技巧：

- 1. As we understand that strong nucleophiles are required for SN2 reaction, and most of the strong nucleophiles are those with negative charges, for example OH – , OR – . These nucleophiles can be either shown as anions OH – , CH3O – , C2H5O – , *or* in salt format like NaOH, KOH, CH3ONa, C2H5ONa in the reaction conditions. You should understand that it is the same thing. The anion format are easy to identify and also highlight the nature of these species, however since anions must stay together with counter cations as salt, the salt format show the actual chemical formula of the compound used in the reaction.
- 2. Since polar aprotic solvent favors SN2 reactions, so any of above anions or salt can be used together with DMSO, DMF etc, such as OH –/DMSO, CH3ONa/DMF etc .

> 我们了解到，SN2反应需要强亲核试剂，而大多数强亲核试剂都是带负电荷的物种，例如OH⁻、OR⁻。这些亲核试剂在反应条件下可以以阴离子形式存在，如OH⁻、CH₃O⁻、C₂H₅O⁻，也可以以盐的形式存在，如NaOH、KOH、CH₃ONa、C₂H₅ONa。你应该理解，这些其实是同一种物质。阴离子形式更容易识别，并且能突出这些物种的性质；但由于阴离子必须与反离子结合成盐，因此盐的形式则显示了反应中实际使用的化合物的化学式。

由于极性非质子溶剂有利于SN2反应，因此上述阴离子或盐形式的亲核试剂可以与DMSO、DMF等溶剂一起使用，例如OH⁻/DMSO、CH₃ONa/DMF等。

However, sometimes you may see the combination like CH3ONa/CH3OH, that is the combination of CH3O – together with its conjugate acid CH3OH. It may seems contradictory, why a strong nucleophile for SN2 combine with solvent for SN1? The reality is that CH3ONa here still act as strong nucleophile and can be used for SN2 reaction and CH3OH is the solvent for CH3ONa. The reason why CH3OH is used together as solvent is that the CH3ONa can be prepared by treating an alcohol with Na. For example:

> 然而，有时你可能会看到类似 CH₃ONa/CH3OH 的组合，即 CH₃O⁻ 与其共轭酸 CH₃OH 的组合。这似乎有些矛盾，为什么一个适用于 SN2 反应的强亲核试剂要与适用于 SN1 反应的溶剂结合使用？实际上，在这种情况下，CH₃ONa 仍然作为强亲核试剂，可用于 SN2 反应，而 CH₃OH 是 CH₃ONa 的溶剂。之所以将 CH₃OH 作为溶剂使用，是因为 CH₃ONa 可以通过将醇与钠反应制得。例如：

Other alcohol can also react with Na metal (or potassium metal, K) to generate the corresponding RONa.

> 其他醇类也可以与钠金属（或钾金属，K）反应生成相应的RNa。

The reaction between alcohol and NaH can be used as well.

> 醇与NaH的反应也可用于此反应。

2 ROH + 2 Na 
$$\longrightarrow$$
 2 RONa + H<sub>2</sub>  
ROH + NaH  $\longrightarrow$  RONa + H<sub>3</sub>

> 2 ROH + 2 Na → 2 RONa + H₂  
ROH + NaH → RONa + H₂

Since alcohol are in excess in the above reactions, it is also a good solvent for the resulting alkoxide, and RO–/ROH combination is used commonly together. The RO– in this combination can be used as strong nucleophile for SN2 reaction, or base in elimination reaction (**Chapter 8**).

> 由于上述反应中醇类过量，因此它也是生成的烷氧基（alkoxide）的良好溶剂，RO–/ROH 组合常被一起使用。在该组合中，RO– 可以作为 SN2 反应中的强亲核试剂，或作为消除反应中的碱（第8章）。

# 7.6 Extra Topics on Nucleophilic Substitution Reaction

> 7.6 核亲核取代反应的扩展内容

Our discussions so far focus on the fundamental concepts about SN1 and SN2 mechanism, and the reactions we learned about proceed in the regular way. There are some other conditions can be "added" to the basic nucleophilic substitution reactions, to make the reaction look different, or more challenge. However, understanding the basic concepts well is very helpful for us to deal with various situations. The reaction may looks different, but essentially it is still the same.

> 到目前为止，我们的讨论主要集中在SN1和SN2反应机理的基本概念上，以及我们所学的反应通常按照常规方式进行。还有一些其他条件可以“添加”到基本的亲核取代反应中，使反应看起来不同，或者更具挑战性。然而，深入理解这些基本概念对我们应对各种反应情况非常有帮助。反应可能看起来不同，但其本质仍然是相同的。

### 0.1 **7.6.1 SN1 Reaction with Carbocation Rearrangement**

> 0.1 7.6.1 亲核取代反应（SN1反应）与碳正离子重排

Let's take a look at a SN1 reaction.

> 让我们来看一个SN1反应。

$$CH_{3} \xrightarrow{C} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{Br} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3}COOH} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} CH_{3} \xrightarrow{CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3}} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_{3} CH_$$

> 

*Figure 7.6a Reaction with Carbocation Rearrangement*

> 图7.6a 烃正离子重排反应

With the secondary substrate and neutral nucleophile (CH3COOH), this is a SN1 reaction, and solvolysis that CH3COOH acts as both solvent and nucleophile. It is supposed to give the acetate as product, with the acetate replace the Br. However, as shown in the reaction equation that the acetate was **not** introduced on the carbon with leaving group Br, but was connected on the next carbon instead. What is the reason for the unexpected structure of the product?

> 在次级底物和中性亲核试剂（CH₃COOH）存在下，该反应属于SN1反应，CH₃COOH同时作为溶剂和亲核试剂发生溶溶反应。理论上，该反应应生成乙酸根离子，取代Br⁻。然而，如反应式所示，乙酸根并未连接在带有离去基团Br的碳原子上，而是连接在下一个碳原子上。产物出现这种意外结构的原因是什么？

For reactions involve carbocation intermediate, it is a common phenomena that the carbocation *might* rearrange, if such rearrangement leads to a **more stable** carbocation, and this is called **carbocation rearrangement**. Because of the carbocation rearrangement, the product of the above reaction is different than expected. This can be explained with the step-by-step mechanism below.

> 涉及碳正离子中间体的反应中，碳正离子可能发生重排，如果这种重排能够形成更稳定的碳正离子，这种现象称为碳正离子重排。由于碳正离子重排，上述反应的产物与预期不同。这可以通过以下分步机理解释。

*Figure 7.6b Step by step carbocation rearrangement*

> 图7.6b 步骤式碳正离子重排

When Br – leaves, the initial carbocation formed is a *secondary* one. The CH3 group on the next carbon then shift with its bonding electrons to the positively charged carbon, and creating a new more stable *tertiary* **carbocation**. The *tertiary* carbocation then reacts with nucleophile CH3COOH to give the final acetate product. The CH3 group shift with the electron pair, and such move is called 1,2-methanideshift. "1,2-" here refer to the movement occur between two adjacent carbons, not necessarily means C1 and C2.

> 当溴离子（Br⁻）离去时，最初形成的碳正离子是一个二级碳正离子。随后，下一个碳原子上的甲基（CH₃）带着其成键电子迁移至带正电的碳原子上，形成一个新的、更加稳定的三级碳正离子。该三级碳正离子随后与亲核试剂乙酸（CH₃COOH）反应，生成最终的乙酸根产物。甲基带着电子对迁移，这种迁移过程称为1,2-甲基重排。此处的“1,2-”指的是两个相邻碳原子之间的迁移，而不一定特指C₁和C₂。

Other than CH3 group, the H atom in other reactions could shift as well with the electron pair, if such shift can lead to a more stable carbocation. The shift of hydrogen is called 1,2-hydride shift. A couple of notes about the carbocation rearrangement:

> 除了CH₃基团外，其他反应中的H原子也可以与电子对一起移动，如果这种移动能够形成更稳定的碳正离子。氢原子的移动称为1,2-氢迁移。关于碳正离子重排的几点说明：

- Any reaction that involves carbocation intermediate might have rearrangement.
- Not all carbocations rearrange. Carbocations **only** rearrange if they become more stable as a result of the rearrangement.
- The shift is usually 1,2-shift, that means it occur between two adjacent carbons.

> 任何涉及碳正离子中间体的反应都可能发生重排。  
并非所有碳正离子都会发生重排。只有当重排后碳正离子变得更加稳定时，才会发生重排。  
重排通常为1,2-位迁移，即发生在相邻的两个碳原子之间。

#### 0.1.1 **7.6.2 Intramolecular Nucleophilic Substitution Reaction**

> 0.1.1 7.6.2 分子内亲核取代反应

For the reactions we learned before, the substrate with leaving group and the nucleophile are always two separate compounds. It is actually possible for one compound containing both leaving group and nucleophile, and the reaction occurs within the same molecule. Such reaction is called the intramolecular (*intra*, Latin for "within") reaction. Cyclic product is obtained from intramolecular reaction.

> 我们之前学习的反应中，底物带有离去基团，而亲核试剂通常是两种不同的化合物。实际上，也有可能是同一个化合物同时含有离去基团和亲核试剂，反应发生在同一体内。这种反应称为**分子内反应**（“intra”源自拉丁语，意为“内部”）。分子内反应可生成环状产物。

Let's talk about the reaction mechanism that rationalize the structure and stereochemistry of the product for following reaction.

> 让我们讨论以下反应的反应机理，以合理解释产物的结构和立体化学。

$$\begin{array}{c} \text{CH}_2\text{CH}_3\\ \text{HOCH}_2(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2^{\text{IVIIII}}\\ \text{Optical active} \end{array} \qquad \begin{array}{c} \text{CH}_3\text{OH}\\ \text{O}\\ \text{CH}_3 \end{array}$$

> 

*Figure 7.6c Intramolecular Nucleophilic Substitution Reaction*

> 图7.6c 分子内亲核取代反应

*Figure 7.6d Intramolecular Mechanism*

> 图7.6d 分子内机制

In the above reaction, the reactant has two functional groups, bromide (Br) and alcohol (OH). A compound with two functional groups is called **bifunctional molecule**. In this reactant, Br is connected on a tertiary carbon that is a good substrate for SN1 reaction, and OH is a good nucleophile for SN1 as well, so the substitution reaction could occur within the same molecule via SN1 mechanism. So the reaction occurs between one end of the molecule, Br, that acts as the leaving group, and the other part of the molecule, OH, which acts as the nucleophile. As a result, a six-membered cyclic ether is formed as the product.

> 在上述反应中，反应物含有两个官能团，即溴（Br）和羟基（OH）。含有两个官能团的化合物被称为双官能团分子。在该反应物中，溴连接在叔碳原子上，这是SN1反应的良好底物，而羟基也是SN1反应的良好亲核试剂，因此，该反应可能在同一分子内通过SN1机理发生。因此，反应发生在分子的一端——作为离去基团的溴，以及分子的另一部分——作为亲核试剂的羟基之间。最终产物为一个六元环醚。

Since the reaction occurs with SN1 mechanism, the carbocation intermediate is in trigonal planar shape, and the nucleophile can attack from either side of the carbocation to give both enantiomers. Therefore, the product is the racemic mixture that is optical inactive. This is consistent with the stereochemistry feature of SN1 reaction we learned before.

> 由于该反应遵循SN1机理，生成的碳正离子中间体呈三角平面结构，亲核试剂可以从碳正离子的两侧进行攻击，从而生成两种对映异构体。因此，产物为外消旋混合物，无旋光性。这与我们之前所学的SN1反应的立体化学特征是一致的。

Usually if the intramolecular reaction could produce five- or six-membered ring as the product, the reaction will be highly favored because of the special stability of five- or six-membered ring.

> 通常，如果分子内反应能够生成五元或六元环产物，该反应将受到高度青睐，因为五元或六元环具有特殊的稳定性。

#### 0.1.2 **7.6.3 Converting Poor Leaving Group to Good Leaving Group**

> 0.1.2 7.6.3 将较差的离去基团转化为较好的离去基团

In early discussions about leaving groups (**section 7.3**), we have mentioned the importance of a good leaving group for both SN1 and SN2 reactions, that the substitution reaction will not occur is a poor leaving group present. For some situations however, the poor leaving group could be converted to a good leaving group to make the reaction feasible. We will see a couple of strategies for such purpose.

> 在早期关于离去基团（第7.3节）的讨论中，我们已经提到，良好的离去基团对于SN1和SN2反应都非常重要，如果存在不良离去基团，取代反应就不会发生。然而，在某些情况下，不良离去基团可以被转化为良好的离去基团，从而使反应可行。我们将看到几种实现这一目的的策略。

# **By Acid Catalyst H<sup>+</sup>**

> 酸催化剂 H<sup>+</sup>

**Example:** Propose the mechanism to rationalize the reaction.

> 示例：提出反应机理以解释该反应。

$$\begin{array}{c} \text{CH}_2\text{CH}_3 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2\text{WW} \\ \text{CH}_3 \end{array} \\ \begin{array}{c} \text{OH} \\ \text{CH}_3 \end{array} \\ \begin{array}{c} \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3 \end{array} \\ \\ \text{Optical active} \\ \end{array} \\ \begin{array}{c} \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3 \end{array} \\ \begin{array}{c} \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3 \end{array} \\ \begin{array}{c} \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3 \end{array} \\ \begin{array}{c} \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3 \end{array} \\ \begin{array}{c} \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3 \end{array} \\ \begin{array}{c} \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3 \end{array} \\ \begin{array}{c} \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3 \end{array} \\ \begin{array}{c} \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3 \end{array} \\ \begin{array}{c} \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH}_3(\text{CH}_2)_2\text{CH}_2 \\ \text{CH$$

> 

*Figure 7.6e Reaction*

> 图7.6e 反应

$$\begin{array}{cccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccc$$

> 

$$\begin{array}{cccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccc$$

> 

$$\begin{array}{cccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccc$$

> 

*Figure 7.6f Mechanism*

> 图7.6f 机理

The last three steps in the above mechanism are the standardsteps of SN1 mechanism. However, the reaction won't proceed without the first step. In the first step, which is an acid-base reaction, a proton is rapidly transferred to the OH group, and get the alcohol protonated. By protonation, the OH group is converted to H2O, that is a much weaker base therefore a good leaving group. In step 2, water molecule departs with the electron pair and leave behind a carbocation intermediate. The following steps are just SN1, that explains why the product is the racemic mixture. The acid H<sup>+</sup> was regenerated in step 4 and can be reused for further reactions, therefore only catalytical amount of H<sup>+</sup> is necessary to start the process.

> 上述机理中的最后三个步骤属于SN1反应的典型步骤。然而，反应若没有第一步是无法进行的。第一步是一个酸碱反应，质子迅速转移到羟基（OH）上，使醇发生质子化。通过质子化，羟基转化为水（H₂O），即一个更弱的碱，因此是一个优良的离去基团。在第二步中，水分子带着一对电子离去，留下一个碳正离子中间体。接下来的步骤就属于典型的SN1反应，这也解释了为什么产物是外消旋混合物。在第四步中，酸H⁺被再生并可用于进一步反应，因此只需催化量的H⁺即可启动整个反应过程。

### 0.1 **By Sulfonyl Chloride**

> 0.1 磺酰氯法

Another commonly applied method for converting OH group to a better leaving group is by introducing a sulfonate ester. When alcohol reacts with sulfonyl chloride, with the presence of weak base, the sulfonate ester is formed.

> 另一种常用于将羟基（OH）转化为更好的离去基团的方法是引入磺酸酯。当醇与磺酰氯反应并在弱碱存在下进行时，会生成磺酸酯。

*Figure 7.6g Alcohol reacting with tosyl chloride to produce tosylate*

> 图7.6g 醇与对甲苯磺酰氯反应生成对甲苯磺酸酯

As the example shown above, when *p*-toluenesulfonyl chloride (tosyl chloride, TsCl) is used, the resulting ester is ptoluenesulfonate (tosylate, OTs). Does tosyl group look familiar to you? Yes, we learned about with this species in **section 3.2**. As the conjugate base of strong acid *p*-toluenesulfonic acid (TsOH), OTs is the very weak base and therefore an excellent leaving group. Pyridine here acts as the weak base to neutralize the side product HCl and facilitate the reaction to completion. The detailed mechanism for this reaction is not required in this course.

> 如上例所示，当使用对甲基苯磺酰氯（对甲苯磺酰氯，TsCl）时，生成的酯为对甲基苯磺酸酯（对甲苯磺酸酯，OTs）。这个对甲苯磺基（tosyl group）看起来熟悉吗？是的，我们在第3.2节中已经学习过这一类物质。作为强酸对甲基苯磺酸（TsOH）的共轭碱，OTs是一种非常弱的碱，因此是一个优良的离去基团。此处的吡啶起着弱碱的作用，中和副产物HCl，从而促进反应完全进行。本课程中无需详细讨论该反应的机理。

Other than introducing OTs, other commonly applied sulfonyl chlorides include MsCl and TfCl, and the sulfonate ester OMs (mesylate) and OTf (triflate) are formed respectively.

> 除了引入OTs之外，其他常用磺酰氯还包括MsCl和TfCl，分别生成磺酸酯类OMs（甲磺酸酯）和OTf（三氟甲磺酸酯）。

*Figure 7.6h Conversion of Alcohol to Mesylate or Triflate*

> 图7.6h 醇转化为甲磺酸酯或三氟甲磺酸酯

Once the primary alcohol has been converted to OTs (or OMs, OTf), it is then the good substrate for SN2 reaction. With the appropriate nucleophile added in a separate step, for example CH3O – , the SN2 reaction takes place readily to give ether as the final product, as shown below.

> 一旦伯醇被转化为OTs（或OMs、OTf），它就成为SN2反应的良好底物。在另一个步骤中加入适当的亲核试剂（例如CH₃O⁻），SN2反应即可顺利进行，最终得到醚类产物，如下所示。

*Figure 7.6i Step by step synthesis scheme of butyl methyl ether from 1-butanol (with structures of intermediates shown)*

> 图7.6i 从1-丁醇逐步合成丁基甲基醚的合成路线（中间体结构示意图）

The overall synthesis of butyl methyl ether from 1-butanol involves two separate steps: the conversion of OH to OTs, and then the replacement of OTs by CH3O through SN2 reaction. The two steps have to be carried out one after the other, however the whole synthesis scheme can also be shown as below:

> 从1-丁醇合成丁基甲醚的整体过程包括两个独立的步骤：将羟基（OH）转化为甲磺酸酯（OTs），然后通过SN2反应用甲氧基（CH₃O）取代OTs。虽然这两个步骤必须依次进行，但整个合成路线也可以表示如下：

*Figure 7.6j Synthesis scheme of butyl methyl ether from 1-butanol (structures of intermediates are NOT shown)*

> 图7.6j 从1-丁醇合成丁基甲基醚的合成路线（中间体结构未显示）

# Note:

> 注意：

- Figure 7.6j represents the common and conventional way to show the multiple-step synthesis in organic chemistry. The reaction conditions (reagent, catalyst, solvent, temperature etc.) for each step are shown on top and bottom of the equation arrow. Only the structures of starting material and final product(s) are shown, and the structures of the intermediate products for each step are not included.
- The individual steps need to be labelled as 1), 2) etc. for the proper order, they can not be mixed together.

> 图7.6j展示了有机化学中常见的、传统的多步合成反应表示方法。每个反应步骤的反应条件（如试剂、催化剂、溶剂、温度等）显示在反应箭头的上方和下方。仅展示起始原料和最终产物的结构，而每一步中间产物的结构则未包含在内。各个反应步骤需要用1)、2)等进行标注，以表明正确的顺序，不能将它们混合在一起。

# CHAPTER 8 ELIMINATION REACTIONS

> 第8章 消除反应

Nucleophilic substitution reaction is not the only possible reaction for alkyl halides and other substrates with a good leaving group. These substrates could also undergo elimination reaction. In an **elimination** reaction, a small molecule (XY) is removed from two adjacent atoms of the reactant, and a multiple bond is formed in the product:

> 亲核取代反应并不是卤代烷及其他具有良好离去基团的底物唯一可能的反应类型。这些底物还可能发生消除反应。在消除反应中，一个较小的分子（XY）从反应物中相邻的两个原子上被移除，并在产物中形成一个多重键：

*Figure 8.0a General equation of elimination reaction*

> 图8.0a 消除反应的一般方程式

For elimination reaction of alkyl halides, the major product alkene is produced together with the small HX (X is halogen) molecule, which is the side inorganic product. Such reaction with removal of a proton and a halide ion is called **dehydrohalogenation**. Dehydrohalogenation is a commonly applied method for the synthesis of alkene.

> 在卤代烷的消除反应中，主要生成烯烃产物，同时还会生成少量的HX（X为卤素）小分子，这是一种旁路的无机产物。这种通过脱去一个质子和一个卤素离子的反应被称为脱卤化氢反应。脱卤化氢反应是合成烯烃常用的合成方法之一。

$$\begin{array}{c|c}
X & H \\
\hline
C & C
\end{array}$$
base
$$C = C + HX$$

> 基础

*Figure 8.0b Dehydrohalogenation of alkyl halide*

> 图8.0b 烷基卤化物的脱卤化氢反应

In the discussions of elimination reaction, the carbon atom that bonded to the leaving group (halogen for alkyl halide) is called the **alpha (α) carbon** atom, and the carbon atom adjacent to α-carbon is called the **beta (β) carbon** atom. In dehydrohalogenation, it is the hydrogen atom on β-carbon that is eliminated together with halogen, as HX, therefore the reaction is often called as **β-elimination**, or **1,2-elimination**. (The number 1,2- indicate that the atoms being removed are on two adjacent carbons, not necessarily means C1 and C2 atoms.)

> 在讨论消除反应时，与离去基团（如卤代烷中的卤素）相连的碳原子称为α（α）碳原子，与α碳原子相邻的碳原子称为β（β）碳原子。在脱卤化氢反应中，消除的是β碳原子上的氢原子与卤素，以HX的形式离去，因此该反应常被称为β-消除反应，或1,2-消除反应。（数字1,2表示被消除的原子位于两个相邻的碳原子上，并不一定意味着是C1和C2原子。）

![](_page_285_Figure_0.jpeg)

*Figure 8.0c Alpha and Beta carbon*

> 图8.0c α碳和β碳

Beside the substrate, a base is required for elimination reactions, other than the nucleophile for substitution. Similar to substitution reaction, elimination reactions also have different rate laws, and therefore involve different mechanisms. The elimination mechanisms are E1 and E2. You may expect that E1 is the unimolecular reaction with first order rate law, and E2 is the second order bimolecular reaction. That is correct. We will go through the mechanism in details first, then compare between elimination and substitution.

> 除了底物之外，消除反应还需要一种碱，而不仅仅是亲核试剂用于取代反应。与取代反应类似，消除反应也有不同的速率方程，因此涉及不同的反应机理。消除反应的机理包括E1和E2两种。你可能会预期E1是符合一级速率方程的单分子反应，而E、2则是符合二级速率方程的双分子反应。这种理解是正确的。我们将首先详细讲解这两种反应机理，然后再比较消除反应与取代反应。

# 8.1 E2 Reaction

> 8.1 E2 反应

### 0.1 **8.1.1 E2 Mechanism**

> 0.1 8.1.1 E2反应机理

E2 mechanism is the **bimolecular elimination** mechanism, that the reaction rate depends on the concentration of *both* substrate and base. We will take the elimination reaction of 2-bromo-2-methylpropane as an example for discussion.

> E2机制是双分子消除反应机制，即反应速率取决于底物和碱的浓度。我们将以2-溴-2-甲基丙烷的消除反应为例进行讨论。

$$H_3C$$
  $\longrightarrow$   $CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+ CH_3$   $+$

> 

*Figure 8.1a Bimolecular Elimination Reaction*

> 图8.1a 双分子消除反应

It was mentioned earlier that HX is the side product of dehydrohalogenation, why there is no HX (HBr for this reaction) in the reaction equation? It could be understood as that with the presence of excess base (OH – ) in the reaction mixture, HBr reacts with OH – to give H2O and Br – . The following discussion of the mechanism will help you to understand this better.

> 前面已经提到，HX 是脱卤化氢反应的副产物，那么为什么反应方程式中没有出现 HX（本反应中为 HBr）呢？这可以理解为，在反应混合物中存在过量的碱（OH⁻），HBr 与 OH⁻ 反应生成 H₂O 和 Br⁻。接下来对反应机理的讨论将帮助你更好地理解这一点。

E2 mechanism is also a single-step concerted reaction, similar to SN2, with multiple electron pair transfers happen at the same time.

> E2反应机理也是一种单步协同反应，与SN2类似，反应过程中多个电子对的转移同时发生。

![](_page_286_Figure_10.jpeg)

*Figure 8.1b E2 Reaction Mechanism*

> 图8.1b E2反应机理

Base, OH – , uses its electron pair to attack a β-hydrogen on β-carbon, and starts to form a bond; at the same time, the β C-H sigma bond begins to move in to become the π bond of a double bond, and meanwhile Br begins to depart by taking the bonding electrons with it. A transition state is formed in the reaction process with partially breaking and partially forming bonds. At the completion of the reaction, the C=C double bond and H2O molecule are fully formed, with Br – leaves completely.

> 碱（OH⁻）利用其孤对电子攻击β碳上的β-氢原子，开始形成化学键；同时，β碳上的C-Hσ键开始向内移动，形成双键的π键，与此同时，Br⁻开始离去，携带 bonding 电子一起离开。在反应过程中形成一个过渡态，其中部分键断裂，部分键形成。反应完成时，C=C双键和H₂O分子完全形成，Br⁻完全离去。

Since both the substrate (halide) and the base are involved in the single-step mechanism, E2 is the second order reaction.

> 由于底物（卤化物）和碱都参与单步反应机制，E2 反应属于二级反应。

#### 0.1.1 **8.1.2 Regioselectivity of E2 reaction: Zaitsev's Rule** *vs***Hofmann Rule**

> 0.1.1 8.1.2 E2反应的区域选择性：齐特规则（Zaitsev's Rule）与霍夫曼规则（Hofmann Rule）

For the reaction we talked in above section, there are three β-carbons in the substrate 2-bromo-2-methylpropane, however they are all *identical*, so the reaction gives only one single elimination product 2-methylpropene.

> 在上文所讨论的反应中，底物2-溴-2-甲基丙烷中含有三个β-碳原子，但它们彼此相同，因此反应只生成一种消除产物，即2-甲基丙烯。

For other alkyl halides, if there are *different* β-carbons in the substrate, then the elimination reaction may yield more than one products. For example, the dehydrohalogenation of 2-bromo-2-methylbutane can produce two products, 2-methyl-2-butene and 2-methyl-1-butene, by following two different pathways.

> 对于其他卤代烷，如果底物中存在不同的β-碳原子，则消除反应可能会生成多种产物。例如，2-溴-2-甲基丁烷的脱卤化氢反应可以通过两种不同的反应路径生成两种产物：2-甲基-2-丁烯和2-甲基-1-丁烯。

![](_page_287_Figure_5.jpeg)

*Figure 8.1c Regioselectivity of E2 reaction*

> 图8.1c E2反应的区域选择性

Between the two possible products, 2-methyl-2-butene is a trisubstituted alkenes, whereas 2-methyl-1-butene is monosubstituted. For alkenes, the more alkyl groups bonded on the double bond carbons, the more stable the alkene is. Generally, the relative stability of alkenes with different amount of substituents is:

> 在两种可能的产物中，2-甲基-2-丁烯是三取代烯烃，而2-甲基-1-丁烯是单取代烯烃。对于烯烃而言，双键碳原子上连接的烷基越多，烯烃越稳定。一般来说，不同取代数的烯烃的相对稳定性为：

#### 0.1.2 tetrasubstituted > trisubstituted > disubstituted > monosubstituted > ethene

> 0.1.2 四取代 > 三取代 > 二取代 > 单取代 > 乙烯

Therefore, 2-methyl-2-butene is more stable than 2-methyl-1-butene. When a small size base is used for the elimination reaction, such as OH – , CH3O – , EtO– , it turned out that the relative stability of the product is the key factor to determine the major product. As a result, 2-methyl-2-butene is the major product for above reaction.

> 因此，2-甲基-2-丁烯比2-甲基-1-丁烯更稳定。当使用小体积的碱（如OH⁻、CH₃O⁻、EtO⁻）进行消除反应时，产物的相对稳定性是决定主要产物的关键因素。因此，上述反应的主要产物为2-甲基-2-丁烯。

As a general trend, when small base is applied, the elimination products can be predicted by **Zaitsev's rule**, that said the **more substituted alkene is obtained preferably**. So the Zaitsev's rule essentially can be explained by the higher stability of the more substituted alkenes.

> 总体而言，当使用小体积的碱时，消除反应的产物可由齐特尔规则（Zaitsev's rule）预测，即更取代的烯烃是主要产物。因此，齐特尔规则本质上可以由更取代的烯烃具有更高的稳定性来解释。

$$\begin{array}{c|ccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccc$$

> 

*Figure 8.1d Elimination reaction occurs by following Zaitsev's rule with small base applied*

> 图8.1d 消除反应遵循齐梯夫规则，使用小体积的碱进行反应

However, if a bulky base is applied in the elimination, such as *t*-BuOK, the reaction favors the formation of less substituted alkenes.

> 然而，如果在消除反应中使用空间位阻较大的碱，例如叔丁基钾（t-BuOK），则反应更倾向于生成取代基较少的烯烃。

Br

> 溴

$$H_3C$$
  $C$   $C$   $C$   $C$   $C$   $C$   $C$   $C$   $C$

> 

*Figure 8.1e Elimination reaction occurs following Hofmann rule with bulky base applied*

> 图8.1e 消除反应遵循霍夫曼规则，使用大位阻碱时发生

This is mainly because of steric hinderance. With *t*-BuO – attacking the β-hydrogen, it is difficult for this big bulky base to approach the hydrogens from the β-carbon that is bonded with more substituents (as shown in pathway (a) below), while the hydrogen of the methyl group is much easily to be accessed (in pathway (b) instead. When the elimination yields the less substituted alkene, it is said that it follows the **Hofmann rule**.

> 这主要是由于空间位阻效应。当叔丁氧基（t-BuO⁻）进攻β-氢时，这个体积庞大的碱难以接近那些连接更多取代基的β碳原子上的氢原子（如下面路径(a)所示）。而甲基上的氢原子则更容易被接近（如路径(b)所示）。当消除反应生成取代基较少的烯烃时，这种情况则遵循霍夫曼规则（Hofmann rule）。

![](_page_289_Figure_0.jpeg)

*Figure 8.1f Hofmann rule: Bulky base t-BuO- (pathway a), Bulky base t-BuO- is less hindered*

> 图8.1f 洪德曼规则：大位阻碱t-BuO⁻（途径a），大位阻碱t-BuO⁻位阻较小

#### 0.1.3 **8.1.3 Stereochemistry of E2 Reaction**

> 0.1.3 8.1.3 E2反应的立体化学

The E2 mechanism has special stereochemistry requirement to ensure it does proceed. First, the bond connected with the leaving group and the bond connected with the H must be in the same plane, to allow the proper orbital overlapping of the two carbons in the formation of π bond of the alkene product. Second, the leaving group and H must be in antiposition to each other. This is because the anti-position allows the transition state of the reaction is in the more stable staggered conformation, that helps to lower down the energy level of the transition state and speed up the reaction. Overall, E2 reaction proceeds with the leaving group and H are in **anti coplanar** conformation.

> E2历程具有特殊的立体化学要求，以确保反应能够顺利进行。首先，与离去基团相连的键和与氢原子相连的键必须处于同一平面上，以允许两个碳原子之间发生适当的轨道重叠，从而形成烯烃产物的π键。其次，离去基团和氢原子必须处于反式位置。这是因为反式位置使得反应的过渡态处于更稳定的锯齿形构象中，有助于降低过渡态的能量水平，从而加快反应速率。总体而言，E2反应在离去基团和氢原子处于反式共平面构型时进行。

![](_page_289_Picture_4.jpeg)

*Figure 8.1g Anti coplanar conformation of H and LG is required in E2 mechanism*

> 图8.1g E2机理需要H和LG处于反共平面构型

Because of the anti-coplanar conformation requirement for E2 reaction, one stereoisomer will be produced preferably over the other, and this is called **stereoselectivity**. For the following example, the elimination of (2*S*,3*S*)-2-bromo-3-phenylbutane produces the *E* isomer specifically, not the *Z* isomer at all. This is because when H is in anti-position to the leaving group Br, the whole compound is in staggered conformation, and the other groups *retain* their relative position in elimination that leads to the *E* isomer.

> 由于E2反应需要反共面构型，因此一种立体异构体将优先于另一种生成，这种现象称为立体选择性。在以下示例中，(2S,3S)-2-溴-3-苯基丁烷的消除反应将特异性地生成E异构体，而不会生成Z异构体。这是因为当H与离去基团Br处于反位时，整个分子处于锯齿形构型，其他基团在消除过程中保持相对位置，从而生成E异构体。

$$\begin{array}{cccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccc$$

>

> 练习 8.1 显示下列反应的消除产物

Answers to Practice Questions Chapter 8

> 第八章练习题答案

#### 0.1.1 **8.1.4 Bases in E2 Reactions (Brief Summary)**

> 0.1.1 8.1.4 E2 反应中的碱（简要总结）

The most commonly applied bases in E2 reaction are hydroxide OH – , and alkoxide RO– . Specifically, the combination of base with corresponding alcohol are used broadly, such as: CH3ONa/CH3OH, C2H5ONa/C2H5OH.

> E2反应中最常使用的碱是氢氧根离子OH⁻和烷氧基离子RO⁻。具体而言，常用相应的醇与碱配伍，例如：CH₃ONa/CH₃OH、C₂H₅ONa/C₂H₅OH。

Examples of small bases: OH – , CH3O – , C2H5O – , NH2 – Examples of big bulky bases: *t*-BuO – , LDA (lithium diisopropylamide)

> 小碱的例子：OH⁻、CH₃O⁻、C₂H₅O⁻、NH₂⁻  
大体积碱的例子：t-BuO⁻、LDA（锂二异丙基氨基化物）

# 8.2 E1 Reaction

> 8.2 E1 反应

### 0.1 **E1 Mechanism**

> 0.1 E1历程

Similar to substitutions, some elimination reactions show first-order kinetics. These reactions go through E1 mechanism, that is the multiple-step mechanism includes the carbocation intermediate.

> 与取代反应类似，一些消除反应也表现出一级反应动力学。这类反应遵循E1机理，即多步骤机理中包含碳正离子中间体。

When *t*-butyl bromide reacts with ethanol, small amount of elimination products obtained via E1 mechanism.

> 当叔丁基溴与乙醇反应时，通过E1机制可得到少量的消除产物。

$$\begin{array}{c|ccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccc$$

> 

The overall elimination involves two steps:

> 整个消除反应包括两个步骤：

$$\begin{array}{cccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccccc$$

> 

$$CH_3$$
  $CH_3$   $CH_3$   $CH_2$   $CH_3$   $CH_3$   $CH_3$   $CH_3$   $CH_3$

> 

Step 1: The bromide dissociates and forms a tertiary (3°) carbocation. This is a slow bond-breaking step, it is also the rate-determining step for the whole reaction. Since only the bromide substrate involved in the rate-determining step, the reaction rate law is first order. That is the reaction rate only depends on the concentration of (CH3)3Br, and has nothing to do with the concentration of base, ethanol.

> 步骤1：溴离子解离并形成三级（3°）碳正离子。这是一个缓慢的键断裂步骤，同时也是整个反应的速率决定步骤。由于只有溴离子底物参与了速率决定步骤，因此反应速率定律为一级反应。也就是说，反应速率仅取决于（CH₃）₃Br的浓度，而与碱或乙醇的浓度无关。

Step 2: The hydrogen on β-carbon (β-carbon is the one beside the positively charged carbon) is acidic because of the adjacent positive charge. The base, EtOH, reacts with the β-H by removing it, and the C-H bond electron pair moves in to form the C-C π bond.

> 步骤2：β-碳（即正电碳原子旁边的碳原子）上的氢原子具有酸性，这是由于邻近的正电荷所导致。碱（EtOH）通过移除β-氢与之反应，碳-氢键的电子对向碳原子转移，形成碳-碳π键。

The base ethanol in this reaction is a neutral molecule, and therefore a very weak base. Since strong base favors E2, so weak base is a good choice for E1, by discouraging from E2. Ethanol acts as the solvent as well, so E1 reaction is also the **solvolysis** reaction.

> 该反应中的乙醇碱是中性分子，因此是一种非常弱的碱。由于强碱有利于E2反应，因此弱碱是进行E1反应的良好选择，可以抑制E2反应的发生。乙醇同时作为溶剂，因此E1反应也被称为溶剂解反应。

For E1 reaction, if more than one alkenes could be possibly formed as product, the major product will also be the more substituted alkene, like E2, because of the stability of those alkenes.

> 对于E1反应，如果可能生成多种烯烃产物，那么主要产物仍然是取代度更高的烯烃，这与E2反应类似，因为这些烯烃的稳定性更高。

$$H_3C$$
